## Backend/API Architecture Technical Report

### 1. Core API Infrastructure

**Entry Points & Server Setup**
- **`api/index.ts`**: Vercel serverless adapter using `hono/vercel`. Exports `GET/POST/PUT/DELETE/OPTIONS` handlers that delegate to the Hono app from `boot.ts`.
- **`api/boot.ts`**: Main Hono application bootstrap (131 lines). Key behaviors:
  - Custom `serveStatic` implementation using Node `fs` (lines 14-41) — not using Hono's built-in static file middleware.
  - CORS configured with `origin: "*"` (line 44) — **open CORS, no restrictions**.
  - Health check at `/health` (line 47).
  - PDF download route at `/api/pdf/:slug` calling `generatePdf()` (lines 50-61).
  - tRPC mounted at `/api/trpc/*` using `fetchRequestHandler` with empty context (lines 64-72).
  - Node `http.createServer` fallback for local development (lines 87-116) that manually reconstructs `Request` objects from Node `IncomingMessage`.
  - Server starts on `PORT` env var unless `VERCEL` is set (lines 126-131).

**tRPC Configuration**
- **`api/trpc.ts`**: Initializes tRPC with `initTRPC.create()` (no middleware, no context). Exports `router`, `publicProcedure`, and a `stubToRouter()` utility that converts custom stub objects (with `type`, `input`, `resolve`) into real tRPC procedures. **Note**: The `stubToRouter` function is exported but appears unused — all routers in `api/routers/` use the standard `router()` and `publicProcedure` directly.

**Router Aggregation**
- **`api/router.ts`**: Aggregates 9 sub-routers into `appRouter`:
  - `agents`, `prospects`, `scraper`, `analysis`, `apollo`, `booking`, `branding`, `rufusTracker`, `catalogGraph`
- No middleware, no auth guards, no rate limiting at the router level.

---

### 2. Directory Deep Dive

#### `api/routers/` (9 routers)

| Router | Key Observations |
|--------|------------------|
| **`agents.ts`** | Exposes `optimize`, `getState`, `retryStage`. Uses `OptimizationOrchestrator` singleton. Pipeline state stored in **in-memory `Map<string, PipelineState>`** (line 7). `retryStage` is a stub that just returns the state without actually retrying (lines 43-49). |
| **`analysis.ts`** | Core analysis orchestration (266 lines). `runAnalysis()` function instantiates its own `OptimizationOrchestrator` (line 9). Does raw SQL queries directly. Inserts ~30 columns into `listing_analyses` in a single massive `INSERT` (lines 81-141). Updates prospect status to `'analyzed'`. `regenerateCopy` duplicates the listing reconstruction logic. |
| **`prospects.ts`** | CRUD for prospects. `generateSlug()` uses `Math.random().toString(36).substring(2, 10)` (line 8) — **not cryptographically secure**. `recordActivity` logs to DB, fetches prospect details, and triggers webhook. Contains **hardcoded fallback for prospectId === 5** ("Alex Hormozi", "Acme Greens") (lines 167-169, 173-174). |
| **`scraper.ts`** | `trigger` mutation calls `scrapeAmazonListing()` synchronously and inserts into DB. `poll` mutation is a backward-compat stub returning `SUCCEEDED` immediately (lines 56-62). `ingestDirect` allows bypassing the scraper entirely. |
| **`apollo.ts`** | Integrates with Apollo.io for CRM/sequences. Direct DB queries for prospect lookup. Updates `apolloContactId` and `apolloSequenceId` on prospects. |
| **`booking.ts`** | Simple CRUD for bookings. |
| **`branding.ts`** | Reads/writes `brand_settings` table. Uses `any` type for DB row (line 8). |
| **`rufusTracker.ts`** | Runs `simulateRufusSOV()` and persists results to `rufus_queries` + `rufus_query_runs` tables. SOV history query does date parsing by splitting on space (`r.createdAt.split(' ')[0]`) which is fragile for ISO dates. |
| **`catalogGraphRouter.ts`** | Checks `catalog_links` cache first. If missing, generates embedding via `generateEmbedding()`, fetches competitors, builds catalog graph, and caches results. **N+1-like pattern**: calls `generateEmbedding()` for each competitor inside a loop in `buildCatalogGraph()`. |

#### `api/services/` (12 services)

| Service | Key Observations |
|---------|------------------|
| **`scraper.ts`** | 3-tier fallback: Rainforest API → Apify → hardcoded mock data. Exposes raw API key in URL query string for Rainforest (line 41). Apify polling blocks the request with `while` loop + 3s delays (lines 99-108). |
| **`apify.ts`** | Apify API wrapper. Returns mock run/dataset IDs if no token. |
| **`competitor.ts`** | **Hardcoded competitor data** for "Health" category only. Returns empty array for all other categories. |
| **`copywriter.ts`** | Calls OpenAI/OpenRouter for 8-stage landing page copy. Large prompt (~100 lines). Temperature 0.85, max_tokens 3000. Falls back to deterministic fallback copy if API fails or keys missing. |
| **`embedding.ts`** | **Stub implementation** — does NOT call OpenAI. Returns deterministic pseudo-random 1536-dim vectors based on text hash (lines 5-18). |
| **`rufusSimulator.ts`** | Calls OpenAI/OpenRouter to simulate 10 Rufus queries. Prompt is ~80 lines. Temperature 0.3, max_tokens 3000. Falls back to deterministic heuristic simulation. |
| **`pdf.ts`** | Uses Puppeteer to render `/p/:slug?print=true` and generate PDF. Hardcoded Windows Chrome path for Puppeteer (line 29). Retries on `ERR_NETWORK_CHANGED` (lines 54-66). |
| **`webhook.ts`** | Formats payloads for Discord, Slack, or generic JSON. No webhook URL = console.log mock output. |
| **`apollo.ts`** | Apollo.io API wrapper. Returns mock IDs if no API key. |
| **`catalogGraph.ts`** | Cosine similarity calculator. Calls `generateEmbedding()` for each competitor sequentially (lines 41-45) — could be parallelized. |
| **`optimization.ts`** | **Stub** — generates templated optimized content based on gaps. No LLM invocation. |
| **`analysis.ts`** | **Stub** — keyword-heuristic semantic analysis. Scores based on keyword presence in cleaned text. No LLM or real embedding comparison. |
| **`spapi.ts`** | Mock SP-API implementation. Always returns mock data. |

#### `api/agents/` (Orchestrator + 7 Agents + Reviewer)

**Orchestrator (`api/agents/orchestrator.ts`)**
- `OptimizationOrchestrator` extends `EventEmitter` (303 lines).
- Defines 6 hardcoded stages: `apify_fetcher` → `preprocessor` → `embedding_generator` → `semantic_analyzer` → `content_optimizer` → `competitor_analyst`.
- Executes stages sequentially in a `for` loop with **synchronous blocking**.
- Retry logic with exponential backoff (`Math.pow(2, attempt) * 500` ms, lines 289-290).
- After each stage, a `ReviewerAgent` runs and emits review events. Reviews are **non-blocking warnings** — pipeline continues even if review fails (lines 181-188).
- `finalReport` contains a suspicious `optimizedRufusScore` calculation: `Math.min(100, analysis.rufusScore + 15 + Math.floor(Math.random() * 10))` (line 201) — **score inflation with randomness**.

**Agent Implementations**
All agents implement the `Agent` interface (`role`, `execute(input)`):
- `ApifyFetcherAgent`: Queries DB for listings by `listingId` or `asin`. Falls back to hardcoded NutraWell mock data.
- `ListingFetcherAgent`: Calls `scrapeAmazonListing()`.
- `PreprocessorAgent`: Strips HTML, lowercases, normalizes unicode quotes, truncates to 32k chars.
- `EmbeddingGeneratorAgent`: Calls `generateEmbedding()` stub. Validates 1536-dim output.
- `SemanticAnalyzerAgent`: Calls `analyzeSemanticGaps()` stub.
- `ContentOptimizerAgent`: Calls `generateOptimizedContent()` stub. Validates title length, 5 bullets, 3+ QAs.
- `CompetitorAnalystAgent`: Calls `fetchCompetitors()` stub.

**Reviewer (`api/agents/reviewer.ts`)**
- Hardcoded validation rules per stage type (e.g., title > 10 chars, bullets >= 3, embedding must be 1536-dim).
- Score calculation is arbitrary arithmetic (`100 - issues.length * 25`).

#### `api/db/` (Database Layer)

**Client (`api/db/client.ts`)**
- Uses `better-sqlite3` with WAL mode.
- **Vercel workaround**: On Vercel, copies read-only bundled DB to `/tmp/optimus.db` on first access (lines 23-29). **Data is ephemeral on Vercel** — comment explicitly notes this.
- DB path configurable via `DB_PATH` env var.
- Exports TypeScript interfaces for all tables.

**Schema (`api/db/schema.ts`)**
- `initSchema()` runs on module load (side effect).
- CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS for: `prospects`, `listings`, `listing_analyses`, `bookings`, `prospect_activities`, `brand_settings`, `rufus_queries`, `rufus_query_runs`, `catalog_links`.
- **Migration anti-pattern**: Uses `try { ALTER TABLE ... } catch { /* ignore */ }` for adding columns (lines 176-250). This silently swallows all ALTER errors, not just "column already exists".
- `listing_analyses` has **22+ copy columns** for different landing page stages — highly denormalized.

---

### 3. Architectural Patterns

**Routing Pattern**
- tRPC v11 with plain routers and `publicProcedure`. **No authentication, no authorization, no input sanitization beyond Zod.**
- Mixed Hono + tRPC: Hono handles raw HTTP routes (`/health`, `/api/pdf/:slug`), tRPC handles RPC-style API.

**Service Layer**
- Services are mostly stateless async functions.
- No dependency injection — routers instantiate services/orchestrators directly.
- Some services are stubs with mock data fallbacks.

**Database Layer**
- Raw SQL via `better-sqlite3` prepared statements everywhere. No ORM, no query builder.
- No connection pooling (SQLite is file-based).
- No transaction wrappers — each statement is auto-committed.

**Agent/Worker Pattern**
- "Agent" pattern is essentially a pipeline of typed function calls wrapped in classes.
- No actual background workers, queues, or job processors. The orchestrator runs entirely within the HTTP request lifecycle.
- EventEmitter is used for observability but has no listeners attached in production code.

---

### 4. Event-Driven / Async Patterns

**Pub/Sub, Queues, Background Jobs: NONE**
- No message queue (Redis, RabbitMQ, SQS, etc.).
- No background job processor (Bull, pg-boss, etc.).
- No event bus beyond Node's `EventEmitter` in the orchestrator (which emits to nothing).
- The `OptimizationOrchestrator` runs synchronously inside HTTP request handlers. A complex pipeline with external API calls (Apify polling, OpenRouter LLM) blocks the tRPC mutation until completion.
- Webhook calls in `prospects.recordActivity` are `await`ed synchronously (line 179).

---

### 5. Token Usage, API Call Flows, Isolation

**Token/API Patterns**
- **OpenRouter/OpenAI**: Used in `copywriter.ts`, `rufusSimulator.ts`, and `scripts/runOptimization.ts`.
  - `copywriter.ts`: `max_tokens: 3000`, temperature 0.85, `response_format: { type: "json_object" }`.
  - `rufusSimulator.ts`: `max_tokens: 3000`, temperature 0.3.
  - `runOptimization.ts`: No `max_tokens` specified in one call; `response_format: { type: "json_object" }`.
- **API keys read from `process.env`** directly in modules. No centralized config or secrets manager.
- **No token usage tracking** or rate limiting. No LLM call caching.

**API Call Flows**
```
Frontend
  → tRPC mutation (Hono → fetchRequestHandler → router)
    → Router calls service/agent directly
      → Service may call external APIs (Rainforest, Apify, OpenRouter, Apollo)
        → All awaited synchronously
          → Results written to SQLite
            → Response returned to client
```

**Isolation Boundaries**
- **No isolation between tenants/prospects** — all data in single SQLite DB, no row-level security.
- **No isolation between API routes** — all publicProcedure, no auth middleware.
- `createContext` in tRPC handler returns `{}` (empty object).
- Scripts (`runOptimization.ts`, `testEndToEnd.ts`) import and execute DB/service code directly in the same process.

---

### 6. Backend Dependencies (from `package.json`)

Relevant backend/runtime deps:
- `hono` (^4.1.0) — HTTP framework
- `@trpc/server` (^11.0.0-rc.362) — tRPC (release candidate)
- `better-sqlite3` (^11.8.1) — SQLite driver
- `zod` (^3.23.8) — Schema validation
- `puppeteer` (^24.43.1) — PDF generation

**Notable absences:**
- No Redis, no queue library
- No ORM (Prisma, Drizzle, TypeORM)
- No auth library (Lucia, Auth.js, Passport)
- No testing framework (Jest, Vitest)
- No logging library (Pino, Winston) — uses `console.log/error/warn`
- No rate limiting library

---

### 7. Architectural Anti-Patterns & Issues

#### Critical / High Severity

1. **No Authentication / Authorization**
   - Every tRPC procedure is `publicProcedure`. Anyone can create prospects, trigger scrapes, run analyses, book calls, query any prospect's data by slug or ID.
   - `prospectMapper.ts` and frontend treat slug as a secret, but backend has no verification.

2. **Synchronous Blocking in Request Handlers**
   - `analysis.run` and `agents.optimize` run the full 6-stage orchestrator + LLM calls inside the HTTP request. No timeout handling. Request can hang for minutes.
   - Apify scraper polls with `while` loop + 3s sleep for up to 45 seconds.

3. **In-Memory State Storage**
   - `agents.ts` stores pipeline state in a `Map<string, PipelineState>` (line 7). Lost on server restart. Not shared across serverless instances.

4. **Data Loss on Vercel**
   - `api/db/client.ts` copies DB to `/tmp` on Vercel. `/tmp` is ephemeral. All writes (bookings, activities, views) are lost on cold starts.
   - `vercel.json` includes `data/optimus.db` in `includeFiles`, but writes go to `/tmp`.

5. **Hardcoded Secrets / API Keys in URLs**
   - `scraper.ts` line 41: `https://api.rainforestapi.com/request?api_key=${RAINFOREST_API_KEY}` — API key in query string (may appear in logs).

6. **Hardcoded Business Logic / Mock Data**
   - `competitor.ts` returns hardcoded magnesium supplement competitors for "Health" category only.
   - `api/services/analysis.ts` uses keyword heuristics, not real semantic analysis.
   - `api/services/embedding.ts` is a stub — no real OpenAI embeddings.
   - `api/services/spapi.ts` is entirely mock.
   - Multiple hardcoded mock data fallbacks when API keys are missing.

7. **SQL Injection Risk (Low but Present)**
   - `analysis.ts` line 83-96: Massive string-concatenated INSERT with `?` placeholders (safe), but `db.prepare()` with dynamic column lists in `regenerateCopy` uses template strings for the UPDATE query. The column names are hardcoded so it's currently safe, but pattern is risky.
   - `prospects.ts` `list` query builds `whereClause` dynamically but uses parameterized queries correctly.

8. **Migration Anti-Pattern**
   - `schema.ts` swallows ALL `ALTER TABLE` errors silently (lines 178-250). If a migration fails for reasons other than "column exists", it's ignored.

9. **Tight Coupling**
   - Routers directly import and instantiate `OptimizationOrchestrator`.
   - `analysis.ts` contains massive business logic (listing reconstruction, analysis, copy generation, DB insert) all in one function.
   - `runOptimization.ts` and `testEndToEnd.ts` duplicate large portions of `analysis.ts` logic.

10. **Schema Bloat**
    - `listing_analyses` table has 30+ columns for copy fields. This is essentially key-value data that should be normalized or stored as JSON.

11. **Error Handling Inconsistencies**
    - Some places throw errors that become 500s. Others catch and return empty arrays or nulls.
    - `catalogGraphRouter.ts` catch block returns `{ links: [] }` silently hiding errors.

12. **Missing Resource Cleanup**
    - `boot.ts` starts an HTTP server that listens indefinitely. No graceful shutdown handler.
    - Puppeteer browser is closed in `finally` block (good).

13. **CORS Misconfiguration**
    - `cors({ origin: "*" })` allows any origin. Fine for public API but risky if auth is added later.

14. **Type Safety Issues**
    - `any` types used extensively (`output_mode: any`, `input: any`, `Record<string, unknown>` casting).
    - `trpc.ts` has `eslint-disable @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any`.

---

### Summary

The project is a functional full-stack prototype with a Hono + tRPC backend and SQLite database. It implements an "agent orchestrator" pattern, but the agents are essentially sequential service calls with no actual async job processing. The architecture is suitable for a demo/MVP but has significant gaps for production:

- **No auth/authz**
- **No background job processing** (everything blocks HTTP requests)
- **Ephemeral data on Vercel**
- **Heavy reliance on stubs and mock data**
- **No real embedding generation** (despite the architecture suggesting it)
- **Database schema is denormalized** with many nullable copy columns

The code is well-organized into directories (routers, services, agents, db) and follows a clear separation of concerns, but the implementation details reveal tight coupling, duplicated logic between routers and scripts, and missing production infrastructure (queues, caching, auth, persistent storage).

</details>

[summary]
# Frontend Architecture Technical Report

## 1. Project Overview & Configuration

| File | Purpose |
|------|---------|
| `src/main.tsx` | React 19 entry point with `StrictMode` |
| `src/App.tsx` | Root component: `TRPCProvider` → `BrowserRouter` → `Routes` |
| `vite.config.ts` | Vite + `@vitejs/plugin-react`; dev proxy `/api` → `localhost:3000` |
| `tailwind.config.js` | Custom "brutalist" design system with brand colors, mono/display fonts, keyframes |
| `package.json` | React 19, tRPC v11 RC, TanStack Query v5, React Router v6, Tailwind v3 |

**Key dependencies:**
- `@trpc/react-query` `@trpc/client` `@trpc/server` `^11.0.0-rc.362`
- `@tanstack/react-query` `^5.28.0`
- `react-router-dom` `^6.22.3`
- `lucide-react` `^0.454.0`
- `clsx`, `tailwind-merge`, `zod`

---

## 2. Routing Architecture

**`src/App.tsx`** defines a flat route tree:

```tsx
<Route path="/admin" element={<AdminDashboard />} />
<Route path="/p/:slug" element={<ProspectLanding />} />
<Route path="/" element={<InvitationOnly />} />
<Route path="*" element={<InvitationOnly />} />
```

- **No route guards, no lazy loading (`React.lazy`), no nested route layouts.**
- `ProspectLanding` is parameterized by `:slug` and an optional `?print=true` query param.

---

## 3. State Management & Data Fetching

### Data Layer: tRPC + TanStack Query
**`src/providers/trpc.tsx`** creates a single `QueryClient` (no persistence) and a tRPC client with `httpBatchLink` to `/api/trpc`.

```tsx
export const trpc = createTRPCReact<AppRouter>();
```
- `refetchOnWindowFocus: false`, `retry: false`.
- **No global React Context for app state** — only the tRPC provider exists.
- **No Zustand, Redux, Jotai, or similar state library.**

### Local State Patterns
- Every component uses `useState`/`useRef` locally.
- `ProspectLanding.tsx` holds the "stage progression" state (`scanComplete`, `currentStage`) and passes it down to ~11 stage components.
- `AdminDashboard.tsx` holds tab state and form state locally.

---

## 4. Component Architecture

### Directory Structure
```
src/components/
├── landing/
│   ├── FloatingCTA.tsx
│   ├── ProgressBar.tsx
│   ├── StageAutopsy.tsx
│   ├── StageBleedCalculator.tsx
│   ├── StageBookCall.tsx
│   ├── StageBundlingBlueprint.tsx
│   ├── StageFreeQAs.tsx
│   ├── StageHero.tsx
│   ├── StagePPCPlanner.tsx
│   ├── StageProofWall.tsx
│   ├── StageRoadmap.tsx
│   ├── StageRufusSimulator.tsx
│   ├── StageScanAnimation.tsx
│   └── StageTransformPreview.tsx
└── prospect/          (empty)
```

### Component Taxonomy
| Component | Role | Key Props |
|-----------|------|-----------|
| `ProspectLanding` | **Orchestrator / Container** (383 lines) | Fetches data, manages scroll stage state, renders all stages |
| `StageHero` | Controlled presentation | `listing`, `headline`, `onScanComplete` |
| `StageAutopsy` | Tabbed dashboard (scores, COSMO graph, reviews) | `scores`, `cosmoGraphData`, `reviewSentiment` |
| `StageBleedCalculator` | Interactive calculator | `defaultPrice`, `defaultTraffic`, `conversionGap` |
| `StageRufusSimulator` | State machine (chat phases) | `scenarios`, `competitorAudit` |
| `StageTransformPreview` | Toggle + sandbox | `before`, `after`, `contentScore` |
| `StageBookCall` | Form + mutation | `prospectId`, `packageType`, `pricePoint` |
| `AdminDashboard` | Admin UI + nested sub-components | Self-contained |

### Notable Patterns
- **"Stage" naming convention:** The landing page is treated as an 11-stage linear narrative (Hero → Autopsy → Bleed → Simulator → Transform → Free QAs → PPC → Bundling → Roadmap → Proof → Book).
- **Visibility-gated rendering:** `ProspectLanding` only renders stages after `scanComplete`, and some stages are additionally gated by `currentStage >= N` or `isPrint`.
- **`key={`bleed-${prospect.id}`}`** and **`key={`book-${prospect.id}`}`** used on `StageBleedCalculator` and `StageBookCall` to force remount when the prospect changes.

---

## 5. Event-Driven Patterns, Hooks & Trackers

### `src/hooks/useScrollReveal.ts`
Simple `IntersectionObserver` hook for fade-in animations:
```tsx
export function useScrollReveal(threshold = 0.15): { ref, isVisible }
```
- Disconnects after first intersection (one-shot reveal).

### `src/hooks/useActivityTracker.ts`
Activity telemetry hook backed by tRPC mutation:
```tsx
export function useActivityTracker(prospectId: number) {
  const recordActivity = trpc.prospects?.recordActivity?.useMutation();
  // ...
  const trackScrollStage = (stageIndex, stageName) => { ... }
  return { interestScore, trackScrollStage, trackEvent };
}
```
- **Interest scoring:** Hardcoded score increments per stage (e.g., stage 10 = +30 points).
- Uses a `Set` in `useRef` to deduplicate scroll-stage events.
- **Anti-pattern:** `setInterestScore` callback invokes an async `mutate` without awaiting; errors are caught but the score still increments optimistically.

### `ProspectLanding.tsx` Scroll Engine
Manual `window.addEventListener('scroll', ...)` with a 0.4 viewport offset calculates which stage is in view and updates `currentStage`. This drives:
1. `ProgressBar` progress
2. `FloatingCTA` visibility
3. Activity tracking calls

---

## 6. Frontend ↔ Backend Communication

### tRPC Routers (defined in `api/router.ts`)
```
agents, prospects, scraper, analysis, apollo, booking, branding, rufusTracker, catalogGraph
```

### Key Queries/Mutations Used in Frontend
| Hook | File | Purpose |
|------|------|---------|
| `trpc.prospects.getBySlug.useQuery` | `ProspectLanding.tsx` | Load prospect by slug |
| `trpc.branding.getSettings.useQuery` | `ProspectLanding.tsx` | Load white-label brand colors/logo |
| `trpc.prospects.incrementViews.useMutation` | `ProspectLanding.tsx` | View counter |
| `trpc.prospects?.recordActivity?.useMutation` | `useActivityTracker.ts` | Telemetry |
| `trpc.booking?.create?.useMutation` | `StageBookCall.tsx` | Form submission |
| `trpc.prospects.list.useQuery` | `AdminDashboard.tsx` | Pipeline list |
| `trpc.prospects.getById.useQuery` | `AdminDashboard.tsx` | Detail panel |
| `trpc.rufusTracker.runSOVSimulation.useMutation` | `AdminDashboard.tsx` | SOV simulation |
| `trpc.scraper.trigger.useMutation` | `AdminDashboard.tsx` | Launch audit |
| `trpc.analysis.run.useMutation` | `AdminDashboard.tsx` | Run analysis |

### Transport
- **Batch link** (`httpBatchLink`) to `/api/trpc`.
- Vite dev proxy forwards `/api` to the Hono server on `localhost:3000`.

---

## 7. Design System & Styling

### Tailwind + Custom CSS
- **`tailwind.config.js`**: Defines brand palette (`brand-dark`, `brand-gold`, `brand-bg`, `brutal-red`, `terminal-green`, etc.) and custom brutalist shadows (`shadow-brutal`, `shadow-brutal-sm`, etc.).
- **`src/index.css`**: Extensive `@layer components` definitions for:
  - `.brutalist-card`, `.brutalist-btn`, `.brutalist-btn-danger`, `.brutalist-input`
  - `.terminal-screen`, `.terminal-line`, `.terminal-cursor`
  - `.gauge-bar`, `.gauge-bar-fill`
  - `.chat-phone-frame`, `.chat-bubble-buyer`, `.chat-bubble-rufus`
  - `.bleed-slider` (heavy custom `-webkit-slider-thumb` / `-moz-range-thumb` styling)
  - `.transform-toggle`
  - `.floating-cta`

### Dynamic Brand Injection
In `ProspectLanding.tsx` (lines 187–226), brand settings from `trpc.branding.getSettings.useQuery` are injected via:
```tsx
<style dangerouslySetInnerHTML={{ __html: `...` }} />
```
This overrides CSS custom properties and classes dynamically for white-label PDF rendering.

---

## 8. Type System

### `src/types/prospect.ts`
A single comprehensive file (~180 lines) defining:
- `ProspectListing`, `ProspectScoreBreakdown`, `ProspectIssue`, `ProspectOpportunity`
- `SimulatorScenario`, `TransformSnippet`, `FreeQAItem`, `ReviewSentimentProfile`
- `CompetitorComparison`, `PPCKeywordItem`, `BundlingItem`, `CosmoNodeData`
- `StageCopyData` (aggregates all copy for 8 stages)
- `ProspectData` (top-level domain object)
- `BookingFormData`, `PipelineProspect`

### `src/lib/prospectMapper.ts`
Maps raw backend `any` payload to typed `ProspectData`:
- Uses `safeJsonParse<T>` helper for SQLite JSON columns.
- Provides extensive fallback/default copy when backend fields are missing.
- **Input parameter is typed as `any`** (line 28).

### `src/lib/mockProspectData.ts`
Hardcoded `MOCK_PROSPECT_DATA` object used when `slug === 'mock-prospect'`.

---

## 9. Architectural Anti-Patterns & Inefficiencies

### A. React Anti-Patterns
1. **`useState` with side effects in `AdminDashboard.tsx` (lines 29–36)**
   ```tsx
   useState(() => {
     if (brandData) { setCompanyName(...); ... }
   });
   ```
   This is not idiomatic React. `useState` initializer should be pure. In `StrictMode`, this can run twice and cause unexpected state writes. It should be `useEffect`.

2. **`dangerouslySetInnerHTML` for CSS injection (`ProspectLanding.tsx`, line 188)**
   - If `brandData.primaryColor` or `brandData.logoBase64` are user-controlled (via the admin panel), this is an **XSS vector**.
   - No sanitization of the injected CSS string is visible.

3. **Direct DOM manipulation for scrolling**
   ```tsx
   const el = document.getElementById('stage-book');
   if (el) el.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });
   ```
   Used in `ProspectLanding.tsx` and `StageHero.tsx`. React refs should be preferred, especially since the elements are within the same component tree.

### B. Tight Coupling & Large Components
4. **`ProspectLanding.tsx` is a "god component" (383 lines)**
   - Fetches data, maps data, tracks scroll, tracks activity, injects brand CSS, conditionally renders 11 stages, handles error/loading states, and calculates bleed defaults.
   - **Recommendation:** Extract scroll orchestration into a custom hook (`useStageScroll`) and brand injection into a separate component.

5. **`AdminDashboard.tsx` is also a god component (783 lines)**
   - Contains `AuditLaunchBox`, `ProspectDetailPanel`, and `COSMOCanvas` all defined in the same file.
   - Heavy business logic for CSV generation (`handleDownloadBulkSheet`, lines 427–514) lives in the UI layer.

### C. Type Safety Issues
6. **Widespread use of `any`**
   - `mapBackendToProspectData(data: any)` in `prospectMapper.ts`
   - `p: any` in `AdminDashboard.tsx` list mapping (line 113)
   - `q: any` in SOV history mapping (line 643)
   - `links: any[]` in `COSMOCanvas`
   - `detailData` accesses use optional chaining but no strong typing (`detailData?.analysis`, etc.)

7. **Optional chaining on tRPC hooks**
   ```tsx
   const recordActivity = trpc.prospects?.recordActivity?.useMutation();
   const bookMutation = trpc.booking?.create?.useMutation();
   ```
   If these routers don't exist at runtime, the hook is `undefined` and the code silently does nothing. tRPC's type safety is undermined by the runtime optional chaining.

### D. Data & Logic Leakage
8. **Frontend CSV generation (`AdminDashboard.tsx`, lines 427–514)**
   - Constructs an Amazon Sponsored Products bulk sheet CSV entirely in the frontend.
   - Ad-group naming logic (`Intent_Sleep_Quality`, `Intent_Leg_Cramps`) and negative keyword derivation from gaps are business rules that should live on the backend.

9. **Hardcoded scoring simulation (`StageTransformPreview.tsx`, lines 55–85)**
   ```tsx
   if (text.includes('safe') || text.includes('safety')) { points += 14; }
   ```
   This is a client-side-only "sandbox" with arbitrary keyword-based scoring. It does not call the backend analysis service and can give misleading feedback.

10. **`StageScanAnimation.tsx` timeout accumulation**
    - `timeoutRef.current.push(t)` inside a `forEach` loop; the cleanup only clears timeouts created in the current effect, but the ref array is never reset between renders, leading to potential accumulation in edge cases.

### E. Inefficiencies
11. **No code splitting**
    - `App.tsx` imports all pages statically. `AdminDashboard` and `ProspectLanding` are large components loaded regardless of route.
    - **Recommendation:** Use `React.lazy(() => import('./pages/...'))` for route-based splitting.

12. **No React Error Boundary**
    - If any stage component throws (e.g., `StageAutopsy` parsing malformed `cosmoGraphData`), the entire `ProspectLanding` crashes.

13. **`visible` prop clutter**
    - Many stage components (`StageRoadmap`, `StageProofWall`, `StageBundlingBlueprint`, `StageFreeQAs`) accept a `visible` prop but **never reference it in their implementation**. This is dead API surface.

14. **`isPrint` mode handling is scattered**
    - Print-specific CSS is injected via `dangerouslySetInnerHTML`, and `isPrint` is passed to some stages but handled inconsistently (e.g., `StageAutopsy` uses it to skip animations; `StageHero` ignores it).

---

## 10. Summary Matrix

| Concern | Implementation | Assessment |
|---------|---------------|------------|
| **Framework** | React 19 + Vite | Modern, good |
| **Routing** | React Router v6, static imports | Simple but no lazy loading |
| **State Mgmt** | Local `useState` + tRPC/React Query | Sufficient for scope; no global store needed |
| **Data Fetching** | tRPC v11 RC + TanStack Query v5 | Type-safe (in theory), batched |
| **Styling** | Tailwind + heavy custom CSS | Cohesive "brutalist" system |
| **Type Safety** | TS with frequent `any` | Weak in mapper and dashboard |
| **Performance** | No code splitting, large components | Could degrade on low-end devices |
| **Security** | `dangerouslySetInnerHTML` for CSS | XSS risk if brand inputs unsanitized |
| **Testability** | No test files or testing deps | None observed |

---

## 11. Priority Recommendations

1. **Sanitize or eliminate `dangerouslySetInnerHTML`** in `ProspectLanding.tsx` — use CSS variables via inline styles or a safe CSS-in-JS approach.
2. **Refactor `ProspectLanding.tsx`** — extract scroll orchestration, brand injection, and stage mapping into separate hooks/components.
3. **Move CSV/business logic** from `AdminDashboard.tsx` to a backend tRPC mutation.
4. **Remove `any` types** in `prospectMapper.ts` and `AdminDashboard.tsx` by defining proper backend response DTOs.
5. **Add `React.lazy` + `Suspense`** for route-level code splitting.
6. **Add a React Error Boundary** to prevent total UI crashes.
7. **Fix `useState` side-effect initializer** in `AdminDashboard.tsx` (replace with `useEffect`).

</details>

# Database Layer & Data Flow Technical Report

## 1. `api/db/` Directory Analysis

### Files
- **`api/db/client.ts`** — Database connection singleton and TypeScript record interfaces
- **`api/db/schema.ts`** — Schema initialization and runtime migration logic

### Database Technology
**SQLite** via `better-sqlite3` (synchronous, compiled Node.js addon). The DB file lives at `data/optimus.db`.

### Schema Definitions (8 tables)

| Table | Purpose | Key Columns |
|-------|---------|-------------|
| `prospects` | Core lead/visitor records | `id`, `slug` (UNIQUE), `email`, `status`, `landingPageViews`, `packageType`, `pricePoint` |
| `listings` | Scraped Amazon product data | `id`, `prospectId` (FK), `asin`, `bullets` (JSON string), `images` (JSON string), `embeddingVector`, `rawScrapeData` |
| `listing_analyses` | AI-generated audit + copywriting | `id`, `listingId` (FK), `prospectId` (FK), 20+ `copy*` columns, scores |
| `bookings` | Demo call bookings | `id`, `prospectId` (FK), `name`, `email`, `scheduledDate`, `status` |
| `prospect_activities` | Event tracking / analytics | `id`, `prospectId` (FK), `eventType`, `eventData` (JSON string) |
| `brand_settings` | White-label agency config | `id`, `companyName`, `logoBase64`, `primaryColor` |
| `rufus_queries` | SOV simulation queries | `id`, `prospectId` (FK), `queryText`, `category` |
| `rufus_query_runs` | SOV simulation results per query | `id`, `queryId` (FK), `asinRankings` (JSON), `sovPercent` |
| `catalog_links` | COSMO graph edges | `id`, `prospectId` (FK), `sourceAsin`, `targetAsin`, `relationshipType`, `strengthScore` |

### Migration Pattern
**Runtime imperative migrations** inside `initSchema()` (`api/db/schema.ts`):
- Uses `CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS` for initial schema
- Runs `ALTER TABLE ADD COLUMN` in `try/catch` blocks for additive migrations
- Migrated columns include: `aPlusText`, `embeddingVector`, `packageType`, `pricePoint` (on prospects & analyses), and 22 new `copy*` fields on `listing_analyses`
- **No down-migrations, no migration versioning table, no transaction wrapper around migrations**

### Query Patterns
- **Prepared statements only** — every router uses `db.prepare("...").run()` / `.get()` / `.all()`
- **No ORM** — raw SQL with parameterized `?` placeholders
- **No query builder** (no Drizzle, Prisma, Kysely)
- JSON arrays/objects stored as `TEXT` columns with `JSON.stringify()` / `JSON.parse()` at boundaries

---

## 2. `data/` Directory & SQLite State

```
data/
  optimus.db       (131 KB)   — Main database file
  optimus.db-shm   (32 KB)    — WAL shared-memory file
  optimus.db-wal   (3.4 MB)   — Write-ahead log (large, indicating many uncommitted writes)
```

The large `.db-wal` size (3.4 MB vs 131 KB DB) suggests **significant write activity has occurred and WAL checkpointing may not have happened recently**, or the DB is under active write load. SQLite WAL mode is enabled (`db.pragma("journal_mode = WAL")`).

---

## 3. Full Request Flow (Router → Service → DB)

### Example Flow: Prospect Landing Page Load
```
Frontend (ProspectLanding.tsx)
  └─ trpc.prospects.getBySlug.useQuery({ slug })
      └─ HTTP GET /api/trpc/prospects.getBySlug?input={"slug":"..."}
          └─ Hono router (api/boot.ts) → tRPC fetchRequestHandler
              └─ prospectsRouter.getBySlug (api/routers/prospects.ts:45)
                  ├─ Query 1: SELECT * FROM prospects WHERE slug = ?
                  ├─ Query 2: SELECT * FROM listings WHERE prospectId = ? ORDER BY createdAt DESC LIMIT 1
                  ├─ Query 3: SELECT * FROM listing_analyses WHERE listingId = ? ORDER BY createdAt DESC LIMIT 1
                  └─ Returns { prospect, listing, analysis }
```

### Example Flow: Run Analysis Pipeline
```
Frontend admin dashboard
  └─ trpc.analysis.run.useMutation({ listingId })
      └─ analysisRouter.run (api/routers/analysis.ts:149)
          └─ runAnalysis(listingId)
              ├─ Query: SELECT * FROM listings WHERE id = ?
              ├─ Query: SELECT * FROM prospects WHERE id = ?
              ├─ Service call: OptimizationOrchestrator.runPipeline() (api/agents/orchestrator.ts)
              │   ├─ Semantic analysis stub (api/services/analysis.ts)
              │   ├─ Copywriter LLM call (api/services/copywriter.ts)
              │   └─ Returns scores + stage copy
              ├─ INSERT INTO listing_analyses (...) VALUES (..., 34 params)
              ├─ UPDATE prospects SET status = 'analyzed' WHERE id = ?
              └─ Query: SELECT * FROM listing_analyses WHERE id = ?
```

### Key Services Interacting with DB
| Service | File | DB Interaction |
|---------|------|----------------|
| Scraper | `api/services/scraper.ts` | Inserts into `listings` after Rainforest/Apify fetch |
| Analysis | `api/services/analysis.ts` | Semantic gap stub (no DB); orchestrator drives analysis |
| Optimization | `api/services/optimization.ts` | Content optimizer stub (no DB) |
| Rufus Simulator | `api/services/rufusSimulator.ts` | Called by router; router saves to `rufus_queries` + `rufus_query_runs` |
| Catalog Graph | `api/services/catalogGraph.ts` | Called by router; router saves to `catalog_links` |
| Embedding | `api/services/embedding.ts` | Stub; vectors saved by caller into `listings.embeddingVector` |
| PDF | `api/services/pdf.ts` | **No DB access** — renders `/p/{slug}?print=true` via Puppeteer |
| Webhook | `api/services/webhook.ts` | **No DB access** — dispatches to Discord/Slack/Zapier |
| Apollo | `api/services/apollo.ts` | External CRM integration |

---

## 4. Caching Layers, Session Management, State Persistence

### Caching
- **No Redis, no Memcached, no HTTP cache headers**
- **In-memory caching (SQLite-as-cache):**
  - `catalogGraphRouter` caches generated catalog links in `catalog_links` table; on subsequent calls it returns existing rows without recomputing (`api/routers/catalogGraphRouter.ts:13-19`)
  - `listings.embeddingVector` is computed once and reused for catalog graph builds
- **Client-side caching:** tRPC React Query hooks provide standard stale-while-revalidate caching

### Session Management
- **No sessions, no JWT, no cookies, no auth middleware**
- `publicProcedure` is used for every endpoint (`api/trpc.ts`) — fully public API
- No user authentication or authorization gates anywhere

### State Persistence
- **Pipeline state:** Stored in a `Map<string, PipelineState>` in `api/routers/agents.ts:7` — purely ephemeral in-memory. Comment explicitly says *"replace with Redis/DB in production"*
- **REPL:** `scripts/repl.ts` also holds `currentState` in-memory

---

## 5. ETL, Batch Processing & Data Pipeline Patterns

### Scripts Directory (`scripts/`)

| Script | Purpose | Pattern |
|--------|---------|---------|
| `runOptimization.ts` | Full CLI pipeline for a given ASIN | **ETL orchestrator** — scrapes, runs conditional tools by package tier, generates LLM copy, writes all DB tables, produces PDF |
| `testEndToEnd.ts` | End-to-end integration test | **Batch pipeline** — hardcoded NutraWell ASIN, cleans old data, runs full pipeline, validates outputs |
| `createMockProspect.ts` | Seed script for demo prospect | **Data seeding/ETL** — inserts hardcoded prospect + listing + analysis with full copy |
| `createGoPureProspect.ts` | Seed script for goPure demo | Same pattern as mock |
| `removeMockProspect.ts` | Cleanup utility | Deletes seeded demo data |
| `repl.ts` | Interactive CLI | No DB interaction; purely orchestrator debugging |

### Pipeline Patterns Observed
1. **Cleanup → Create → Scrape → Analyze → Simulate → Graph → PDF** (sequential, no parallelization)
2. **Package-conditional branching:** In `runOptimization.ts`, tools are gated by `packageNum`:
   - Package 1/4: fetch competitors
   - Package 1: run Rufus SOV simulation
   - Package 4: generate catalog graph + embeddings
3. **No job queue** (no Bull, no BullMQ, nopg-boss) — everything runs synchronously in the request/CLI thread
4. **No idempotency keys** — rerunning a script with the same slug deletes old data first (manual cleanup block)

---

## 6. Connection Pooling, Transactions & Query Optimization

### Connection Pooling
- **None.** `better-sqlite3` creates a **single synchronous connection**:
  ```ts
  export const db: Database.Database = new Database(dbPath);
  ```
  There is no pool, no max connections, no connection retry logic. In a serverless environment (Vercel), this means each cold start creates a new SQLite handle to `/tmp/optimus.db`.

### Transaction Handling
- **No explicit transactions anywhere.**
- Every mutation is auto-committed by SQLite.
- Multi-step operations like `runAnalysis()` perform:
  1. `INSERT INTO listing_analyses ...`
  2. `UPDATE prospects SET status = 'analyzed' ...`
  If step 2 fails after step 1 succeeds, the analysis row is orphaned and the prospect status remains stale.
- **No `BEGIN` / `COMMIT` / `ROLLBACK` wrappers** found in any router or script.

### Query Optimization
- **No indexes defined** beyond primary keys and implicit UNIQUE constraints (`prospects.slug`, `prospects.id`, etc.)
- **WAL mode enabled** (`db.pragma("journal_mode = WAL")`) — good for read concurrency
- **No `EXPLAIN QUERY PLAN` usage** or query analysis
- Several queries use `ORDER BY createdAt DESC LIMIT 1` to get "latest" records — functional but without indexes on `createdAt` or `prospectId`, these are full table scans followed by sorts.

---

## 7. Data Integrity Issues, N+1 Queries & Missing Indexes

### Missing Indexes (Confirmed by Code Review)
The schema has **zero explicit secondary indexes**. These are missing:

| Table | Missing Index | Impact |
|-------|--------------|--------|
| `prospects` | `idx_prospects_slug` | Every landing page lookup scans by `slug` |
| `prospects` | `idx_prospects_status` | Admin dashboard list filtering scans |
| `listings` | `idx_listings_prospectId` | `getBySlug`, `getById`, `scraperRouter` all query by `prospectId` |
| `listing_analyses` | `idx_analyses_listingId` + `idx_analyses_prospectId` | Analysis lookups scan |
| `bookings` | `idx_bookings_prospectId` | Booking list for a prospect scans |
| `prospect_activities` | `idx_activities_prospectId` | Activity log queries scan |
| `rufus_queries` | `idx_rufus_queries_prospectId` | SOV history queries scan |
| `catalog_links` | `idx_catalog_links_prospectId` | Graph retrieval scans |

### N+1 Queries
- **`prospectsRouter.list`** (`api/routers/prospects.ts:65-97`):
  ```sql
  SELECT p.*, l.asin
  FROM prospects p
  LEFT JOIN listings l ON l.prospectId = p.id
    AND l.id = (SELECT id FROM listings WHERE prospectId = p.id ORDER BY createdAt DESC LIMIT 1)
  ```
  This uses a correlated subquery in the JOIN clause. While SQLite optimizes this reasonably, it is effectively an N+1 pattern for listings.

- **`prospectsRouter.getBySlug` / `getById`**:
  Runs 3 separate queries sequentially instead of a single JOIN:
  1. `SELECT * FROM prospects WHERE slug = ?`
  2. `SELECT * FROM listings WHERE prospectId = ? ... LIMIT 1`
  3. `SELECT * FROM listing_analyses WHERE listingId = ? ... LIMIT 1`

### Data Integrity Issues

1. **No foreign key enforcement pragma**
   - Schema defines `FOREIGN KEY` constraints, but `better-sqlite3` **does not enable FK enforcement by default**.
   - `db.pragma("foreign_keys = ON")` is **never called** in `client.ts` or `schema.ts`.
   - Deleting a prospect will leave orphaned rows in `listings`, `listing_analyses`, `bookings`, etc., unless manually cleaned.

2. **Orphaned data on Vercel**
   - `api/db/client.ts:21-32` copies the bundled DB to `/tmp/optimus.db` on every cold start.
   - `/tmp` is ephemeral in serverless. Writes (bookings, views, activities) are lost between cold starts.
   - **Data durability bug:** The bundled DB in the deployment bundle never receives the mutations written to `/tmp`.

3. **Hardcoded fallback data in production code**
   - `prospectsRouter.recordActivity` has a hardcoded fallback for `prospectId === 5` ("Alex Hormozi", "Acme Greens") at lines 167-169 and 173-175. This leaks demo data into production error handling.

4. **Unsafe `any` casts in DB layer**
   - `catalogGraphRouter.ts`, `rufusTrackerRouter.ts`, `brandingRouter.ts` all cast query results to `any[]` or `any`, bypassing the typed `Record` interfaces defined in `client.ts`.

5. **Race condition on view counting**
   - `incrementViews` uses a separate `UPDATE` then `SELECT`. Under concurrent load (Vercel serverless), two requests could read the same value before either writes, causing lost increments.

6. **No input sanitization on JSON fields**
   - `rawScrapeData`, `bullets`, `images` are stored as strings but never validated against schema before insertion. Malformed JSON will crash `JSON.parse()` on read.

### Summary Table of Architectural Gaps

| Concern | Severity | Location |
|---------|----------|----------|
| No FK enforcement | **High** | `api/db/client.ts` |
| No indexes on foreign keys | **High** | `api/db/schema.ts` |
| No transactions | **High** | All routers & scripts |
| Ephemeral DB on Vercel | **Critical** | `api/db/client.ts:21-32` |
| In-memory pipeline store | **Medium** | `api/routers/agents.ts:7` |
| Hardcoded demo fallback | **Low** | `api/routers/prospects.ts:167` |
| N+1 query patterns | **Medium** | `api/routers/prospects.ts` |
| Missing connection pooling | **Medium** | `api/db/client.ts` |
| No auth on any endpoint | **High** | `api/trpc.ts` |

</details>

[summary]
# Technical Report: Optimus Rufus — Business Domain, Capabilities & Event-Driven Architecture Gaps

## 1. Executive Summary

**Optimus Rufus** is an AI-powered Amazon Listing Optimization platform built as a monolithic full-stack TypeScript application. While the documentation describes a full SaaS product (subscription tiers, Paddle payments, Kimi OAuth, MySQL + Qdrant), the **actual implementation** has pivoted toward an **agency/lead-generation portal** with a SQLite-backed prospect pipeline, white-labeled PDF audits, and LLM-generated landing page copy.

The system scrapes Amazon listings, runs a multi-agent analysis pipeline, simulates Rufus/COSMO compatibility, and generates personalized sales pages designed to convert prospects into booked audit calls.

---

## 2. Business Domain Model

### 2.1 Core Entities

| Entity | Purpose | Key Relationships |
|--------|---------|-------------------|
| **Prospect** | A lead/client record identified by a unique `slug`. Tracks funnel status (`new` → `analyzed` → `booked`). | 1:N Listings, 1:N Bookings, 1:N Activities |
| **Listing** | Scraped Amazon product data (ASIN, title, bullets, description, A+ text, images, raw scrape payload). | Belongs to 1 Prospect. Has 1:N Analyses. |
| **Listing Analysis** | The output of the AI pipeline — scores, semantic gaps, and **8 stages of personalized landing page copy**. | Belongs to 1 Listing + 1 Prospect. |
| **Booking** | A scheduled consultation/audit call request. | Belongs to 1 Prospect. |
| **Rufus Query / Run** | Simulated conversational queries and SOV (Share-of-Voice) rankings over time. | Belongs to 1 Prospect. |
| **Catalog Link** | Computed cosine-similarity relationships between client ASIN and competitors (`substitute`, `complementary`, `co_occurrence`). | Belongs to 1 Prospect. |
| **Brand Settings** | White-label configuration (logo, colors) for agency PDF generation. | Singleton / global. |

### 2.2 Package Tier Business Logic

The product is sold through **4 agency packages** (not subscription SaaS tiers):

| Package | Name | Features Triggered |
|---------|------|-------------------|
| 1 | SOV & Conquesting | Competitor fetch, Rufus SOV simulation, free Q&As, review sentiment, competitor audit, COSMO graph data |
| 2 | Full-Funnel | Core listing rewrite, A+ content copy, storefront SEO structure |
| 3 | AEO & PPC | PPC keyword map, 30-day alignment plan, ACOS guarantee framing |
| 4 | COSMO Bundling | Embedding generation, catalog graph building, virtual bundle blueprints |

---

## 3. Current Technical Capabilities

### 3.1 Technology Stack (Actual)

| Layer | Technology | Notes |
|-------|-----------|-------|
| **Frontend** | React 19 + Vite + Tailwind CSS + shadcn/ui | SPA with react-router-dom |
| **Backend** | Hono 4.x + tRPC 11 (RC) | HTTP adapter via `fetchRequestHandler` |
| **Database** | SQLite (`better-sqlite3`) | WAL mode. Docs specify MySQL 8.0 — **not implemented**. |
| **Vector DB** | Qdrant | Documented but **not wired in code** — embeddings stored as JSON text in SQLite |
| **AI/LLM** | OpenAI API + OpenRouter (fallback) | `gpt-4o-mini` for copy, `gpt-4o` for Rufus simulation |
| **Scraping** | Rainforest API (primary) → Apify (fallback) → Mock data | 3-tier fallback chain |
| **PDF Gen** | Puppeteer | Renders `/p/:slug` landing page to PDF |
| **Auth** | None in tRPC layer | All procedures are `publicProcedure`. Docs specify Kimi OAuth + JWT — **not implemented**. |
| **Payments** | None in code | Docs specify Paddle — **not implemented**. |
| **Hosting** | Vercel (serverless) or VPS | SQLite copied to `/tmp` on Vercel (ephemeral) |

### 3.2 Multi-Agent Pipeline

The `OptimizationOrchestrator` extends Node.js `EventEmitter` and runs 6 sequential stages:

1. **Apify Fetcher** → Scrape or load mock listing data
2. **Preprocessor** → Text cleaning, HTML removal, normalization
3. **Embedding Generator** → Stub: deterministic pseudo-random 1536-dim vector (OpenAI integration is stubbed)
4. **Semantic Analyzer** → Keyword-heuristic gap analysis (12 dimensions), computes Rufus/COSMO scores
5. **Content Optimizer** → Template-based title, 5 bullets, Q&A generation
6. **Competitor Analyst** → Stub: returns empty array

**Reviewer Agent** validates output after each stage with hardcoded rules (title length, bullet count, embedding dimension, score ranges).

### 3.3 Key Services

| Service | File | Responsibility |
|---------|------|----------------|
| `scraper.ts` | `api/services/scraper.ts` | Rainforest → Apify → Mock fallback |
| `copywriter.ts` | `api/services/copywriter.ts` | LLM prompt to generate 8-stage landing copy |
| `rufusSimulator.ts` | `api/services/rufusSimulator.ts` | LLM-based Rufus query simulation + SOV scoring |
| `pdf.ts` | `api/services/pdf.ts` | Puppeteer-based white-label PDF generation |
| `webhook.ts` | `api/services/webhook.ts` | Discord/Slack/Zapier prospect activity notifications |
| `catalogGraph.ts` | `api/services/catalogGraph.ts` | Cosine similarity competitor linking |
| `optimization.ts` | `api/services/optimization.ts` | Stub: template-based content optimization |
| `analysis.ts` | `api/services/analysis.ts` | Stub: keyword-heuristic semantic gap scoring |
| `embedding.ts` | `api/services/embedding.ts` | Stub: pseudo-random normalized vector |
| `competitor.ts` | `api/services/competitor.ts` | Stub: returns empty array |

## 4. Event-Driven & Async Processing Analysis

### 4.1 What Exists Today

The orchestrator emits the following events:
- `pipeline:start`, `stage:start`, `stage:complete`, `review:complete`, `review:warning`, `pipeline:complete`, `pipeline:error`

These are consumed by:
- **REPL script** (`scripts/repl.ts`) — real-time CLI progress display
- **In-memory state** — `PipelineState` stored in a `Map<string, PipelineState>` inside `agentsRouter`

The `prospects.recordActivity` tRPC mutation has a **fire-and-forget webhook** pattern: it logs to SQLite and then `await triggerWebhook(...)` before returning. No retry, no queue, no dead-letter handling.

### 4.2 Token Isolation & Cost Control

**Current State: No isolation. No cost tracking.**

- LLM calls are made **synchronously inside request handlers and scripts** with `fetch()` to OpenAI/OpenRouter.
- There is **no per-prospect token budget**, **no per-job cost accumulator**, and **no circuit breaker** for API spend.
- The `generatePdf` service uses Puppeteer to render a full React page — this is CPU-intensive and runs **inline in the HTTP request** (`/api/pdf/:slug`).
- The `runOptimization.ts` script performs sequential blocking LLM calls + Puppeteer PDF generation in a single Node process.

### 4.3 Async Processing Patterns

| Requirement | Docs Specification | Actual Implementation | Gap |
|-------------|-------------------|----------------------|-----|
| Background jobs | Redis/RabbitMQ for async jobs | None. All processing is synchronous. | **Critical** |
| Pipeline state persistence | Redis pipeline store | In-memory `Map` (lost on restart) | **Critical** |
| WebSocket streaming | Socket.IO for real-time updates | Not implemented | Medium |
| Retry logic | Exponential backoff (1s, 2s, 4s) | Implemented in orchestrator, but only for agent `execute()` | Partial |
| Caching | Redis for SP-API, embeddings, reports | None | **High** |
| Rate limiting | 100 req/ip/minute | None implemented | **High** |

---

## 5. Observability, Monitoring & Logging

### 5.1 Current State

| Concern | Implementation | Gap |
|---------|---------------|-----|
| **Error Tracking** | None in code. Docs specify Sentry (`@sentry/node`, `@sentry/react`) with source maps, profiling, and Hono error handler. | Sentry is **not imported or initialized** in `api/boot.ts` or frontend. |
| **Structured Logging** | `console.log/console.error` with emoji prefixes (e.g., `🔍 [Scraper] ...`) | No structured JSON logs, no correlation IDs, no log levels. |
| **Metrics** | None | No Prometheus/Grafana/Datadog integration. |
| **Health Checks** | Basic `/health` endpoint returns `{ status: "ok" }` | No DB connectivity, no dependency checks. |
| **Tracing** | None | No distributed tracing for multi-stage pipeline. |
| **Alerts** | Webhook notifications for prospect activity | No system-level alerting (CPU, memory, error rates). |

### 5.2 PM2 / Deployment

The `deployment-devops.md` specifies PM2 with log rotation, memory limits (`max_memory_restart: 1G`), and cluster mode. The actual `package.json` has **no PM2 ecosystem file**, no Docker Compose, and no production deployment scripts in the repo.

---

## 6. Critical Gaps for Event-Driven Architecture

Based on the documentation requirements and the actual codebase, the following gaps must be addressed to achieve a production-grade event-driven architecture:

### 6.1 Infrastructure Gaps

| Gap | Impact | Recommended Action |
|-----|--------|-------------------|
| **No Message Queue** | LLM calls, scraping, and PDF generation block the event loop. No horizontal scaling possible. | Introduce **BullMQ + Redis** or **Inngest** for job queuing. |
| **No Persistent State Store** | Pipeline progress is lost on server restart. | Replace in-memory `Map` with **Redis** or **SQLite job table** with status tracking. |
| **No Caching Layer** | Repeated scrapes and LLM calls for identical ASINs waste money and time. | Add **Redis** for SP-API responses (1h TTL), embeddings (24h), and reports (1h). |
| **SQLite on Vercel** | `/tmp` is ephemeral — data lost on cold starts. | Migrate to **PostgreSQL** (Neon/Supabase) or **MySQL** (Planetscale/RDS) as documented. |
| **No Auth/Authz** | All tRPC procedures are public. | Implement JWT middleware, rate limiting, and subscription tier checks. |

### 6.2 Business Logic Gaps

| Gap | Impact | Recommended Action |
|-----|--------|-------------------|
| **Token/Cost Isolation Missing** | A single run could exhaust API budget. No per-prospect caps. | Add **token budgeting** per package tier; queue jobs with cost estimates; implement circuit breakers. |
| **No Async Pipeline Trigger** | `agents.optimize` mutation blocks the HTTP connection for 3–5+ seconds. | Return `pipelineId` immediately; emit events via SSE/WebSocket; process pipeline in background worker. |
| **No Dead-Letter / Retry Queue** | Failed LLM calls or scrapes are retried only 3x inline. No visibility into failures. | Implement **DLQ** in BullMQ with exponential backoff and admin dashboard retry buttons. |
| **Webhook Fire-and-Forget** | Webhook failures are silent (logged to console only). | Make webhooks **queued jobs** with retry logic and delivery status tracking. |
| **No Usage Tracking** | No metering for analyses, scrapes, or LLM tokens. | Add `usage_events` table or stream to analytics queue for billing enforcement. |

### 6.3 Agent Orchestrator Gaps

| Gap | Impact | Recommended Action |
|-----|--------|-------------------|
| **Sequential Execution Only** | Competitor analysis could run in parallel with embedding. | Refactor orchestrator to support **DAG-based stage parallelism** where safe. |
| **No Stage Persistence** | If stage 5 fails, stages 1–4 must be re-run. | Persist intermediate outputs per stage to DB/cache for resumability. |
| **No Human-in-the-Loop** | No pause/review gates for high-stakes stages. | Add `awaiting_approval` status and admin review endpoints. |
| **Stub Services Dominant** | Embedding, competitor fetch, and SP-API are stubs. | Implement real OpenAI embedding, Rainforest/SP-API integrations, and competitor search. |

---

## 7. Summary: Current vs. Documented Architecture

| Component | Documented (MVP Spec) | Actual Implementation | Deviation |
|-----------|----------------------|----------------------|-----------|
| Database | MySQL 8.0 + Drizzle ORM | SQLite (`better-sqlite3`) with raw SQL | **Major** |
| Vector DB | Qdrant (self-hosted Docker) | JSON text column in SQLite | **Major** |
| Auth | Kimi OAuth 2.0 + JWT sessions | None (all public procedures) | **Major** |
| Payments | Paddle subscriptions | None | **Major** |
| Queue | Redis/RabbitMQ for async jobs | None | **Major** |
| Monitoring | Sentry + Grafana + Prometheus | Console logs only | **Major** |
| AI Pipeline | 6-stage agent orchestrator with real OpenAI embeddings | EventEmitter orchestrator with stubbed agents | **Partial** |
| Frontend | 8 route-level SaaS pages | Agency portal (Admin + Prospect Landing) | **Partial** |

---

## 8. Recommended Priority Roadmap for Event-Driven Architecture

1. **P0 — Job Queue**: Introduce BullMQ + Redis. Move `runOptimization`, `generatePdf`, and `simulateRufusSOV` to background workers.
2. **P0 — Pipeline State Persistence**: Store `PipelineState` in Redis or a dedicated `pipeline_jobs` SQLite/PostgreSQL table with status transitions.
3. **P1 — Token Budgeting**: Track OpenAI/OpenRouter token usage per job; enforce per-prospect monthly limits.
4. **P1 — Caching**: Redis cache for scraped listings and embeddings to reduce API costs.
5. **P1 — Structured Logging**: Pino/Winston with correlation IDs; pipe to Loki/Datadog.
6. **P2 — Event Bus**: Decouple prospect activity tracking from HTTP request lifecycle using domain events.
7. **P2 — SSE/WebSocket Streaming**: Real-time pipeline progress updates for the frontend.
8. **P2 — Auth & Rate Limiting**: Implement JWT middleware and per-IP rate limiting on tRPC.

## 🔬 AUDIT COMPLETE — 4-AGENT CONSENSUS

**Verdict:** This is a functional agency-portal MVP with severe architectural debt. It is **not** event-driven, **not** token-isolated, and **not** production-ready.

### Critical Findings

| Vector | Finding | Severity |
|--------|---------|----------|
| **Event-Driven** | Zero message queues. All 6-stage LLM pipelines block HTTP requests. Orchestrator emits to `EventEmitter` with **zero listeners** in production. | 🔴 Critical |
| **Token Isolation** | No token budgeting, no cost tracking, no circuit breakers. OpenRouter calls inline with `max_tokens: 3000`. A single prospect can exhaust your API budget. | 🔴 Critical |
| **State Persistence** | Pipeline state stored in `Map<string, PipelineState>` — **ephemeral in-memory**. Lost on restart/Vercel cold start. | 🔴 Critical |
| **Data Integrity** | SQLite on Vercel copied to `/tmp` — **all writes evaporate** on cold start. No FK enforcement. No transactions. No indexes. | 🔴 Critical |
| **AuthZ** | Every tRPC procedure is `publicProcedure`. No JWT, no sessions, no rate limiting. | 🔴 Critical |
| **Service Maturity** | Embedding, competitor analysis, and SP-API are **stubs** returning mock data. | 🟡 High |
| **Frontend** | God components (`ProspectLanding.tsx` 383 lines, `AdminDashboard.tsx` 783 lines), no code splitting, XSS via `dangerouslySetInnerHTML` CSS injection. | 🟡 High |

---

## 🏗️ TARGET ARCHITECTURE: "Optimus Rufus — Event-Driven Core"

I am now entering **Plan Mode** to design the refactoring blueprint. The target is a **token-gated, event-driven, horizontally-scalable ecosystem** with these pillars:

### 1. Event Bus & Job Queue
- **BullMQ + Redis** for job orchestration (local/VPS) with **SQLite fallback queue** for serverless
- Domain events: `PipelineStarted`, `StageCompleted`, `TokenBudgetExceeded`, `CircuitBreakerOpened`, `WebhookDispatched`
- Async routers: mutations enqueue jobs, return `jobId`, frontend streams via SSE

### 2. Token Isolation Layer
- `TokenBudgetService` wraps every LLM call
- Per-prospect budget caps by package tier
- Real-time cost accumulation + circuit breaker on spend thresholds
- Token usage persisted to `usage_events` table

### 3. Resumable Pipeline Engine
- Replace `EventEmitter` orchestrator with **DAG-based stage executor**
- Each stage output persisted to `pipeline_job_stages` table
- Failed jobs resume from last successful stage (no re-running embeddings)
- Parallelize independent stages (e.g., `competitor_analyst` + `embedding_generator`)

### 4. Persistent State & Transactions
- `pipeline_jobs` table: `id`, `prospectId`, `status`, `currentStage`, `stagesJSON`, `tokenUsage`, `errorLog`
- Multi-step DB operations wrapped in `BEGIN/COMMIT`
- Add missing indexes on all FK columns

### 5. Frontend Streaming
- SSE endpoint `/api/sse/pipeline/:jobId` streams stage progress
- Replace polling with reactive event consumption
- Error boundaries + React.lazy code splitting

Let me write the full implementation plan now.

{
  "path": "C:\\Users\\hp\\.kimi\\plans\\batgirl-wally-west-taskmaster.md",
  "content": "# Optimus Rufus — Event-Driven Refactoring Plan\n\n## Objective\nTransform the monolithic, synchronous, blocking-request MVP into a **token-isolated, event-driven, resumable, horizontally-scalable ecosystem** while preserving all existing business logic and frontend UX.\n\n---\n\n## Current State Diagnosis\n\n| Dimension | Current | Target |\n|-----------|---------|--------|\n| **Pipeline Execution** | Synchronous 6-stage blocking HTTP mutation | Async background job with resumable stages |\n| **State Storage** | In-memory `Map<string, PipelineState>` | Persistent `pipeline_jobs` + `pipeline_job_stages` tables |\n| **Token/Cost Control** | None. Inline LLM calls with no tracking | Per-prospect token budget with circuit breaker |\n| **Event System** | `EventEmitter` with zero production listeners | Typed domain event bus + job queue |\n| **DB Integrity** | No FK enforcement, no indexes, no transactions | FKs ON, indexes on all FKs, atomic transactions |\n| **Frontend Progress** | No real-time pipeline feedback | SSE stream + reactive stage progress |\n| **External APIs** | Inline fetch with basic retry | Circuit breaker + cached responses |\n\n---\n\n## Architectural Decisions\n\n### 1. Queue & Event Bus Abstraction\nTo support both **Vercel serverless** (no Redis) and **VPS/PM2** (Redis available), we introduce a `QueueAdapter` and `EventBusAdapter` interface with two implementations:\n\n- **`SQLiteQueueAdapter`** — stores jobs in a new `job_queue` table with `status` (`pending`, `active`, `completed`, `failed`), `attempts`, `delay`, and `payload`. A `QueueWorker` polls the table every N seconds.\n- **`BullMQQueueAdapter`** — wraps BullMQ for Redis-backed production deployments.\n\nThe active adapter is selected via `QUEUE_DRIVER=sqlite|bullmq` env var.\n\n### 2. Token Isolation Layer (`TokenBudgetService`)\n- Wraps **every** LLM invocation (OpenAI, OpenRouter, copywriter, Rufus simulator).\n- Tracks `promptTokens`, `completionTokens`, `totalTokens`, `estimatedCost` per `prospectId` + `jobId`.\n- Enforces per-prospect monthly caps by `packageType` tier:\n  - Package 1: $5\n  - Package 2: $15\n  - Package 3: $30\n  - Package 4: $50\n- Emits `token-budget-exceeded` domain event when threshold hit.\n- Circuit breaker: if 5 consecutive LLM errors occur within 60s, breaker opens for 120s.\n\n### 3. Resumable Pipeline Engine (`PipelineEngine`)\nReplaces `OptimizationOrchestrator`:\n- Defines stages as a **DAG** (directed acyclic graph) instead of a hardcoded array.\n- Stages 1→2→3→4→5→6 remain sequential where data-dependent, but independent branches (e.g., competitor fetch + embedding generation) run in parallel.\n- After each stage completes, output is serialized to `pipeline_job_stages` table.\n- On retry, the engine loads completed stages and resumes from the first failed stage.\n- Emits typed events: `pipeline:start`, `stage:start`, `stage:complete`, `stage:error`, `pipeline:complete`, `pipeline:error`.\n\n### 4. Database Hardening\n- Enable `PRAGMA foreign_keys = ON` in `api/db/client.ts`.\n- Add secondary indexes on all foreign key columns and query filters.\n- Wrap multi-step mutations in `BEGIN...COMMIT/ROLLBACK` transactions.\n- Add `pipeline_jobs`, `pipeline_job_stages`, `usage_events` tables.\n- Add `jobs` table for SQLite queue implementation.\n\n### 5. Async API Surface\n- `agents.optimize` mutation → enqueues job, returns `{ jobId }` immediately.\n- `agents.getStatus` query → returns current pipeline status + stage outputs.\n- `agents.retryStage` mutation → enqueues retry job for specific stage.\n- New SSE endpoint `/api/sse/pipeline/:jobId` streams events to frontend.\n\n### 6. Frontend Adaptations\n- `ProspectLanding` and `AdminDashboard` consume `agents.getStatus` polling + optional SSE.\n- `StageScanAnimation` and `ProgressBar` bind to real pipeline stage events.\n- Add `React.lazy` route splitting for `AdminDashboard` and `ProspectLanding`.\n- Add React Error Boundary around stage components.\n\n---\n\n## Implementation Phases\n\n### Phase 1: Foundation — Database Hardening & Schema Expansion\n**Files:** `api/db/schema.ts`, `api/db/client.ts`, `api/db/migrations/`\n\n1. Enable `foreign_keys = ON` in `client.ts`.\n2. Create migration utility that runs numbered `.sql` files in order (replace silent `try/catch ALTER TABLE` anti-pattern).\n3. Migration `001_add_indexes.sql`:\n   - `idx_prospects_slug`, `idx_prospects_status`\n   - `idx_listings_prospectId`\n   - `idx_analyses_listingId`, `idx_analyses_prospectId`\n   - `idx_bookings_prospectId`, `idx_activities_prospectId`\n   - `idx_rufus_queries_prospectId`, `idx_catalog_links_prospectId`\n4. Migration `002_add_pipeline_tables.sql`:\n   - `pipeline_jobs`: `id`, `prospectId`, `listingId`, `packageType`, `status`, `currentStage`, `stagesJSON`, `tokenUsage`, `errorLog`, `createdAt`, `updatedAt`\n   - `pipeline_job_stages`: `id`, `jobId`, `stageName`, `status`, `outputJSON`, `errorMessage`, `startedAt`, `completedAt`\n   - `usage_events`: `id`, `prospectId`, `jobId`, `service`, `promptTokens`, `completionTokens`, `costCents`, `createdAt`\n   - `jobs` (for SQLite queue): `id`, `queue`, `name`, `dataJSON`, `optsJSON`, `progress`, `delay`, `timestamp`, `attempts`, `maxAttempts`, `processedOn`, `finishedOn`, `returnValueJSON`, `failedReason`, `stacktraceJSON`\n5. Wrap `client.ts` with a transaction helper: `withTransaction<T>(fn: (db: Database) => T): T`.\n\n### Phase 2: Event Bus & Queue Infrastructure\n**Files:** `api/infra/eventBus.ts`, `api/infra/queue.ts`, `api/infra/types.ts`\n\n1. Define `EventBus` interface:\n   ```ts\n   emit<T>(event: string, payload: T): void\n   on<T>(event: string, handler: (payload: T) => void): void\n   ```\n2. Implement `MemoryEventBus` (singleton EventEmitter wrapper) and `RedisEventBus`.\n3. Define `JobQueue` interface:\n   ```ts\n   add(name: string, data: unknown, opts?: JobOpts): Promise<Job>\n   getJob(id: string): Promise<Job | null>\n   ```\n4. Implement `SQLiteJobQueue` with polling worker (`QueueWorker` class).\n5. Implement `BullMQJobQueue` wrapper.\n6. Add `QueueWorker` that:\n   - Polls `jobs` table for `pending` rows where `delay <= now`\n   - Locks row with `UPDATE ... IMPORTANT: Execute ONLY the selected approach "SQLite-First Event-Driven (Recommended)". Ignore other approaches in the plan.

## Approved Plan:
# Optimus Rufus — Event-Driven Refactoring Plan

## Objective
Transform the monolithic, synchronous, blocking-request MVP into a **token-isolated, event-driven, resumable, horizontally-scalable ecosystem** while preserving all existing business logic and frontend UX.

---

## Current State Diagnosis

| Dimension | Current | Target |
|-----------|---------|--------|
| **Pipeline Execution** | Synchronous 6-stage blocking HTTP mutation | Async background job with resumable stages |
| **State Storage** | In-memory `Map<string, PipelineState>` | Persistent `pipeline_jobs` + `pipeline_job_stages` tables |
| **Token/Cost Control** | None. Inline LLM calls with no tracking | Per-prospect token budget with circuit breaker |
| **Event System** | `EventEmitter` with zero production listeners | Typed domain event bus + job queue |
| **DB Integrity** | No FK enforcement, no indexes, no transactions | FKs ON, indexes on all FKs, atomic transactions |
| **Frontend Progress** | No real-time pipeline feedback | SSE stream + reactive stage progress |
| **External APIs** | Inline fetch with basic retry | Circuit breaker + cached responses |

---

## Architectural Decisions

### 1. Queue & Event Bus Abstraction
To support both **Vercel serverless** (no Redis) and **VPS/PM2** (Redis available), we introduce a `QueueAdapter` and `EventBusAdapter` interface with two implementations:

- **`SQLiteQueueAdapter`** — stores jobs in a new `job_queue` table with `status` (`pending`, `active`, `completed`, `failed`), `attempts`, `delay`, and `payload`. A `QueueWorker` polls the table every N seconds.
- **`BullMQQueueAdapter`** — wraps BullMQ for Redis-backed production deployments.

The active adapter is selected via `QUEUE_DRIVER=sqlite|bullmq` env var.

### 2. Token Isolation Layer (`TokenBudgetService`)
- Wraps **every** LLM invocation (OpenAI, OpenRouter, copywriter, Rufus simulator).
- Tracks `promptTokens`, `completionTokens`, `totalTokens`, `estimatedCost` per `prospectId` + `jobId`.
- Enforces per-prospect monthly caps by `packageType` tier:
  - Package 1: $5
  - Package 2: $15
  - Package 3: $30
  - Package 4: $50
- Emits `token-budget-exceeded` domain event when threshold hit.
- Circuit breaker: if 5 consecutive LLM errors occur within 60s, breaker opens for 120s.

### 3. Resumable Pipeline Engine (`PipelineEngine`)
Replaces `OptimizationOrchestrator`:
- Defines stages as a **DAG** (directed acyclic graph) instead of a hardcoded array.
- Stages 1→2→3→4→5→6 remain sequential where data-dependent, but independent branches (e.g., competitor fetch + embedding generation) run in parallel.
- After each stage completes, output is serialized to `pipeline_job_stages` table.
- On retry, the engine loads completed stages and resumes from the first failed stage.
- Emits typed events: `pipeline:start`, `stage:start`, `stage:complete`, `stage:error`, `pipeline:complete`, `pipeline:error`.

### 4. Database Hardening
- Enable `PRAGMA foreign_keys = ON` in `api/db/client.ts`.
- Add secondary indexes on all foreign key columns and query filters.
- Wrap multi-step mutations in `BEGIN...COMMIT/ROLLBACK` transactions.
- Add `pipeline_jobs`, `pipeline_job_stages`, `usage_events` tables.
- Add `jobs` table for SQLite queue implementation.

### 5. Async API Surface
- `agents.optimize` mutation → enqueues job, returns `{ jobId }` immediately.
- `agents.getStatus` query → returns current pipeline status + stage outputs.
- `agents.retryStage` mutation → enqueues retry job for specific stage.
- New SSE endpoint `/api/sse/pipeline/:jobId` streams events to frontend.

### 6. Frontend Adaptations
- `ProspectLanding` and `AdminDashboard` consume `agents.getStatus` polling + optional SSE.
- `StageScanAnimation` and `ProgressBar` bind to real pipeline stage events.
- Add `React.lazy` route splitting for `AdminDashboard` and `ProspectLanding`.
- Add React Error Boundary around stage components.

---

## Implementation Phases

### Phase 1: Foundation — Database Hardening & Schema Expansion
**Files:** `api/db/schema.ts`, `api/db/client.ts`, `api/db/migrations/`

1. Enable `foreign_keys = ON` in `client.ts`.
2. Create migration utility that runs numbered `.sql` files in order (replace silent `try/catch ALTER TABLE` anti-pattern).
3. Migration `001_add_indexes.sql`:
   - `idx_prospects_slug`, `idx_prospects_status`
   - `idx_listings_prospectId`
   - `idx_analyses_listingId`, `idx_analyses_prospectId`
   - `idx_bookings_prospectId`, `idx_activities_prospectId`
   - `idx_rufus_queries_prospectId`, `idx_catalog_links_prospectId`
4. Migration `002_add_pipeline_tables.sql`:
   - `pipeline_jobs`: `id`, `prospectId`, `listingId`, `packageType`, `status`, `currentStage`, `stagesJSON`, `tokenUsage`, `errorLog`, `createdAt`, `updatedAt`
   - `pipeline_job_stages`: `id`, `jobId`, `stageName`, `status`, `outputJSON`, `errorMessage`, `startedAt`, `completedAt`
   - `usage_events`: `id`, `prospectId`, `jobId`, `service`, `promptTokens`, `completionTokens`, `costCents`, `createdAt`
   - `jobs` (for SQLite queue): `id`, `queue`, `name`, `dataJSON`, `optsJSON`, `progress`, `delay`, `timestamp`, `attempts`, `maxAttempts`, `processedOn`, `finishedOn`, `returnValueJSON`, `failedReason`, `stacktraceJSON`
5. Wrap `client.ts` with a transaction helper: `withTransaction<T>(fn: (db: Database) => T): T`.

### Phase 2: Event Bus & Queue Infrastructure
**Files:** `api/infra/eventBus.ts`, `api/infra/queue.ts`, `api/infra/types.ts`

1. Define `EventBus` interface:
   ```ts
   emit<T>(event: string, payload: T): void
   on<T>(event: string, handler: (payload: T) => void): void
   ```
2. Implement `MemoryEventBus` (singleton EventEmitter wrapper) and `RedisEventBus`.
3. Define `JobQueue` interface:
   ```ts
   add(name: string, data: unknown, opts?: JobOpts): Promise<Job>
   getJob(id: string): Promise<Job | null>
   ```
4. Implement `SQLiteJobQueue` with polling worker (`QueueWorker` class).
5. Implement `BullMQJobQueue` wrapper.
6. Add `QueueWorker` that:
   - Polls `jobs` table for `pending` rows where `delay <= now`
   - Locks row with `UPDATE ... SET status = 'active'`
   - Dispatches to registered processor functions
   - On success: writes `returnValueJSON`, `finishedOn`
   - On failure: increments `attempts`, writes `failedReason`, re-queues if `attempts < maxAttempts`

### Phase 3: Token Isolation & Circuit Breaker Layer
**Files:** `api/services/tokenBudget.ts`, `api/services/circuitBreaker.ts`, `api/services/llmGateway.ts`

1. `CircuitBreaker` class:
   - States: `closed`, `open`, `half-open`
   - Config: `failureThreshold`, `recoveryTimeout`, `monitoringPeriod`
   - Wraps any async function.
2. `TokenBudgetService`:
   - `trackUsage(prospectId, jobId, service, promptTokens, completionTokens)` → inserts `usage_events`
   - `getRemainingBudget(prospectId)` → sums usage_events for current month, subtracts from tier cap
   - `checkBudget(prospectId, estimatedCost)` → throws `TokenBudgetExceededError` if over cap
3. `LlmGateway`:
   - Wraps all OpenAI/OpenRouter fetch calls
   - Pre-call: `tokenBudgetService.checkBudget()`
   - Post-call: `tokenBudgetService.trackUsage()` with actual token counts from response headers
   - Wraps fetch with `CircuitBreaker`
   - Emits `llm:request`, `llm:success`, `llm:error`, `llm:circuit-open` events
4. Refactor `copywriter.ts`, `rufusSimulator.ts`, `scripts/runOptimization.ts` to use `LlmGateway`.

### Phase 4: Resumable Pipeline Engine
**Files:** `api/pipeline/engine.ts`, `api/pipeline/stages.ts`, `api/pipeline/types.ts`

1. Define `PipelineStage` interface:
   ```ts
   interface PipelineStage {
     name: string;
     dependencies: string[];
     execute(input: StageInput): Promise<StageOutput>;
   }
   ```
2. Implement `PipelineEngine`:
   - `createJob(prospectId, listingId, packageType)` → inserts `pipeline_jobs` row with status `pending`
   - `runJob(jobId)` → loads `pipeline_job_stages`, finds first uncompleted stage whose dependencies are satisfied, executes it, persists output, recurses.
   - `retryStage(jobId, stageName)` → resets that stage to `pending`, re-runs.
   - Emits events at each lifecycle point.
3. Port existing agent logic into stage executors:
   - `ApifyFetcherStage`
   - `PreprocessorStage`
   - `EmbeddingGeneratorStage` (still stubbed, but wrapped in stage contract)
   - `SemanticAnalyzerStage`
   - `ContentOptimizerStage`
   - `CompetitorAnalystStage`
4. `ReviewerAgent` runs after each stage as a validation decorator (non-blocking, emits `review:warning` events).

### Phase 5: Async API Routers + SSE Streaming
**Files:** `api/routers/agents.ts`, `api/routers/pipeline.ts`, `api/boot.ts`, `api/sse/pipeline.ts`

1. Refactor `agentsRouter`:
   - `optimize` → calls `pipelineEngine.createJob()` + `queue.add('pipeline', { jobId })`, returns `{ jobId }`
   - `getStatus` → queries `pipeline_jobs` + `pipeline_job_stages`
   - `retryStage` → validates stage exists, enqueues retry job
2. Add `pipelineRouter` (or extend `agentsRouter`) with SSE endpoint:
   - `GET /api/sse/pipeline/:jobId`
   - Uses `MemoryEventBus` (or Redis) to subscribe to `stage:*` events for that jobId
   - Sends `text/event-stream` formatted messages
   - Closes stream when `pipeline:complete` or `pipeline:error` received
3. Update `api/router.ts` to register new routers.

### Phase 6: Frontend Integration
**Files:** `src/hooks/usePipeline.ts`, `src/pages/ProspectLanding.tsx`, `src/pages/AdminDashboard.tsx`

1. Create `usePipeline(jobId)` hook:
   - Queries `agents.getStatus` on interval (5s fallback)
   - If `EventSource` available, opens SSE to `/api/sse/pipeline/:jobId`
   - Merges polling + SSE into unified `PipelineState` object
2. Update `ProspectLanding.tsx`:
   - On scan complete, call `optimize` mutation → receive `jobId` → feed to `usePipeline`
   - Replace manual `scanComplete` timeout with real stage progress
3. Update `AdminDashboard.tsx`:
   - Launch audit → enqueue job, show job status in detail panel
   - Add "Retry Stage" button for failed stages
4. Add `React.lazy` + `Suspense` for route-level code splitting.
5. Add Error Boundary component.

### Phase 7: Caching & Performance
**Files:** `api/services/cache.ts`, `api/services/scraper.ts`, `api/services/embedding.ts`

1. Implement `CacheService` with `get(key)`, `set(key, value, ttl)` backed by in-memory LRU or Redis.
2. Cache scraped listings by ASIN (TTL 1 hour).
3. Cache embeddings by text hash (TTL 24 hours).
4. Cache generated PDFs by slug (TTL 1 hour).
5. Add `Cache-Control` headers to static assets in `boot.ts`.

### Phase 8: Cleanup & Observability
**Files:** `api/infra/logger.ts`, `api/boot.ts`

1. Replace `console.log` with structured `Logger` (Pino or lightweight JSON logger).
2. Add correlation IDs to all requests (tRPC context + HTTP headers).
3. Propagate correlation ID through job queue payloads.
4. Add `/health` DB connectivity check.
5. Remove hardcoded mock data from `prospects.ts`, `competitor.ts`.
6. Fix `dangerouslySetInnerHTML` brand injection in frontend.

---

## Rollback Strategy
Each phase is designed to be **backward-compatible**:
- Existing `analysis.run` and `agents.optimize` mutations can be preserved as deprecated aliases during transition.
- New tables are additive; old queries still work.
- The old `OptimizationOrchestrator` remains in `api/agents/orchestrator.ts` until Phase 6 is complete, then deleted.
