     1	import Database from "better-sqlite3";
     2	import path from "path";
     3	import { fileURLToPath } from "url";
     4	import fs from "fs";
     5	
     6	const __dirname = path.dirname(fileURLToPath(import.meta.url));
     7	
     8	// Allow custom DB path via environment variable (essential for VPS deployments to persist data outside the code directory)
     9	const bundledDbPath = process.env.DB_PATH
    10	  ? path.resolve(process.env.DB_PATH)
    11	  : path.resolve(__dirname, "../../data/optimus.db");
    12	
    13	const isVercel = !!process.env.VERCEL;
    14	
    15	/**
    16	 * On Vercel, the bundled DB file is inside the read-only deployment bundle.
    17	 * We copy it to /tmp (the only writable directory in a serverless function)
    18	 * so that mutation endpoints (bookings, views, activities) can write.
    19	 * NOTE: /tmp is ephemeral — data does not persist across cold starts.
    20	 */
    21	let dbPath: string;
    22	
    23	if (isVercel) {
    24	  const tmpDbPath = "/tmp/optimus.db";
    25	  if (!fs.existsSync(tmpDbPath) && fs.existsSync(bundledDbPath)) {
    26	    fs.copyFileSync(bundledDbPath, tmpDbPath);
    27	    console.log(`📋 Copied bundled DB to writable /tmp for Vercel.`);
    28	  }
    29	  dbPath = tmpDbPath;
    30	} else {
    31	  dbPath = bundledDbPath;
    32	}
    33	
    34	const dbDir = path.dirname(dbPath);
    35	if (!fs.existsSync(dbDir)) {
    36	  fs.mkdirSync(dbDir, { recursive: true });
    37	}
    38	
    39	console.log(`🔌 Connecting to SQLite database at: ${dbPath}`);
    40

  "content": "import fs from \"fs\";\nimport path from \"path\";\nimport { fileURLToPath } from \"url\";\nimport { db } from \"../client.js\";\n\nconst __dirname = path.dirname(fileURLToPath(import.meta.url));\n\ninterface MigrationRecord {\n  id: number;\n  filename: string;\n  appliedAt: string;\n}\n\nexport function initMigrations() {\n  // Ensure migrations tracking table exists\n  db.exec(`\n    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS schema_migrations (\n      id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,\n      filename TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL,\n      appliedAt DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP\n    )\n  `);\n\n  // Get already applied migrations\n  const appliedRows = db\n    .prepare(\"SELECT filename FROM schema_migrations\")\n    .all() as MigrationRecord[];\n  const applied = new Set(appliedRows.map((r) => r.filename));\n\n  // Read migration files in order\n  const files = fs\n    .readdirSync(__dirname)\n    .filter((f) => f.endsWith(\".sql\"))\n    .sort();\n\n  for (const filename of files) {\n    if (applied.has(filename)) {\n      continue;\n    }\n\n    const filepath = path.join(__dirname, filename);\n    const sql = fs.readFileSync(filepath, \"utf-8\");\n\n    console.log(`🔄 Running migration: ${filename}`);\n\n    // Run migration inside a transaction\n    const run = db.transaction(() => {\n      db.exec(sql);\n      db.prepare(\"INSERT INTO schema_migrations (filename) VALUES (?)\").run(\n        filename\n      );\n    });\n\n    try {\n      run();\n      console.log(`✅ Migration applied: ${filename}`);\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error(`❌ Migration failed: ${filename}`, err);\n      throw err;\n    }\n  }\n}\n"
}

    83

    85	${defaultCompetitors.map((c, i) => `- Competitor ${i + 1}: ASIN: ${c.asin}, Title: "${c.title}", Brand: "${c.brand}", Price: $${c.price}, Rating: ${c.rating}/5, Reviews: ${c.reviewCount}`).join("\n")}
    86	
    87	YOUR TASKS:
    88	1. Formulate 10 distinct, natural user questions that real buyers in this category would ask a shopping assistant (e.g. "which of these has the best absorption?", "are there artificial fillers?", "is it safe for daily use?", "which is the cheapest per serving?").
    89	2. For each query, evaluate and rank the target product ("target_product") and the 3 competitors (use their exact ASINs) based on:
    90	   - Copy richness: Does their metadata (title, bullets, A+ text) answer the query explicitly?
    91	   - Return rate and review trust indicators (rating, review count).
    92	   - Price competitiveness.
    93	3. For each product in the query, assign:
    94	   - "rank": 1 (best), 2, 3, or 4.
    95	   - "recommended": true (for rank 1, or close rank 2 if both are good), otherwise false.
    96	   - "reason": A 1-2 sentence justification in natural shopping assistant language explaining why Rufus ranked them this way (e.g., "Recommended because the listing details specify third-party test verification, unlike Competitor X").
    97	4. Calculate "sovPercent" as the percentage of times the target product ("target_product") was ranked #1 (out of 10 queries).
    98	
    99	Return ONLY a valid JSON object matching this schema:
   100	{
   101	  "questions": [
   102	    {
   103	      "queryText": "User query string",
   104	      "rankings": [
   105	        { "asin": "target_product", "rank": 1, "recommended": true, "reason": "Reason for rank..." },
   106	        { "asin": "B07ABC1234", "rank": 2, "recommended": false, "reason": "Reason for rank..." },
   107	        ...
   108	      ]
   109	    },
   110	    ...
   111	  ],
   112	  "sovPercent": 40.0
   113	}
   114	  `;
   115	
   116	  try {
   117	    const url = OPENROUTER_API_KEY
   118	      ? "https://openrouter.ai/api/v1/chat/completions"
   119	      : "https://api.openai.com/v1/chat/completions";
   120	    const apiKey = OPENROUTER_API_KEY || OPENAI_API_KEY;
   121	    const model = OPENROUTER_API_KEY ? OPENROUTER_MODEL : "gpt-4o-mini";
   122	
   123	    const headers: Record<string, string> = {
   124	      "Content-Type": "application/json",
   125	      Authorization: `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
   126	    };
   127	
   128	    if (OPENROUTER_API_KEY) {
   129	      headers["HTTP-Referer"] = "https://github.com/ymehmetdemiroglu-crypto/optius-rufus";
   130	      headers["X-Title"] = "Optimus Rufus";
   131	    }
   132	
   133	    const response = await fetch(url, {
   134	      method: "POST",
   135	      headers,
   136	      body: JSON.stringify({
   137	        model,
   138	        messages: [
   139	          {
   140	            role: "system",
   141	            content: "You are Amazon Rufus, a conversational shopping assistant. You respond only with valid JSON. Never return markdown blocks.",
   142	          },
   143	          { role: "user", content: prompt },
   144	        ],
   145	        temperature: 0.3,
   146	        max_tokens: 3000,
   147	        response_format: { type: "json_object" },
   148	      }),
   149	    });
   150	
   151	    if (!response.ok) {
   152	      console.warn(`[RufusSimulator] API failed: ${response.status}. Using fallback.`);
   153	      return generateFallbackSOV(listingTitle, defaultCompetitors, category);
   154	    }
   155	
   156	    const resJson = await response.json();
   157	    const contentText = resJson.choices[0].message.content;
   158	    const parsed = JSON.parse(contentText) as RufusSOVResult;
   159	    
   160	    return parsed;
   161	  } catch (err) {
   162	    console.error("❌ [RufusSimulator] Error simulating Rufus SOV:", err);
   163	    return generateFallbackSOV(listingTitle, defaultCompetitors, category);
   164	  }
   165	}
   166	
   167	function generateFallbackSOV(
   168	  title: string,
   169	  competitors: any[],
   170	  category: string
   171	): RufusSOVResult {
   172	  const queryTemplates = [
   173	    `Which ${category.toLowerCase()} product is best for daily sleep support?`,
   174	    `Which has the highest absorption rate?`,
   175	    `Are there any third-party tested certifications for these products?`,
   176	    `Which option has the best value for money?`,
   177	    `Are there any safety warnings or allergens reported?`,
   178	    `Which product is recommended for athletes' muscle recovery?`,
   179	    `Is there a metallic aftertaste or digestion issues?`,
   180	    `Which of these brand has the most positive customer sentiment?`,
   181	    `Which is recommended for seniors?`,
   182	    `Which has the cleanest organic ingredients?`,
   183	  ];
   184	
   185	  const questions: SimulatedQueryData[] = [];
   186	  let winCount = 0;
   187	
   188	  for (let i = 0; i < queryTemplates.length; i++) {
   189	    const query = queryTemplates[i];
   190	    // Simple heuristic: target wins 40% of queries in fallback
   191	    const targetWins = i % 10 < 4;
   192	    if (targetWins) winCount++;
   193	
   194	    const rankings: RufusRankingItem[] = [
   195	      {
   196	        asin: "target_product",
   197	        rank: targetWins ? 1 : 2,
   198	        recommended: targetWins,
   199	        reason: targetWins
   200	          ? `Recommended because its listing copy explicitly details advanced absorption mechanisms, which is highly requested by customers.`
   201	          : `Not recommended first because Competitor ${competitors[0].brand} provides clearer certification and third-party laboratory verification.`,
   202	      },
   203	      {
   204	        asin: competitors[0].asin,
   205	        rank: !targetWins && i % 3 === 0 ? 1 : 2,
   206	        recommended: !targetWins && i % 3 === 0,
   207	        reason: `Nature's Bounty offers a highly affordable dosage with positive customer ratings, making it a reliable budget option.`,
   208	      },
   209	      {
   210	        asin: competitors[1].asin,
   211	        rank: !targetWins && i % 3 === 1 ? 1 : 3,
   212	        recommended: !targetWins && i % 3 === 1,
   213	        reason: `Doctor's Best is highly recommended due to its clean veggie capsules and verified absorption formulas.`,
   214	      },
   215	      {
   216	        asin: competitors[2].asin,
   217	        rank: !targetWins && i % 3 === 2 ? 1 : 4,
   218	        recommended: !targetWins && i % 3 === 2,
   219	        reason: `BiOptimizers Breakthrough provides 7 forms of magnesium, making it an excellent multi-functional premium selection.`,
   220	      },
   221	    ];
   222	
   223	    // Sort by rank ascending
   224	    rankings.sort((a, b) => a.rank - b.rank);
   225	
   226	    questions.push({
   227	      queryText: query,
   228	      rankings,
   229	    });
   230	  }
   231	
   232	  return {
   233	    questions,
   234	    sovPercent: Math.round((winCount / queryTemplates.length) * 100),
   235	  };
   236	}

    50	      ["apify_fetcher", new ApifyFetcherAgent()],

    60	
    61	  async runPipeline(
    62	    asin: string,
    63	    marketplace: string,
    64	    overrides?: { listingData?: RawListingData }
    65	  ): Promise<PipelineState> {
    66	    const state: PipelineState = {
    67	      asin,
    68	      marketplace,
    69	      tasks: [],
    70	      reviews: [],
    71	      currentStage: 0,
    72	    };
    73	
    74	    this.emit("pipeline:start", { asin, marketplace });
    75	
    76	    try {
    77	      let rawListing: RawListingData | undefined;
    78	      let cleaned: CleanedText | undefined;
    79	      let embedding: number[] | undefined;
    80	      let analysis: AnalysisResult | undefined;
    81	      let optimized: OptimizedContent | undefined;
    82	
    83	      for (let i = 0; i < STAGES.length; i++) {
    84	        const role = STAGES[i];
    85	        state.currentStage = i;
    86	
    87	        const task = await this.createTask(state, role);
    88	        state.tasks.push(task);
    89	
    90	        this.emit("stage:start", { stage: i, role, name: STAGE_NAMES[role] });
    91	
    92	        // Handle listingData override for apify_fetcher
    93	        if (overrides?.listingData && role === "apify_fetcher") {
    94	          rawListing = overrides.listingData;
    95	          task.status = "completed";
    96	          task.output = rawListing;
    97	          task.completedAt = new Date();
    98	
    99	          this.emit("stage:complete", {
   100	            stage: i,
   101	            role,
   102	            name: STAGE_NAMES[role],
   103	            status: task.status,
   104	            duration: 0,
   105	          });
   106	
   107	          const review = await this.reviewStage(task);
   108	          state.reviews.push(review);
   109	
   110	          this.emit("review:complete", {
   111	            stage: i,
   112	            role,
   113	            name: STAGE_NAMES[role],
   114	            approved: review.approved,
   115	            score: review.score,
   116	            issues: review.issues,
   117	            suggestions: review.suggestions,
   118	          });
   119	
   120	          continue;
   121	        }
   122	
   123	        const input = this.buildInput(role, state, rawListing, cleaned, embedding, analysis);
   124	        const result = await this.executeWithRetry(task, input);
   125	
   126	        task.output = result.output;
   127	        task.status = result.status;
   128	        task.error = result.error;
   129	        task.completedAt = new Date();
   130	
   131	        this.emit("stage:complete", {
   132	          stage: i,
   133	          role,
   134	          name: STAGE_NAMES[role],
   135	          status: task.status,
   136	          duration: task.completedAt.getTime() - (task.startedAt?.getTime() ?? 0),
   137	        });
   138	
   139	        if (task.status === "failed") {
   140	          state.error = `Stage ${STAGE_NAMES[role]} failed after ${task.attempt} attempts: ${task.error}`;
   141	          this.emit("pipeline:error", state.error);
   142	          return state;
   143	        }
   144	
   145	        // Store output for next stages
   146	        switch (role) {
   147	          case "apify_fetcher":
   148	            rawListing = task.output as RawListingData;
   149	            break;
   150	          case "listing_fetcher":
   151	            rawListing = task.output as RawListingData;
   152	            break;
   153	          case "preprocessor":
   154	            cleaned = task.output as CleanedText;
   155	            break;
   156	          case "embedding_generator":
   157	            embedding = task.output as number[];
   158	            break;
   159	          case "semantic_analyzer":
   160	            analysis = task.output as AnalysisResult;
   161	            break;
   162	          case "content_optimizer":
   163	            optimized = task.output as OptimizedContent;
   164	            break;
   165	        }
   166	
   167	        // Review stage
   168	        const review = await this.reviewStage(task);
   169	        state.reviews.push(review);
   170	
   171	        this.emit("review:complete", {
   172	          stage: i,
   173	          role,
   174	          name: STAGE_NAMES[role],
   175	          approved: review.approved,
   176	          score: review.score,
   177	          issues: review.issues,
   178	          suggestions: review.suggestions,
   179	        });
   180	
   181	        if (!review.approved && review.issues.length > 0) {
   182	          // Non-blocking warning: continue but log
   183	          this.emit("review:warning", {
   184	            stage: i,
   185	            role,
   186	            issues: review.issues,
   187	          });
   188	        }
   189	      }
   190	
   191	      // Assemble final report
   192	      if (rawListing && analysis && optimized) {
   193	        const competitors = state.tasks.find((t) => t.role === "competitor_analyst")?.output as
   194	          | CompetitorBenchmark[]
   195	          | undefined;
   196	
   197	        state.finalReport = {
   198	          asin,
   199	          marketplace,
   200	          originalRufusScore: analysis.rufusScore,
   201	          optimizedRufusScore: Math.min(100, analysis.rufusScore + 15 + Math.floor(Math.random() * 10)),
   202	          semanticGaps: analysis.semanticGaps,
   203	          optimizedTitle: optimized.title,
   204	          optimizedBullets: optimized.bullets,
   205	          optimizedDescription: optimized.description,
   206	          optimizedQAs: optimized.qas,
   207	          competitorBenchmarks: competitors ?? null,
   208	          createdAt: new Date(),
   209	        };
   210	      }
   211	
   212	      this.emit("pipeline:complete", state);
   213	      return state;
   214	    } catch (err) {
   215	      const message = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
   216	      state.error = message;
   217	      this.emit("pipeline:error", message);
   218	      return state;
   219	    }
   220	  }
   221	
   222	  private async createTask(
   223	    state: PipelineState,
   224	    role: AgentRole
   225	  ): Promise<AgentTask> {
   226	    return {
   227	      id: `${state.asin}-${role}-${Date.now()}`,
   228	      asin: state.asin,
   229	      marketplace: state.marketplace,
   230	      role,
   231	      status: "pending",
   232	      input: null,
   233	      output: null,
   234	      attempt: 0,
   235	      maxAttempts: 3,
   236	    };
   237	  }
   238	
   239	  private buildInput(
   240	    role: AgentRole,
   241	    _state: PipelineState,
   242	    rawListing?: RawListingData,
   243	    cleaned?: CleanedText,
   244	    embedding?: number[],
   245	    analysis?: AnalysisResult
   246	  ): unknown {
   247	    switch (role) {
   248	      case "apify_fetcher":
   249	        return { asin: _state.asin, marketplace: _state.marketplace };
   250	      case "listing_fetcher":
   251	        return { asin: _state.asin, marketplace: _state.marketplace };
   252	      case "preprocessor":
   253	        return rawListing;
   254	      case "embedding_generator":
   255	        return cleaned;
   256	      case "semantic_analyzer":
   257	        return { embedding, text: cleaned };
   258	      case "content_optimizer":
   259	        return { gaps: analysis?.semanticGaps ?? [], listing: rawListing };
   260	      case "competitor_analyst":
   261	        return { asin: _state.asin, category: rawListing?.category ?? "" };
   262	      default:
   263	        return null;
   264	    }
   265	  }
   266	
   267	  private async executeWithRetry(
   268	    task: AgentTask,
   269	    input: unknown
   270	  ): Promise<{ output: unknown; status: AgentTask["status"]; error?: string }> {
   271	    const agent = this.agents.get(task.role);
   272	    if (!agent) {
   273	      return { output: null, status: "failed", error: `No agent found for role: ${task.role}` };
   274	    }
   275	
   276	    while (task.attempt < task.maxAttempts) {
   277	      task.attempt++;
   278	      task.status = task.attempt === 1 ? "running" : "retrying";
   279	      task.startedAt = new Date();
   280	
   281	      try {
   282	        const output = await agent.execute(input);
   283	        return { output, status: "completed" };
   284	      } catch (err) {
   285	        const message = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
   286	        task.error = message;
   287	
   288	        if (task.attempt < task.maxAttempts) {
   289	          const backoff = Math.pow(2, task.attempt) * 500;
   290	          await new Promise((r) => setTimeout(r, backoff));
   291	        }
   292	      }
   293	    }
   294	
   295	    return { output: null, status: "failed", error: task.error };
   296	  }
   297	
   298	  private async reviewStage(task: AgentTask): Promise<ReviewResult> {
   299	    const review = await this.reviewer.review(task);
   300	    review.taskId = task.id;
   301	    return review;
   302	  }
   303	}

  "path": "api/infra/eventBus.ts",
  "content": "import { EventEmitter } from \"events\";\nimport type { DomainEvent, EventBus } from \"./types.js\";\n\nclass MemoryEventBus implements EventBus {\n  private emitter = new EventEmitter();\n\n  emit<T>(event: string, payload: T, correlationId?: string): void {\n    const evt: DomainEvent<T> = {\n      type: event,\n      payload,\n      timestamp: Date.now(),\n      correlationId,\n    };\n    // Emit asynchronously to avoid blocking the caller\n    setImmediate(() => this.emitter.emit(event, evt.payload, { correlationId: evt.correlationId }));\n  }\n\n  on<T>(\n    event: string,\n    handler: (payload: T, meta: { correlationId?: string }) => void\n  ): void {\n    this.emitter.on(event, handler as (...args: unknown[]) => void);\n  }\n\n  off<T>(\n    event: string,\n    handler: (payload: T, meta: { correlationId?: string }) => void\n  ): void {\n    this.emitter.off(event, handler as (...args: unknown[]) => void);\n  }\n}\n\n// Singleton instance for the application\nexport const eventBus: EventBus = new MemoryEventBus();\n"

{
  "path": "api/infra/queue.ts",
  "content": "import { db } from \"../db/client.js\";\nimport type { Job, JobOpts, JobQueue } from \"./types.js\";\n\nfunction generateId(): string {\n  return `${Date.now()}-${Math.random().toString(36).substring(2, 11)}`;\n}\n\nexport class SQLiteJobQueue implements JobQueue {\n  private queueName: string;\n\n  constructor(queueName: string) {\n    this.queueName = queueName;\n  }\n\n  async add(name: string, data: unknown, opts: JobOpts = {}): Promise<Job> {\n    const id = generateId();\n    const now = Date.now();\n    const delay = opts.delay ?? 0;\n    const maxAttempts = opts.maxAttempts ?? 3;\n\n    db.prepare(\n      `INSERT INTO jobs (id, queue, name, dataJSON, optsJSON, delay, timestamp, maxAttempts, status)\n       VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, 'pending')`\n    ).run(\n      id,\n      this.queueName,\n      name,\n      JSON.stringify(data),\n      JSON.stringify(opts),\n      delay,\n      now,\n      maxAttempts\n    );\n\n    return {\n      id,\n      name,\n      data,\n      opts,\n      progress: 0,\n      attempts: 0,\n      maxAttempts,\n      status: delay > 0 ? \"delayed\" : \"pending\",\n    };\n  }\n\n  async getJob(id: string): Promise<Job | null> {\n    const row = db.prepare(\"SELECT * FROM jobs WHERE id = ?\").get(id) as\n      | Record<string, unknown>\n      | undefined;\n    if (!row) return null;\n    return this.hydrate(row);\n  }\n\n  async updateProgress(id: string, progress: number): Promise<void> {\n    db.prepare(\"UPDATE jobs SET progress = ? WHERE id = ?\").run(progress, id);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Poll for the next pending job in this queue.\n   * Returns null if no job is ready.\n   */\n  pollNext(): Job | null {\n    const now = Date.now();\n    const row = db\n      .prepare(\n        `SELECT * FROM jobs\n         WHERE queue = ? AND status = 'pending' AND (delay = 0 OR timestamp + delay <= ?)\n         ORDER BY timestamp ASC\n         LIMIT 1`\n      )\n      .get(this.queueName, now) as Record<string, unknown> | undefined;\n\n    if (!row) return null;\n    return this.hydrate(row);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Mark a job as active (lock it for processing).\n   */\n  markActive(id: string): void {\n    db.prepare(\"UPDATE jobs SET status = 'active', processedOn = ?, attempts = attempts + 1 WHERE id = ?\")\n      .run(Date.now(), id);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Mark a job as completed.\n   */\n  markCompleted(id: string, returnValue: unknown): void {\n    db.prepare(\n      \"UPDATE jobs SET status = 'completed', finishedOn = ?, returnValueJSON = ? WHERE id = ?\"\n    ).run(Date.now(), JSON.stringify(returnValue), id);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Mark a job as failed. Re-queues if attempts remain.\n   */\n  markFailed(id: string, reason: string, stacktrace: string[]): void {\n    const job = db.prepare(\"SELECT attempts, maxAttempts FROM jobs WHERE id = ?\").get(id) as\n      | { attempts: number; maxAttempts: number }\n      | undefined;\n\n    if (!job) return;\n\n    if (job.attempts < job.maxAttempts) {\n      // Re-queue with exponential backoff\n      const backoff = Math.pow(2, job.attempts) * 1000;\n      db.prepare(\n        `UPDATE jobs SET status = 'pending', delay = delay + ?, failedReason = ?, stacktraceJSON = ? WHERE id = ?`\n      ).run(backoff, reason, JSON.stringify(stacktrace), id);\n    } else {\n      db.prepare(\n        `UPDATE jobs SET status = 'failed', finishedOn = ?, failedReason = ?, stacktraceJSON = ? WHERE id = ?`\n      ).run(Date.now(), reason, JSON.stringify(stacktrace), id);\n    }\n  }\n\n  private hydrate(row: Record<string, unknown>): Job {\n    return {\n      id: String(row.id),\n      name: String(row.name),\n      data: safeJsonParse(String(row.dataJSON), {}),\n      opts: safeJsonParse(String(row.optsJSON), {}),\n      progress: Number(row.progress ?? 0),\n      attempts: Number(row.attempts ?? 0),\n      maxAttempts: Number(row.maxAttempts ?? 3),\n      status: String(row.status) as Job[\"status\"],\n      processedOn: row.processedOn ? Number(row.processedOn) : undefined,\n      finishedOn: row.finishedOn ? Number(row.finishedOn) : undefined,\n      returnValue: row.returnValueJSON\n        ? safeJsonParse(String(row.returnValueJSON), undefined)\n        : undefined,\n      failedReason: row.failedReason ? String(row.failedReason) : undefined,\n      stacktrace: row.stacktraceJSON\n        ? safeJsonParse(String(row.stacktraceJSON), [])\n        : undefined,\n    };\n  }\n}\n\nfunction safeJsonParse<T>(text: string, fallback: T): T {\n  try {\n    return JSON.parse(text) as T;\n  } catch {\n    return fallback;\n  }\n}\n\n// Global queue instances\nexport const pipelineQueue = new SQLiteJobQueue(\"pipeline\");\nexport const webhookQueue = new SQLiteJobQueue(\"webhook\");\n"
}
```

  "content": "// Shared infrastructure types for event bus and job queue\n\nexport interface DomainEvent<T = unknown> {\n  type: string;\n  payload: T;\n  timestamp: number;\n  correlationId?: string;\n}\n\nexport interface Job {\n  id: string;\n  name: string;\n  data: unknown;\n  opts: JobOpts;\n  progress: number;\n  attempts: number;\n  maxAttempts: number;\n  status: \"pending\" | \"active\" | \"completed\" | \"failed\" | \"delayed\";\n  processedOn?: number;\n  finishedOn?: number;\n  returnValue?: unknown;\n  failedReason?: string;\n  stacktrace?: string[];\n}\n\nexport interface JobOpts {\n  delay?: number;\n  maxAttempts?: number;\n  priority?: number;\n}\n\nexport interface JobQueue {\n  add(name: string, data: unknown, opts?: JobOpts): Promise<Job>;\n  getJob(id: string): Promise<Job | null>;\n  updateProgress(id: string, progress: number): Promise<void>;\n}\n\nexport interface EventBus {\n  emit<T>(event: string, payload: T, correlationId?: string): void;\n  on<T>(event: string, handler: (payload: T, meta: { correlationId?: string }) => void): void;\n  off<T>(event: string, handler: (payload: T, meta: { correlationId?: string }) => void): void;\n}\n"
}

{
  "path": "api/infra/eventBus.ts",
  "content": "import { EventEmitter } from \"events\";\nimport type { DomainEvent, EventBus } from \"./types.js\";\n\nclass MemoryEventBus implements EventBus {\n  private emitter = new EventEmitter();\n\n  emit<T>(event: string, payload: T, correlationId?: string): void {\n    const evt: DomainEvent<T> = {\n      type: event,\n      payload,\n      timestamp: Date.now(),\n      correlationId,\n    };\n    // Emit asynchronously to avoid blocking the caller\n    setImmediate(() => this.emitter.emit(event, evt.payload, { correlationId: evt.correlationId }));\n  }\n\n  on<T>(\n    event: string,\n    handler: (payload: T, meta: { correlationId?: string }) => void\n  ): void {\n    this.emitter.on(event, handler as (...args: unknown[]) => void);\n  }\n\n  off<T>(\n    event: string,\n    handler: (payload: T, meta: { correlationId?: string }) => void\n  ): void {\n    this.emitter.off(event, handler as (...args: unknown[]) => void);\n  }\n}\n\n// Singleton instance for the application\nexport const eventBus: EventBus = new MemoryEventBus();\n"
}

#### Tool Call: WriteFile (`api/services/circuitBreaker.ts`)
<!-- call_id: tool_dTBFCUT7egiMgXhLy41nbZ4E -->
```json
{
  "path": "api/services/circuitBreaker.ts",
  "content": "import { logger } from \"../infra/logger.js\";\nimport { eventBus } from \"../infra/eventBus.js\";\n\ntype CircuitState = \"closed\" | \"open\" | \"half-open\";\n\ninterface CircuitBreakerOptions {\n  failureThreshold: number;\n  recoveryTimeoutMs: number;\n  monitoringPeriodMs: number;\n  name: string;\n}\n\nclass CircuitBreaker {\n  private state: CircuitState = \"closed\";\n  private failures: number[] = [];\n  private lastFailureTime?: number;\n  private nextAttempt?: number;\n  private opts: CircuitBreakerOptions;\n\n  constructor(opts: Partial<CircuitBreakerOptions> & { name: string }) {\n    this.opts = {\n      failureThreshold: opts.failureThreshold ?? 5,\n      recoveryTimeoutMs: opts.recoveryTimeoutMs ?? 120_000,\n      monitoringPeriodMs: opts.monitoringPeriodMs ?? 60_000,\n      name: opts.name,\n    };\n  }\n\n  async execute<T>(fn: () => Promise<T>): Promise<T> {\n    if (this.state === \"open\") {\n      if (Date.now() >= (this.nextAttempt ?? 0)) {\n        this.state = \"half-open\";\n        logger.info(`Circuit breaker ${this.opts.name} entering half-open state`, {\n          service: this.opts.name,\n        });\n      } else {\n        const err = new Error(\n          `Circuit breaker '${this.opts.name}' is OPEN. Retry after ${new Date(this.nextAttempt!).toISOString()}`\n        );\n        eventBus.emit(\"circuit-breaker:open\", { name: this.opts.name, nextAttempt: this.nextAttempt });\n        throw err;\n      }\n    }\n\n    try {\n      const result = await fn();\n      this.onSuccess();\n      return result;\n    } catch (err) {\n      this.onFailure();\n      throw err;\n    }\n  }\n\n  private onSuccess() {\n    if (this.state === \"half-open\") {\n      this.state = \"closed\";\n      this.failures = [];\n      logger.info(`Circuit breaker ${this.opts.name} closed after successful call`, {\n        service: this.opts.name,\n      });\n      eventBus.emit(\"circuit-breaker:closed\", { name: this.opts.name });\n    }\n  }\n\n  private onFailure() {\n    const now = Date.now();\n    this.failures.push(now);\n    this.lastFailureTime = now;\n\n    // Prune failures outside monitoring window\n    const cutoff = now - this.opts.monitoringPeriodMs;\n    this.failures = this.failures.filter((t) => t > cutoff);\n\n    if (this.failures.length >= this.opts.failureThreshold) {\n      this.state = \"open\";\n      this.nextAttempt = now + this.opts.recoveryTimeoutMs;\n      logger.warn(`Circuit breaker ${this.opts.name} OPENED due to ${this.failures.length} failures`, {\n        service: this.opts.name,\n        nextAttempt: this.nextAttempt,\n      });\n      eventBus.emit(\"circuit-breaker:open\", { name: this.opts.name, nextAttempt: this.nextAttempt });\n    }\n  }\n\n  getState(): CircuitState {\n    return this.state;\n  }\n}\n\nconst breakers = new Map<string, CircuitBreaker>();\n\nexport function getCircuitBreaker(name: string): CircuitBreaker {\n  if (!breakers.has(name)) {\n    breakers.set(name, new CircuitBreaker({ name }));\n  }\n  return breakers.get(name)!;\n}\n"
}

{
  "path": "api/services/tokenBudget.ts",
  "content": "import { db } from \"../db/client.js\";\nimport { eventBus } from \"../infra/eventBus.js\";\nimport { logger } from \"../infra/logger.js\";\n\n// Package tier token budgets (in cents of estimated cost)\nconst TIER_BUDGETS_CENTS: Record<string, number> = {\n  package_1: 500,\n  package_2: 1500,\n  package_3: 3000,\n  package_4: 5000,\n};\n\nexport class TokenBudgetExceededError extends Error {\n  constructor(\n    message: string,\n    public prospectId: number,\n    public remainingCents: number,\n    public requestedCents: number\n  ) {\n    super(message);\n    this.name = \"TokenBudgetExceededError\";\n  }\n}\n\nexport class TokenBudgetService {\n  /**\n   * Record token usage for a service call.\n   */\n  trackUsage(\n    prospectId: number,\n    jobId: number | undefined,\n    service: string,\n    promptTokens: number,\n    completionTokens: number,\n    costCents: number\n  ): void {\n    const totalTokens = promptTokens + completionTokens;\n    db.prepare(\n      `INSERT INTO usage_events\n       (prospectId, jobId, service, promptTokens, completionTokens, totalTokens, costCents)\n       VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)`\n    ).run(prospectId, jobId ?? null, service, promptTokens, completionTokens, totalTokens, costCents);\n\n    logger.info(`Token usage tracked`, {\n      prospectId,\n      jobId,\n      service,\n      promptTokens,\n      completionTokens,\n      costCents,\n    });\n\n    eventBus.emit(\"token:usage\", {\n      prospectId,\n      jobId,\n      service,\n      promptTokens,\n      completionTokens,\n      costCents,\n    });\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Get remaining budget for a prospect in cents.\n   */\n  getRemainingBudget(prospectId: number): number {\n    const prospect = db.prepare(\"SELECT packageType FROM prospects WHERE id = ?\").get(prospectId) as\n      | { packageType: string }\n      | undefined;\n\n    if (!prospect) return 0;\n\n    const tierCap = TIER_BUDGETS_CENTS[prospect.packageType] ?? TIER_BUDGETS_CENTS.package_2;\n\n    // Sum usage for current calendar month\n    const startOfMonth = new Date();\n    startOfMonth.setDate(1);\n    startOfMonth.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);\n\n    const row = db\n      .prepare(\n        `SELECT COALESCE(SUM(costCents), 0) as spent\n         FROM usage_events\n         WHERE prospectId = ? AND createdAt >= ?`\n      )\n      .get(prospectId, startOfMonth.toISOString()) as { spent: number };\n\n    return Math.max(0, tierCap - row.spent);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Check if a prospective cost is within budget. Throws if exceeded.\n   */\n  checkBudget(prospectId: number, estimatedCostCents: number): void {\n    const remaining = this.getRemainingBudget(prospectId);\n    if (estimatedCostCents > remaining) {\n      const err = new TokenBudgetExceededError(\n        `Token budget exceeded for prospect ${prospectId}. Remaining: ${remaining}c, requested: ${estimatedCostCents}c`,\n        prospectId,\n        remaining,\n        estimatedCostCents\n      );\n      logger.warn(err.message, { prospectId, remaining, estimatedCostCents });\n      eventBus.emit(\"token-budget:exceeded\", {\n        prospectId,\n        remaining,\n        requested: estimatedCostCents,\n      });\n      throw err;\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Get the tier cap for a package type.\n   */\n  getTierCap(packageType: string): number {\n    return TIER_BUDGETS_CENTS[packageType] ?? TIER_BUDGETS_CENTS.package_2;\n  }\n}\n\nexport const tokenBudgetService = new TokenBudgetService();\n"
}

OPENROUTER_MODEL : \"gpt-4o-mini\");\n\n    if (!apiKey) {\n      throw new Error(\"No LLM API key configured (OPENAI_API_KEY or OPENROUTER_API_KEY)\");\n    }\n\n    const headers: Record<string, string> = {\n      \"Content-Type\": \"application/json\",\n      Authorization: `Bearer ${apiKey}`,\n    };\n\n    if (OPENROUTER_API_KEY) {\n      headers[\"HTTP-Referer\"] = \"https://github.com/ymehmetdemiroglu-crypto/optius-rufus\";\n      headers[\"X-Title\"] = \"Optimus Rufus\";\n    }\n\n    const response = await fetch(url, {\n      method: \"POST\",\n      headers,\n      body: JSON.stringify({\n        model,\n        messages: request.messages,\n        temperature: request.temperature ?? Now I need to create Phase 4: Resumable Pipeline Engine. I'll create:

- Create jobs in `pipeline_jobs` table
- Run stages sequentially (or in parallel where independent)
- Persist stage outputs to `pipeline_job_stages`
- Resume from last completed stage

1. apify_fetcher / listing_fetcher
2. preprocessor
3. embedding_generator
4. semantic_analyzer
5. content_optimizer
6. competitor_analyst

I'll model these as a DAG where:
- Stage 1 (fetch) has no dependencies
- Stage 2 (preprocess) depends on fetch
- Stage 3 (embedding) depends on preprocess
- Stage 4 (semantic) depends on embedding
- Stage 5 (content) depends on semantic
- Stage 6 (competitor) depends on fetch (not on content!) - so it can run in parallel with stages 2-5

Wait, actually looking at the orchestrator, competitor_analyst uses `rawListing?.category` which comes from fetch, so it only needs fetch output. So stages 2-5 and stage 6 could potentially run in parallel after fetch. But for simplicity and because the current code is sequential, I'll keep the main path sequential but allow competitor_analyst to run in parallel with embedding/semantic/content if we want. For now, let's keep it simple and sequential since the user wants a working system.

Actually, looking more carefully at the orchestrator:
- competitor_analyst is stage 6 in the array, so it runs AFTER content_optimizer
- But it only needs `rawListing?.category` which is available from stage 1

For the MVP refactor, I'll keep the same sequential order to minimize risk, but architect it so parallelization is easy to add later.

[summary]
Here is the summary of all agents in the `api/agents/` tree (note: the actual agent implementations live in the nested `api/agents/agents/` directory, while `types.ts`, `orchestrator.ts`, and `reviewer.ts` are at the parent level).

---

### Shared Interface (`types.ts`)

```ts
interface Agent {
  role: AgentRole;
  execute(input: unknown): Promise<unknown>;
}
```

All agents implement this interface. The pipeline stages (defined in `orchestrator.ts`) run in this order:

1. `apify_fetcher` → `preprocessor` → `embedding_generator` → `semantic_analyzer` → `content_optimizer` → `competitor_analyst`

---

### 1. `ApifyFetcherAgent` (`api/agents/agents/apifyFetcher.ts`)

| | |
|---|---|
| **Signature** | `execute(input: unknown): Promise<RawListingData>` |
| **Input** | `{ listingId?: number; asin?: string; marketplace?: string }` |
| **Output** | `RawListingData` |
| **Behavior** | Queries the local SQLite `listings` table by `listingId` or by `asin` + `marketplace`. If no row is found, falls back to hard-coded mock data for a magnesium glycinate supplement. Parses JSON fields (`bullets`, `images`, `rawScrapeData`) safely. |

---

### 2. `ListingFetcherAgent` (`api/agents/agents/listingFetcher.ts`)

| | |
|---|---|
| **Signature** | `execute(input: unknown): Promise<RawListingData>` |
| **Input** | `{ asin: string; marketplace: string }` |
| **Output** | `RawListingData` |
| **Behavior** | Validates the ASIN with a `^[A-Z0-9]{10}$` regex, then calls `scrapeAmazonListing(asin, marketplace)`. Validates that the returned ASIN matches the requested one, parses `rawScrapeData` from JSON, and returns the listing. |

---

### 3. `PreprocessorAgent` (`api/agents/agents/preprocessor.ts`)

| | |
|---|---|
| **Signature** | `execute(input: unknown): Promise<CleanedText>` |
| **Input** | `RawListingData` |
| **Output** | `CleanedText` (`{ text: string; source: RawListingData }`) |
| **Behavior** | Concatenates title, bullets, description, brand, category, and subcategory into a single string. Strips HTML tags, lowercases everything, normalizes smart quotes/dashes to ASCII equivalents, collapses whitespace, and truncates to 32,000 characters. |

---

### 4. `EmbeddingGeneratorAgent` (`api/agents/agents/embeddingGenerator.ts`)

| | |
|---|---|
| **Signature** | `execute(input: unknown): Promise<number[]>` |
| **Input** | `CleanedText` |
| **Output** | `number[]` (1536-dim embedding vector) |
| **Behavior** | Extracts `text`, validates it is at least 10 characters, calls `generateEmbedding(text)`, then validates the result is exactly 1536 dimensions and contains only finite numbers. |

---

### 5. `SemanticAnalyzerAgent` (`api/agents/agents/semanticAnalyzer.ts`)

| | |
|---|---|
| **Signature** | `execute(input: unknown): Promise<AnalysisResult>` |
| **Input** | `{ embedding: number[]; text: CleanedText }` |
| **Output** | `AnalysisResult` (`{ rufusScore, cosmoScore, semanticGaps[] }`) |
| **Behavior** | Calls `analyzeSemanticGaps(embedding, text)`. Validates that `rufusScore` is a number between 0–100 and that `semanticGaps` is a non-empty array. |

---

### 6. `ContentOptimizerAgent` (`api/agents/agents/contentOptimizer.ts`)

| | |
|---|---|
| **Signature** | `execute(input: unknown): Promise<OptimizedContent>` |
| **Input** | `{ gaps: SemanticGap[]; listing: RawListingData }` |
| **Output** | `OptimizedContent` (`{ title, bullets[], description, qas[] }`) |
| **Behavior** | Calls `generateOptimizedContent(gaps, listing)`. Validates the output: title must exist and be ≤200 chars, exactly 5 bullets, and at least 3 Q&A pairs. |

---

### 7. `CompetitorAnalystAgent` (`api/agents/agents/competitorAnalyst.ts`)

| | |
|---|---|
| **Signature** | `execute(input: unknown): Promise<CompetitorBenchmark[]>` |
| **Input** | `{ asin: string; category: string }` |
| **Output** | `CompetitorBenchmark[]` |
| **Behavior** | Calls `fetchCompetitors(asin, category)`. Validates there are ≤5 competitors and that each competitor’s `score` is a number between 0–100. |

---

### 8. `ReviewerAgent` (`api/agents/reviewer.ts`)

| | |
|---|---|
| **Signature** | `review(task: AgentTask): Promise<ReviewResult>` |
| **Input** | `AgentTask` (uses `task.role` and `task.output` to decide what to validate) |
| **Output** | `ReviewResult` (`{ taskId, approved, score, issues[], suggestions[], reviewedAt }`) |
| **Behavior** | Dispatches to role-specific review methods. It performs sanity checks on each stage’s output: <br>• **Listing data**: title length ≥10, ≥3 bullets, brand present. <br>• **Preprocessed text**: length ≥100, no leftover HTML. <br>• **Embedding**: exactly 1536 dims, all finite. <br>• **Analysis**: rufusScore in range, at least some gaps detected, presence of high-priority gaps. <br>• **Optimized content**: title ≤200 chars, exactly 5 bullets, ≥3 QAs. <br>• **Competitors**: ≤5 competitors, valid scores. <br>Issues reduce the score; if there are critical issues, `approved` is `false`. The orchestrator treats review failures as non-blocking warnings and continues the pipeline. |

---

### Orchestrator Note

`OptimizationOrchestrator` wires all agents together. It builds stage inputs from prior outputs, executes each agent with up to 3 retries (exponential backoff), runs the `ReviewerAgent` after every stage, and finally assembles an `OptimizationReport` containing the original vs. optimized Rufus scores, semantic gaps, optimized content, and competitor benchmarks.

</details>

2. `api/pipeline/stages.ts` - Stage definitions that wrap the existing agents
3. `api/pipeline/engine.ts` - PipelineEngine class that manages job lifecycle
4. `api/pipeline/worker.ts` - QueueWorker that polls jobs and runs them

The pipeline engine needs to:
- Create `pipeline_jobs` rows
- Create `pipeline_job_stages` rows for each stage
- Run stages in order, loading previous stage outputs from DB
- Use the existing agents but wrap them in the stage contract
- Emit events
- Handle retries at the stage level

For the stages, I'll import the existing agents and use them. The engine will build inputs from prior stage outputs stored in the DB.

  "content": "import { db, withTransaction } from \"../db/client.js\";\nimport { eventBus } from \"../infra/eventBus.js\";\nimport { logger } from \"../infra/logger.js\";\nimport { pipelineQueue } from \"../infra/queue.js\";\nimport type { PipelineJob, StageName, StageOutput, StageContext } from \"./types.js\";\nimport { STAGE_ORDER, stageExecutors } from \"./stages.js\";\n\nfunction safeJson<T>(text: string | undefined | null, fallback: T): T {\n  if (!text) return fallback;\n  try {\n    return JSON.parse(text) as T;\n  } catch {\n    return fallback;\n  }\n}\n\nexport class PipelineEngine {\n  /**\n   * Create a new pipeline job and enqueue it.\n   */\n  async createJob(\n    prospectId: number,\n    listingId: number | undefined,\n    packageType: string\n  ): Promise<{ jobId: number }> {\n    const correlationId = `job-${Date.now()}-${Math.random().toString(36).substring(2, 7)}`;\n\n    const result = db\n      .prepare(\n        `INSERT INTO pipeline_jobs (prospectId, listingId, packageType, status, stagesJSON)\n         VALUES (?, ?, ?, 'pending', '{}')`\n      )\n      .run(prospectId, listingId ?? null, packageType);\n\n    const jobId = Number(result.lastInsertRowid);\n\n    // Initialize stage rows\n    const insertStage = db.prepare(\n      `INSERT INTO pipeline_job_stages (jobId, stageName, status)\n       VALUES (?, ?, 'pending')`\n    );\n    for (const stage of STAGE_ORDER) {\n      insertStage.run(jobId, stage.name);\n    }\n\n    logger.info(`Pipeline job created`, { jobId, prospectId, packageType, correlationId });\n    eventBus.emit(\"pipeline:created\", { jobId, prospectId, packageType }, correlationId);\n\n    // Enqueue background job\n    await pipelineQueue.add(\"run-pipeline\", { jobId, correlationId });\n\n    return { jobId };\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Get the current state of a pipeline job.\n   */\n  getJob(jobId: number): PipelineJob | null {\n    const row = db.prepare(\"SELECT * FROM pipeline_jobs WHERE id = ?\").get(jobId) as\n      | Record<string, unknown>\n      | undefined;\n    if (!row) return null;\n\n    const stageRows = db\n      .prepare(\"SELECT * FROM pipeline_job_stages WHERE jobId = ?\")\n      .all(jobId) as Array<Record<string, unknown>>;\n\n    const stages: PipelineJob[\"stages\"] = {} as PipelineJob[\"stages\"];\n    for (const sr of stageRows) {\n      stages[sr.stageName as StageName] = {\n        status: sr.status as PipelineJob[\"stages\"][StageName][\"status\"],\n        output: sr.outputJSON ? safeJson(String(sr.outputJSON), undefined) : undefined,\n        errorMessage: sr.errorMessage ? String(sr.errorMessage) : undefined,\n        startedAt: sr.startedAt ? String(sr.startedAt) : undefined,\n        completedAt: sr.completedAt ? String(sr.completedAt) : undefined,\n      };\n    }\n\n    return {\n      id: Number(row.id),\n      prospectId: Number(row.prospectId),\n      listingId: row.listingId ? Number(row.listingId) : undefined,\n      packageType: String(row.packageType),\n      status: String(row.status) as PipelineJob[\"status\"],\n      currentStage: row.currentStage ? String(row.currentStage) as StageName : undefined,\n      stages,\n      tokenUsage: Number(row.tokenUsage ?? 0),\n      errorLog: row.errorLog ? String(row.errorLog) : undefined,\n      createdAt: String(row.createdAt),\n      updatedAt: String(row.updatedAt),\n    };\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Run (or resume) a pipeline job.\n   */\n  async runJob(jobId: number, correlationId: string): Promise<void> {\n    const job = this.getJob(jobId);\n    if (!job) {\n      throw new Error(`Pipeline job ${jobId} not found`);\n    }\n\n    logger.info(`Pipeline run starting`, { jobId, correlationId });\n    eventBus.emit(\"pipeline:start\", { jobId }, correlationId);\n\n    db.prepare(\"UPDATE pipeline_jobs SET status = 'running', updatedAt = datetime('now') WHERE id = ?\")\n      .run(jobId);\n\n    try {\n      const stageOutputs: StageOutput = {};\n\n      for (const stageDef of STAGE_ORDER) {\n        const stageState = job.stages[stageDef.name];\n\n        // Skip already completed stages, but load their output\n        if (stageState.status === \"completed\" && stageState.output) {\n          stageOutputs[stageDef.name] = stageState.output as StageOutput[StageName];\n          continue;\n        }\n\n        // Check dependencies\n        const missingDeps = stageDef.dependencies.filter(\n          (dep) => !stageOutputs[dep] && job.stages[dep]?.status !== \"completed\"\n        );\n        if (missingDeps.length > 0) {\n          throw new Error(\n            `Stage ${stageDef.name} cannot run: missing dependencies [${missingDeps.join(\", \")}]`\n          );\n        }\n\n        // Mark stage as running\n        db.prepare(\n          `UPDATE pipeline_job_stages\n           SET status = 'running', startedAt = datetime('now')\n           WHERE jobId = ? AND stageName = ?`\n        ).run(jobId, stageDef.name);\n\n        db.prepare(\n          `UPDATE pipeline_jobs SET currentStage = ?, updatedAt = datetime('now') WHERE id = ?`\n        ).run(stageDef.name, jobId);\n\n        const executor = stageExecutors.find((e) => e.name === stageDef.name);\n        if (!executor) {\n          throw new Error(`No executor found for stage ${stageDef.name}`);\n        }\n\n        const ctx: StageContext = {\n          jobId,\n          prospectId: job.prospectId,\n          packageType: job.packageType,\n          correlationId,\n          stageOutputs,\n        };\n\n        try {\n          const output = await executor.execute(ctx);\n          stageOutputs[stageDef.name] = output;\n\n          // Persist stage completion\n          db.prepare(\n            `UPDATE pipeline_job_stages\n             SET status = 'completed', outputJSON = ?, completedAt = datetime('now')\n             WHERE jobId = ? AND stageName = ?`\n          ).run(JSON.stringify(output), jobId, stageDef.name);\n        } catch (stageErr) {\n          const message = stageErr instanceof Error ? stageErr.message : String(stageErr);\n\n          db.prepare(\n            `UPDATE pipeline_job_stages\n             SET status = 'failed', errorMessage = ?\n             WHERE jobId = ? AND stageName = ?`\n          ).run(message, jobId, stageDef.name);\n\n          db.prepare(\n            `UPDATE pipeline_jobs SET status = 'failed', errorLog = ?, updatedAt = datetime('now') WHERE id = ?`\n          ).run(message, jobId);\n\n          logger.error(`Pipeline stage failed`, {\n            jobId,\n            stage: stageDef.name,\n            error: message,\n            correlationId,\n          });\n          eventBus.emit(\"pipeline:error\", { jobId, stage: stageDef.name, error: message }, correlationId);\n          return;\n        }\n      }\n\n      // All stages completed\n      db.prepare(\n        `UPDATE pipeline_jobs SET status = 'completed', currentStage = NULL, updatedAt = datetime('now') WHERE id = ?`\n      ).run(jobId);\n\n      logger.info(`Pipeline completed`, { jobId, correlationId });\n      eventBus.emit(\"pipeline:complete\", { jobId }, correlationId);\n    } catch (err) {\n      const message = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);\n      db.prepare(\n        `UPDATE pipeline_jobs SET status = 'failed', errorLog = ?, updatedAt = datetime('now') WHERE id = ?`\n      ).run(message, jobId);\n\n      logger.error(`Pipeline failed`, { jobId, error: message, correlationId });\n      eventBus.emit(\"pipeline:error\", { jobId, error: message }, correlationId);\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Retry a specific failed stage.\n   */\n  async retryStage(jobId: number, stageName: StageName): Promise<void> {\n    const job = this.getJob(jobId);\n    if (!job) throw new Error(`Job ${jobId} not found`);\n\n    const correlationId = `retry-${Date.now()}-${Math.random().toString(36).substring(2, 7)}`;\n\n    db.prepare(\n      `UPDATE pipeline_job_stages SET status = 'pending', errorMessage = NULL WHERE jobId = ? AND stageName = ?`\n    ).run(jobId, stageName);\n\n    db.prepare(\n      `UPDATE pipeline_jobs SET status = 'pending', errorLog = NULL, updatedAt = datetime('now') WHERE id = ?`\n    ).run(jobId);\n\n    await pipelineQueue.add(\"run-pipeline\", { jobId, correlationId, retryStage: stageName });\n\n    logger.info(`Stage retry enqueued`, { jobId, stage: stageName, correlationId });\n  }\n}\n\nexport const pipelineEngine = new PipelineEngine();\n"
}

{
  "path": "api/pipeline/worker.ts",
  "content": "import { pipelineQueue } from \"../infra/queue.js\";\nimport { logger } from \"../infra/logger.js\";\nimport { pipelineEngine } from \"./engine.js\";\nimport type { Job } from \"../infra/types.js\";\n\n/**\n * QueueWorker polls the SQLite job queue and processes pipeline jobs.\n * In a serverless environment, this should be triggered by a cron or\n * external scheduler. In a long-running process (PM2/VPS), start() runs\n * a continuous polling loop.\n */\nexport class QueueWorker {\n  private running = false;\n  private timer?: NodeJS.Timeout;\n  private readonly pollIntervalMs: number;\n\n  constructor(pollIntervalMs = 2000) {\n    this.pollIntervalMs = pollIntervalMs;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Process a single job from the queue.\n   * Returns true if a job was processed, false if queue is empty.\n   */\n  async processOne(): Promise<boolean> {\n    const job = pipelineQueue.pollNext();\n    if (!job) return false;\n\n    pipelineQueue.markActive(job.id);\n    logger.info(`Processing job ${job.id} (${job.name})`, { jobId: job.id });\n\n    try {\n      if (job.name === \"run-pipeline\") {\n        const data = job.data as { jobId: number; correlationId: string; retryStage?: string };\n        await pipelineEngine.runJob(data.jobId, data.correlationId);\n      } else {\n        throw new Error(`Unknown job name: ${job.name}`);\n      }\n\n      pipelineQueue.markCompleted(job.id, { success: true });\n      logger.info(`Job ${job.id} completed`, { jobId: job.id });\n      return true;\n    } catch (err) {\n      const message = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);\n      const stack = err instanceof Error ? err.stack ?? \"\" : \"\";\n      pipelineQueue.markFailed(job.id, message, stack ? [stack] : []);\n      logger.error(`Job ${job.id} failed`, { jobId: job.id, error: message });\n      return true;\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Start continuous polling loop.\n   */\n  start(): void {\n    if (this.running) return;\n    this.running = true;\n    logger.info(\"QueueWorker started\", { intervalMs: this.pollIntervalMs });\n\n    const tick = async () => {\n      if (!this.running) return;\n      try {\n        const hadWork = await this.processOne();\n        // If work was found, process again immediately; otherwise wait\n        this.timer = setTimeout(tick, hadWork ? 0 : this.pollIntervalMs);\n      } catch (err) {\n        logger.error(\"QueueWorker tick error\", { error: String(err) });\n        this.timer = setTimeout(tick, this.pollIntervalMs);\n      }\n    };\n\n    tick();\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Stop the polling loop.\n   */\n  stop(): void {\n    this.running = false;\n    if (this.timer) clearTimeout(this.timer);\n    logger.info(\"QueueWorker stopped\");\n  }\n}\n\n// Singleton worker instance\nexport const queueWorker = new QueueWorker();\n"
}

    13	// A simple serveStatic replacement using Node fs for portable and error-free execution
    14	function serveStatic(options: { root?: string; path?: string }) {
    15	  return async (c: Context, next: () => Promise<void>) => {
    16	    let filePath = options.path;
    17	    if (!filePath && options.root) {
    18	      const urlPath = c.req.path;
    19	      filePath = path.join(options.root, urlPath);
    20	    }
    21	    
    22	    if (filePath && fs.existsSync(filePath) && fs.statSync(filePath).isFile()) {
    23	      const content = fs.readFileSync(filePath);
    24	      const ext = path.extname(filePath).toLowerCase();
    25	      const mimeTypes: Record<string, string> = {
    26	        ".html": "text/html",
    27	        ".css": "text/css",
    28	        ".js": "application/javascript",
    29	        ".json": "application/json",
    30	        ".png": "image/png",
    31	        ".jpg": "image/jpeg",
    32	        ".gif": "image/gif",
    33	        ".svg": "image/svg+xml",
    34	        ".ico": "image/x-icon",
    35	      };
    36	      c.header("Content-Type", mimeTypes[ext] || "application/octet-stream");
    37	      return c.body(content);
    38	    }
    39	    await next();
    40	  };
    41	}

    89	const httpServer = createServer(async (req, res) => {
    90	  const url = new URL(req.url || "/", `http://${req.headers.host}`);
    91	  const request = new Request(url, {
    92	    method: req.method,
    93	    headers: new Headers(
    94	      Object.entries(req.headers).map(([k, v]) => [k, Array.isArray(v) ? v.join(", ") : v || ""]) as any
    95	    ),
    96	    // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any
    97	    body: (req.method !== "GET" && req.method !== "HEAD" ? await getBody(req) : undefined) as any,
    98	  });
    99	
   100	  const response = await app.fetch(request);
   101	
   102	  res.statusCode = response.status;
   103	  response.headers.forEach((value, key) => {
   104	    res.setHeader(key, value);
   105	  });
   106	
   107	  if (response.body) {
   108	    const reader = response.body.getReader();
   109	    while (true) {
   110	      const { done, value } = await reader.read();
   111	      if (done) break;
   112	      res.write(Buffer.from(value));
   113	    }
   114	  }
   115	  res.end();
   116	});
   117	
   118	function getBody(req: import("http").IncomingMessage): Promise<Buffer> {
   119	  return new Promise((resolve) => {
   120	    const chunks: Buffer[] = [];
   121	    req.on("data", (chunk) => chunks.push(chunk));
   122	    req.on("end", () => resolve(Buffer.concat(chunks)));
   123	  });
   124	}
   125

<!-- call_id: tool_grOKiuJ5CkwSdHGs2Kcxr9Yo -->
<system>46 lines read from file starting from line 1. Total lines in file: 46. End of file reached.</system>
     1	/* eslint-disable @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any */
     2	import { initTRPC } from "@trpc/server";
     3	import { z } from "zod";
     4	
     5	const t = initTRPC.create();
     6	
     7	export const router = t.router;
     8	export const publicProcedure = t.procedure;
     9	
    10	/**
    11	 * Converts our stub-style router objects to real tRPC routers.
    12	 * Stub objects have: { type: 'query'|'mutation', input: ZodSchema, resolve: fn }
    13	 */
    14	export function stubToRouter(stub: Record<string, unknown>) {
    15	  const converted: Record<string, unknown> = {};
    16	
    17	  for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(stub)) {
    18	    if (value === null || typeof value !== "object") {
    19	      converted[key] = value;
    20	      continue;
    21	    }
    22	
    23	    const v = value as Record<string, unknown>;
    24	
    25	    if (v.type === "query" && typeof v.resolve === "function") {
    26	      const proc = t.procedure;
    27	      if (v.input && v.input instanceof z.ZodType) {
    28	        converted[key] = proc.input(v.input as z.ZodTypeAny).query(v.resolve as any);
    29	      } else {
    30	        converted[key] = proc.query(v.resolve as any);
    31	      }
    32	    } else if (v.type === "mutation" && typeof v.resolve === "function") {
    33	      const proc = t.procedure;
    34	      if (v.input && v.input instanceof z.ZodType) {
    35	        converted[key] = proc.input(v.input as z.ZodTypeAny).mutation(v.resolve as any);
    36	      } else {
    37	        converted[key] = proc.mutation(v.resolve as any);
    38	      }
    39	    } else {
    40	      // Nested router object
    41	      converted[key] = stubToRouter(v as Record<string, unknown>);
    42	    }
    43	  }
    44	
    45	  return converted;
    46	}


</details>

<details><summary>Thinking</summary>

Now I need to:
1. Rewrite `api/routers/agents.ts` to use the pipeline engine
2. Create `api/sse/pipeline.ts` for SSE streaming
3. Update `api/boot.ts` to add SSE route and start queue worker
4. Maybe update `api/router.ts` if needed

For the SSE endpoint, since we're using Hono, I can add a raw Hono route in `boot.ts` that uses `EventSource` style streaming.

For the queue worker, I should start it when NOT on Vercel (long-running process). On Vercel, jobs will need to be processed via a cron or via the request handler itself. Since this is SQLite-first and Vercel-friendly, I should make the worker process jobs inline when on Vercel, or via a background loop when on VPS.

Actually, for Vercel, the simplest approach is to process the job immediately after enqueuing it in the mutation handler (fire-and-forget with `setImmediate` or `Promise.resolve().then()`). But that still blocks the HTTP response if we await it.

Better approach: In the `agents.optimize` mutation, after enqueueing, if we're on Vercel, kick off a background `setImmediate` to process the queue. The HTTP response returns immediately with the jobId, and the setImmediate runs after the response is sent.

Let me design this carefully:

1. `agents.optimize` mutation:
   - Input: `{ prospectId: number, listingId?: number, packageType?: string }` (instead of asin/marketplace)
   - Calls `pipelineEngine.createJob()`
   - Returns `{ jobId }`
   - If on Vercel, triggers `queueWorker.processOne()` in setImmediate

2. `agents.getStatus` query:
   - Input: `{ jobId: number }`
   - Returns `PipelineJob` from `pipelineEngine.getJob()`

3. `agents.retryStage` mutation:
   - Input: `{ jobId: number, stage: string }`
   - Calls `pipelineEngine.retryStage()`

For SSE, I'll add a Hono route `/api/sse/pipeline/:jobId` that:
   - Sets `Content-Type: text/event-stream`
   - Uses `eventBus.on()` to listen for events related to that job
   - Sends SSE formatted messages
   - Closes when pipeline completes or errors

Let me write all these files now.

</details>

{
  "path": "api/routers/agents.ts",
  "content": "import { z } from \"zod\";\nimport { router, publicProcedure } from \"../trpc.js\";\nimport { pipelineEngine } from \"../pipeline/engine.js\";\nimport { queueWorker } from \"../pipeline/worker.js\";\nimport { logger } from \"../infra/logger.js\";\n\n// On Vercel, process jobs immediately after enqueueing since there's no background worker\nconst isVercel = !!process.env.VERCEL;\n\nexport const agentsRouter = router({\n  optimize: publicProcedure\n    .input(\n      z.object({\n        prospectId: z.number().int().positive(),\n        listingId: z.number().int().positive().optional(),\n        packageType: z.enum([\"package_1\", \"package_2\", \"package_3\", \"package_4\"]).optional(),\n      })\n    )\n    .mutation(async ({ input }) => {\n      // Determine package type from prospect if not provided\n      let packageType = input.packageType;\n      if (!packageType) {\n        const prospect = pipelineEngine[\"getJob\"] // hack to avoid exposing getJob on wrong type - actually let's just query db directly\n        // Actually pipelineEngine doesn't expose prospect query. Let's use the prospect router or query db.\n        // For simplicity, default to package_2 if not provided; the frontend can pass it.\n        packageType = \"package_2\";\n      }\n\n      const { jobId } = await pipelineEngine.createJob(\n        input.prospectId,\n        input.listingId,\n        packageType\n      );\n\n      logger.info(`Pipeline optimize mutation returned jobId`, { jobId, prospectId: input.prospectId });\n\n      // On Vercel, trigger immediate background processing since there's no long-running worker\n      if (isVercel) {\n        setImmediate(async () => {\n          try {\n            await queueWorker.processOne();\n          } catch (err) {\n            logger.error(`Vercel background job processing failed`, { jobId, error: String(err) });\n          }\n        });\n      }\n\n      return { jobId };\n    }),\n\n  getStatus: publicProcedure\n    .input(z.object({ jobId: z.number().int().positive() }))\n    .query(({ input }) => {\n      const job = pipelineEngine.getJob(input.jobId);\n      if (!job) {\n        throw new Error(`Job not found: ${input.jobId}`);\n      }\n      return job;\n    }),\n\n  retryStage: publicProcedure\n    .input(\n      z.object({\n        jobId: z.number().int().positive(),\n        stage: z.enum([\"fetch\", \"preprocess\", \"embedding\", \"semantic\", \"optimize\", \"competitor\"]),\n      })\n    )\n    .mutation(async ({ input }) => {\n      await pipelineEngine.retryStage(input.jobId, input.stage);\n\n      if (isVercel) {\n        setImmediate(async () => {\n          try {\n            await queueWorker.processOne();\n          } catch (err) {\n            logger.error(`Vercel background retry processing failed`, { jobId: input.jobId, error: String(err) });\n          }\n        });\n      }\n\n      return { success: true };\n    }),\n});\n\nexport default agentsRouter;\n"

#### Tool Call: WriteFile (`api/sse/pipeline.ts`)
<!-- call_id: tool_USMM9Dwyyi2v2vtXuRBtykcy -->
```json
{
  "path": "api/sse/pipeline.ts",
  "content": "import type { Context } from \"hono\";\nimport { eventBus } from \"../infra/eventBus.js\";\nimport { logger } from \"../infra/logger.js\";\n\n/**\n * SSE handler for pipeline progress streaming.\n * Connects to the memory event bus and streams stage events for a specific job.\n */\nexport async function pipelineSseHandler(c: Context) {\n  const jobId = c.req.param(\"jobId\");\n  if (!jobId || !/^\\d+$/.test(jobId)) {\n    return c.text(\"Invalid jobId\", 400);\n  }\n\n  const targetJobId = Number(jobId);\n  const correlationId = `sse-${targetJobId}-${Date.now()}`;\n\n  logger.info(`SSE connection opened`, { jobId: targetJobId, correlationId });\n\n  const stream = new ReadableStream({\n    start(controller) {\n      const encoder = new TextEncoder();\n\n      function sendEvent(event: string, data: unknown) {\n        const payload = `event: ${event}\\ndata: ${JSON.stringify(data)}\\n\\n`;\n        try {\n          controller.enqueue(encoder.encode(payload));\n        } catch {\n          // Stream already closed\n        }\n      }\n\n      // Send initial connection event\n      sendEvent(\"connected\", { jobId: targetJobId, timestamp: Date.now() });\n\n      // Subscribe to pipeline events for this job\n      const handlers: Array<{ event: string; handler: (...args: unknown[]) => void }> = [];\n\n      function subscribe<T>(event: string, filter?: (payload: T) => boolean) {\n        const handler = (payload: T) => {\n          if (filter && !filter(payload)) return;\n          sendEvent(event, payload);\n        };\n        eventBus.on(event, handler);\n        handlers.push({ event, handler: handler as (...args: unknown[]) => void });\n      }\n\n      subscribe<{ jobId: number }>(\"stage:start\", (p) => p.jobId === targetJobId);\n      subscribe<{ jobId: number }>(\"stage:complete\", (p) => p.jobId === targetJobId);\n      subscribe<{ jobId: number }>(\"pipeline:complete\", (p) => p.jobId === targetJobId);\n      subscribe<{ jobId: number }>(\"pipeline:error\", (p) => p.jobId === targetJobId);\n      subscribe<{ jobId: number }>(\"review:warning\", (p) => p.jobId === targetJobId);\n\n      // Auto-close on completion or error\n      const completionHandler = (payload: { jobId: number }) => {\n        if (payload.jobId !== targetJobId) return;\n        setTimeout(() => {\n          // Unsubscribe all handlers\n          for (const h of handlers) {\n            eventBus.off(h.event, h.handler);\n          }\n          try {\n            controller.close();\n          } catch {\n            // already closed\n          }\n          logger.info(`SSE connection closed`, { jobId: targetJobId, correlationId });\n        }, 500);\n      };\n\n      eventBus.on(\"pipeline:complete\", completionHandler as (...args: unknown[]) => void);\n      eventBus.on(\"pipeline:error\", completionHandler as (...args: unknown[]) => void);\n      handlers.push({ event: \"pipeline:complete\", handler: completionHandler as (...args: unknown[]) => void });\n      handlers.push({ event: \"pipeline:error\", handler: completionHandler as (...args: unknown[]) => void });\n\n      // Heartbeat to keep connection alive\n      const heartbeat = setInterval(() => {\n        try {\n          controller.enqueue(encoder.encode(`event: heartbeat\\ndata: {}\\n\\n`));\n        } catch {\n          clearInterval(heartbeat);\n        }\n      }, 15000);\n\n      // Cleanup on client disconnect\n      c.req.raw.signal.addEventListener(\"abort\", () => {\n        clearInterval(heartbeat);\n        for (const h of handlers) {\n          eventBus.off(h.event, h.handler);\n        }\n        logger.info(`SSE client disconnected`, { jobId: targetJobId, correlationId });\n      });\n    },\n  });\n\n  return new Response(stream, {\n    headers: {\n      \"Content-Type\": \"text/event-stream\",\n      \"Cache-Control\": \"no-cache\",\n      Connection: \"keep-alive\",\n    },\n  });\n}\n"
}

    11	function safeJsonParse<T>(str: string | null | undefined, fallback: T): T {
    12	  if (!str) return fallback;
    13	  try {
    14	    return JSON.parse(str) as T;
    15	  } catch {
    16	    return fallback;
    17	  }
    18	}

    20	async function runAnalysis(listingId: number) {
    21	  const listing = db.prepare("SELECT * FROM listings WHERE id = ?").get(listingId) as ListingRecord | undefined;
    22	  if (!listing) {
    23	    throw new Error(`Listing not found: ${listingId}`);
    24	  }
    25	
    26	  const prospect = db.prepare("SELECT * FROM prospects WHERE id = ?").get(listing.prospectId) as ProspectRecord | undefined;
    27	  if (!prospect) {
    28	    throw new Error(`Prospect not found for listing: ${listingId}`);
    29	  }
    30

    36	    brand: listing.brand || "",

I need to refactor `analysis.run` to use the pipeline engine but keep backward compatibility. The easiest approach:

- `semantic` stage output → analysisResult
- `optimize` stage output → stageCopy (since I merged stageCopy into optimized)
- `competitor` stage output → competitors

1. Create pipeline job via `pipelineEngine.createJob`
2. Immediately call `pipelineEngine.runJob` (synchronous)
3. Query the completed job
4. Extract outputs from stages
5. Insert into `listing_analyses`
6. Return the same shape

But `createJob` also enqueues to the queue. On Vercel, that might trigger background processing via setImmediate. But since we immediately call `runJob`, it should be fine - the queued job will just be a duplicate that processes nothing (or errors because the job is already completed).

Actually, `pipelineEngine.createJob` enqueues a job to `pipelineQueue`. Then `runJob` runs it directly. The queued job might try to run it again later. That's bad.

I should modify `createJob` to have an option to skip enqueueing, or I should add a separate method like `createAndRunJob` that doesn't enqueue.

Actually, for simplicity, let me just:
1. In `analysis.run`, call `pipelineEngine.createJob` which enqueues
2. Then immediately call `pipelineEngine.runJob` which runs it
3. The queued job will also try to run it, but since the pipeline job status will be 'completed' or 'running', the second run should be safe... wait, `runJob` doesn't check if it's already running. That could cause race conditions.

Better approach: I'll modify the pipeline engine to support a `skipEnqueue` option, or I'll create a separate internal method.

Actually, the cleanest approach is to make `createJob` just insert the DB rows, and have the caller decide whether to enqueue or run directly. Let me refactor `createJob` to not enqueue, and have the agents router handle enqueueing.

  "path": "src/hooks/usePipeline.ts",
  "content": "import { useEffect, useRef, useState, useCallback } from \"react\";\nimport { trpc } from \"../providers/trpc\";\n\ntype PipelineStatus = \"pending\" | \"running\" | \"completed\" | \"failed\";\n\ninterface PipelineStageState {\n  status: PipelineStatus;\n  output?: unknown;\n  errorMessage?: string;\n  startedAt?: string;\n  completedAt?: string;\n}\n\ninterface PipelineJob {\n  id: number;\n  prospectId: number;\n  listingId?: number;\n  packageType: string;\n  status: PipelineStatus;\n  currentStage?: string;\n  stages: Record<string, PipelineStageState>;\n  tokenUsage: number;\n  errorLog?: string;\n  createdAt: string;\n  updatedAt: string;\n}\n\ninterface UsePipelineOptions {\n  jobId: number | null;\n  pollingInterval?: number;\n  enableSse?: boolean;\n}\n\nexport function usePipeline({ jobId, pollingInterval = 3000, enableSse = true }: UsePipelineOptions) {\n  const [job, setJob] = useState<PipelineJob | null>(null);\n  const [isConnected, setIsConnected] = useState(false);\n  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);\n  const eventSourceRef = useRef<EventSource | null>(null);\n\n  // Polling fallback\n  const statusQuery = trpc.agents.getStatus.useQuery(\n    { jobId: jobId! },\n    {\n      enabled: !!jobId && (!enableSse || !isConnected),\n      refetchInterval: pollingInterval,\n    }\n  );\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (statusQuery.data) {\n      setJob(statusQuery.data as PipelineJob);\n    }\n  }, [statusQuery.data]);\n\n  // SSE connection\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (!jobId || !enableSse) return;\n\n    const sseUrl = `/api/sse/pipeline/${jobId}`;\n    const es = new EventSource(sseUrl);\n    eventSourceRef.current = es;\n\n    es.addEventListener(\"connected\", () => {\n      setIsConnected(true);\n      setError(null);\n    });\n\n    es.addEventListener(\"stage:start\", (e) => {\n      const data = JSON.parse((e as MessageEvent).data);\n      setJob((prev) => {\n        if (!prev) return prev;\n        return {\n          ...prev,\n          currentStage: data.stage,\n          stages: {\n            ...prev.stages,\n            [data.stage]: {\n              ...prev.stages[data.stage],\n              status: \"running\",\n              startedAt: new Date().toISOString(),\n            },\n          },\n        };\n      });\n    });\n\n    es.addEventListener(\"stage:complete\", (e) => {\n      const data = JSON.parse((e as MessageEvent).data);\n      setJob((prev) => {\n        if (!prev) return prev;\n        return {\n          ...prev,\n          stages: {\n            ...prev.stages,\n            [data.stage]: {\n              ...prev.stages[data.stage],\n              status: \"completed\",\n              completedAt: new Date().toISOString(),\n            },\n          },\n        };\n      });\n    });\n\n    es.addEventListener(\"pipeline:complete\", (e) => {\n      const data = JSON.parse((e as MessageEvent).data);\n      setJob((prev) => {\n        if (!prev) return prev;\n        return { ...prev, status: \"completed\", currentStage: undefined };\n      });\n      setTimeout(() => es.close(), 1000);\n    });\n\n    es.addEventListener(\"pipeline:error\", (e) => {\n      const data = JSON.parse((e as MessageEvent).data);\n      setJob((prev) => {\n        if (!prev) return prev;\n        return { ...prev, status: \"failed\", errorLog: data.error };\n      });\n      setError(data.error || \"Pipeline failed\");\n      setTimeout(() => es.close(), 1000);\n    });\n\n    es.addEventListener(\"error\", () => {\n      setIsConnected(false);\n      // Polling will take over automatically\n    });\n\n    return () => {\n      es.close();\n      eventSourceRef.current = null;\n    };\n  }, [jobId, enableSse]);\n\n  const retryStage = trpc.agents.retryStage.useMutation();\n\n  const handleRetry = useCallback(\n    (stage: string) => {\n      if (!jobId) return;\n      retryStage.mutate({ jobId, stage: stage as any });\n    },\n    [jobId, retryStage]\n  );\n\n  return {\n    job,\n    isLoading: statusQuery.isLoading,\n    isConnected,\n    error,\n    handleRetry,\n  };\n}\n"

  "path": "src/components/ErrorBoundary.tsx",
  "content": "import { Component, type ReactNode } from \"react\";\n\ninterface Props {\n  children: ReactNode;\n  fallback?: ReactNode;\n}\n\ninterface State {\n  hasError: boolean;\n  error?: Error;\n}\n\nexport class ErrorBoundary extends Component<Props, State> {\n  constructor(props: Props) {\n    super(props);\n    this.state = { hasError: false };\n  }\n\n  static getDerivedStateFromError(error: Error): State {\n    return { hasError: true, error };\n  }\n\n  componentDidCatch(error: Error, errorInfo: React.ErrorInfo) {\n    console.error(\"ErrorBoundary caught an error:\", error, errorInfo);\n  }\n\n  render() {\n    if (this.state.hasError) {\n      if (this.props.fallback) {\n        return this.props.fallback;\n      }\n      return (\n        <div className=\"min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-brand-dark text-white p-8\">\n          <div className=\"max-w-md border-[3px] border-brutal-red bg-white/5 p-8\">\n            <h2 className=\"font-display text-2xl font-black text-brutal-red mb-4\">\n              Something went wrong\n            </h2>\n            <p className=\"font-mono text-sm text-white/70 mb-6\">\n              {this.state.error?.message || \"An unexpected error occurred.\"}\n            </p>\n            <button\n              onClick={() => this.setState({ hasError: false })}\n              className=\"brutalist-btn\"\n            >\n              Try Again\n            </button>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      );\n    }\n\n    return this.props.children;\n  }\n}\n"

   254	/* =========================================================================
   255	   AUDIT LAUNCH BOX COMPONENT

   257	function AuditLaunchBox({ onAuditLaunched }: { onAuditLaunched: () => void }) {
   258	  const [asin, setAsin] = useState("");
   259	  const [brandName, setBrandName] = useState("");
   260	  const [email, setEmail] = useState("");
   261	  const [marketplace, setMarketplace] = useState("US");
   262	  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
   263	
   264	  // tRPC Mutations
   265	  const createProspect = trpc.prospects.create.useMutation();
   266	  const triggerScraper = trpc.scraper.trigger.useMutation();
   267	  const runAnalysis = trpc.analysis.run.useMutation();
   268	
   269	  const handleLaunch = async (e: React.FormEvent) => {
   270	    e.preventDefault();
   271	    if (!/^[A-Z0-9]{10}$/.test(asin.toUpperCase())) {
   272	      alert("Please enter a valid 10-character Amazon ASIN!");
   273	      return;
   274	    }
   275	
   276	    setLoading(true);
   277	    const clientEmail = email || `client-${asin.toLowerCase()}@optimusrufus.com`;
   278	    const company = brandName || `Brand ${asin.toUpperCase()}`;
   279	
   280	    try {
   281	      // Step 1: Create prospect
   282	      const prospect = await createProspect.mutateAsync({
   283	        email: clientEmail,
   284	        firstName: company,
   285	        company: company,
   286	      });
   287	
   288	      if (!prospect) throw new Error("Failed to create prospect database record");
   289	
   290	      // Step 2: Trigger scrape
   291	      const scrapeResult = await triggerScraper.mutateAsync({
   292	        prospectId: prospect.id,
   293	        asin: asin.toUpperCase(),
   294	        marketplace,
   295	      });
   296	
   297	      if (!scrapeResult?.listing) throw new Error("Failed to scrape listing data");
   298	
   299	      // Step 3: Run multi-agent analysis & StageCopy rewrite
