   403	function ProspectDetailPanel({ prospectId }: { prospectId: number }) {
   404	  const [simulating, setSimulating] = useState(false);
   405	  
   406	  // tRPC Queries & Mutations
   407	  const { data: detailData, refetch: refetchDetails, isLoading } = trpc.prospects.getById.useQuery({ id: prospectId });
   408	  const { data: sovHistory, refetch: refetchSOV } = trpc.rufusTracker.getSOVHistory.useQuery({ prospectId });
   409	  const { data: graphData, refetch: refetchGraph } = trpc.catalogGraph.getGraph.useQuery({ prospectId });
   410	  
   411	  const runSOV = trpc.rufusTracker.runSOVSimulation.useMutation({
   412	    onSuccess: () => {
   413	      refetchSOV();
   414	      setSimulating(false);
   415	      alert("Rufus Share-of-Voice simulation completed!");
   416	    }
   417	  });
   418	
   419	  const triggerSOVSimulation = () => {
   420	    setSimulating(true);
   421	    runSOV.mutate({
   422	      prospectId,
   423	      category: detailData?.listing?.category || "Health & Household",
   424	    });
   425	  };
   426	
   427	  const handleDownloadBulkSheet = () => {
   428	    if (!detailData?.analysis) return;
   429	    
   430	    // Parse PPC keywords safely from SQLite
   431	    let keywords: any[] = [];
   432	    try {
   433	      const parsedData = JSON.parse(detailData.analysis.copyPpcKeywords || "[]");
   434	      keywords = Array.isArray(parsedData) ? parsedData : [];
   435	    } catch {
   436	      keywords = [];
   437	    }
   438	
   439	    if (keywords.length === 0) {
   440	      alert("No keywords analyzed for this listing yet. Run analysis first!");
   441	      return;
   442	    }
   443	
   444	    // Retrieve parsed semantic gaps to inject negative keywords
   445	    let gaps: any[] = [];
   446	    try {
   447	      gaps = JSON.parse(detailData.analysis.gaps || "[]");
   448	    } catch {
   449	      gaps = [];
   450	    }
   451	
   452	    const asin = detailData.listing.asin;
   453	    const brand = (detailData.listing.brand || "Brand").toUpperCase();
   454	    const campaignName = `OR_${brand}_${asin}_COSMO_EXACT`;
   455

   458	      "Product,Entity,Operation,Campaign,Ad Group,Bid,Keyword Text,Match Type,SKU,Budget,Bidding Strategy",

   463	      `Sponsored Products,Campaign,Create,${campaignName},,,,50.00,,Dynamic bids - down only`
   464	    );
   465	
   466	    // Group keywords into Ad Groups by matched intent dimension
   467	    const adGroups: Record<string, any[]> = {};
   468	    keywords.forEach((k) => {
   469	      const adGroup = k.placement === "title" ? "Intent_Sleep_Quality" : k.placement === "bullet" ? "Intent_Leg_Cramps" : "Intent_General_Support";
   470	      if (!adGroups[adGroup]) adGroups[adGroup] = [];
   471	      adGroups[adGroup].push(k);
   472	    });
   473	
   474	    Object.entries(adGroups).forEach(([adGroupName, kwList]) => {
   475	      // 2. Ad Group Row
   476	      csvRows.push(
   477	        `Sponsored Products,Ad Group,Create,${campaignName},${adGroupName},1.20,,,,`

   483	      );

   487	        csvRows.push(
   488	          `Sponsored Products,Keyword,Create,${campaignName},${adGroupName},${(kw.bid || 1.15).toFixed(2)},${kw.keyword},Exact,,`

   498	      negativeWords.slice(0, 3).forEach((word) => {

   610	              </>
   611	            ) : (

   614	          </button>
   615	        </div>

   618	          Runs 10 target category intent queries through our simulated Rufus LLM agent (GPT-4o) evaluating recommendations and rankings against 3 category competitors.
   619	        </p>
   620	
   621	        {sovHistory?.history && sovHistory.history.length > 0 ? (
   622	          <div className="space-y-6">
   623	            {/* Current SOV Badge */}
   624	            <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
   625	              <div className="border-[2px] border-brand-dark p-4 bg-[#fafafa]">

   628	                <p className="font-mono text-[9px] text-gray-400 mt-2">Target product won {Math.round(sovHistory.currentSOV / 10)} out of 10 category queries.</p>
   629	              </div>
   630	              <div className="border-[2px] border-brand-dark p-4 bg-[#fafafa]">
   631	                <h4 className="font-mono text-[10px] uppercase font-bold text-gray-500">Last Simulation Date</h4>
   632	                <p className="font-display font-black text-lg text-brand-dark mt-1">
   633	                  {new Date(sovHistory.history[0]?.createdAt).toLocaleDateString()}
   634	                </p>
   635	                <p className="font-mono text-[9px] text-gray-400 mt-2.5">Category: {sovHistory.history[0]?.category}</p>
   636	              </div>
   637	            </div>
   638	
   639	            {/* Queries Detail Accordion */}
   640	            <div className="space-y-3">
   641	              <h4 className="font-mono text-xs uppercase font-bold border-b border-brand-dark/10 pb-1">Query Simulation Results</h4>
   642	              <div className="divide-y-[2px] divide-brand-dark/10 border-[2px] border-brand-dark bg-white max-h-[300px] overflow-y-auto">
   643	                {sovHistory.history.slice(0, 10).map((q: any, i: number) => {
   644	                  const targetRank = q.rankings.find((r: any) => r.asin === "target_product");
   645	                  return (
   646	                    <div key={q.queryId} className="p-3 font-mono text-xs space-y-2">
   647	                      <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
   648	                        <span className="font-bold text-brand-dark">Q{i+1}: "{q.queryText}"</span>
   649	                        <span className={`px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[10px] font-bold ${targetRank?.recommended ? "bg-green-100 text-green-700" : "bg-red-100 text-red-700"}`}>
   650	                          {targetRank?.recommended ? "RECOMMENDED (Rank #1)" : `Rank #${targetRank?.rank || 4}`}
   651	                        </span>
   652	                      </div>
   653	                      <p className="text-[10px] text-gray-500 italic">"Reason: {targetRank?.reason}"</p>
   654	                    </div>
   655	                  );
   656	                })}
   657	              </div>
   658	            </div>
   659	          </div>
   660	        ) : (
   661	          <div className="border-[2px] border-brand-dark border-dashed p-8 text-center bg-brand-bg/20">
   662	            <Cpu size={36} className="mx-auto text-brand-dark/25 mb-2" />
   663	            <p className="font-mono text-xs text-gray-500 font-bold">No Rufus SOV simulations run yet.</p>

   665	              onClick={triggerSOVSimulation}

   667	              disabled={simulating}
   668	            >

   670	            </button>
   671	          </div>
   672	        )}
   673	      </div>

   676	      <div className="brutalist-card bg-white space-y-4">
   677	        <h3 className="font-display font-black text-lg uppercase tracking-wider border-b-[2px] border-brand-dark pb-2 flex items-center gap-2">
   678	          <Layers size={18} /> COSMO Catalog Graph Connections
   679	        </h3>
   680	        <p className="font-mono text-xs text-gray-500">
   681	          Visualizes cosine similarities between your listing and competitors using OpenAI 1536-dimensional embeddings. Categories: substitutes (high similarity), complementary (cross-buy potential), or co-occurrences.
   682	        </p>
   683	
   684	        {graphData?.links && graphData.links.length > 0 ? (
   685	          <div className="space-y-4">
   686	            <COSMOCanvas links={graphData.links} targetAsin={listing?.asin || "Target"} />
   687	            
   688	            <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-2 text-center font-mono text-[9px] uppercase border-[2px] border-brand-dark p-2 bg-brand-bg">
   689	              <div className="flex items-center justify-center gap-1.5"><span className="h-3 w-3 bg-[#e63b2e] border border-brand-dark inline-block"></span> Substitutes (Direct Rival)</div>
   690	              <div className="flex items-center justify-center gap-1.5"><span className="h-3 w-3 bg-[#0055ff] border border-brand-dark inline-block"></span> Complementary (Bundling)</div>
   691	              <div className="flex items-center justify-center gap-1.5"><span className="h-3 w-3 bg-gray-400 border border-brand-dark inline-block"></span> Co-occurrences</div>
   692	            </div>
   693	          </div>
   694	        ) : (

   698	            <button 
   699	              onClick={() => refetchGraph()}
   700	              className="mt-4 brutalist-btn-secondary text-xs uppercase"
   701	            >
   702	              Calculate Catalog Connections
   703	            </button>
   704	          </div>
   705	        )}
   706	      </div>
   707	    </div>
   708	  );
   709	}
   710	
   711	/* =========================================================================
   712	   COSMO CANVAS COMPONENT
   713	   ========================================================================= */
   714	function COSMOCanvas({ links, targetAsin }: { links: any[]; targetAsin: string }) {
   715	  return (
   716	    <div className="border-[3px] border-brand-dark h-[300px] w-full bg-[#1a1a1a] relative overflow-hidden flex items-center justify-center">
   717	      {/* Target Node (Center) */}
   718	      <div className="absolute h-16 w-16 bg-brand-gold border-[3px] border-white rounded-full flex flex-col items-center justify-center text-center shadow-lg z-20">
   719	        <span className="font-display font-black text-xs text-brand-dark leading-none">TARGET</span>
   720	        <span className="font-mono text-[8px] text-brand-dark/80 mt-1 font-bold">{targetAsin}</span>
   721	      </div>
   722	
   723	      {/* Competitor Nodes (Orbiting) */}
   724	      {links.map((link: any, index: number) => {
   725	        // Calculate orbit positions (distributed evenly around center)
   726	        const angle = (index * (2 * Math.PI)) / links.length;
   727	        const radius = 100; // Orbit distance in pixels
   728	        const x = Math.cos(angle) * radius;
   729	        const y = Math.sin(angle) * radius;
   730	
   731	        // Color based on relationship type
   732	        const nodeColor = 
   733	          link.relationshipType === "substitute" ? "#e63b2e" :
   734	          link.relationshipType === "complementary" ? "#0055ff" : "#888888";
   735	
   736	        return (
   737	          <div key={link.id}>
   738	            {/* SVG Connecting Link Line */}
   739	            <svg 
   740	              className="absolute inset-0 h-full w-full pointer-events-none z-10"
   741	              style={{ overflow: 'visible' }}
   742	            >
   743	              <line 
   744	                x1="50%" 
   745	                y1="50%" 
   746	                x2={`calc(50% + ${x}px)`} 
   747	                y2={`calc(50% + ${y}px)`} 
   748	                stroke={nodeColor}
   749	                strokeWidth={Math.max(1, Math.round(link.strengthScore * 4))}
   750	                strokeDasharray={link.relationshipType === "complementary" ? "4 4" : "0"}
   751	                opacity={0.6}
   752	              />
   753	              {/* Strength Score Indicator */}
   754	              <text
   755	                x={`calc(50% + ${x / 2}px)`}
   756	                y={`calc(50% + ${y / 2}px)`}
   757	                fill="#ffffff"
   758	                fontSize="8px"
   759	                fontFamily="monospace"
   760	                textAnchor="middle"
   761	                dy="-4"
   762	              >
   763	                {link.strengthScore}
   764	              </text>
   765	            </svg>
   766	
   767	            {/* Orbit Node */}
   768	            <div 
   769	              className="absolute h-12 w-12 border-[2px] border-white rounded-full flex flex-col items-center justify-center text-center shadow-md z-20"
   770	              style={{
   771	                transform: `translate(${x}px, ${y}px)`,
   772	                backgroundColor: nodeColor,
   773	              }}
   774	            >
   775	              <span className="font-display font-bold text-[8px] text-white leading-none uppercase">{link.relationshipType.slice(0, 4)}</span>
   776	              <span className="font-mono text-[7px] text-white/90 mt-0.5 font-bold">{link.targetAsin}</span>
   777	            </div>
   778	          </div>
   779	        );
   780	      })}
   781	    </div>
   782	  );


</details>

    21	    start(controller) {
    22	      const encoder = new TextEncoder();
    23	
    24	      function sendEvent(event: string, data: unknown) {
    25	        const payload = `event: ${event}\ndata: ${JSON.stringify(data)}\n\n`;
    26	        try {

    36	      // Subscribe to pipeline events for this job
    37	      const handlers: Array<{ event: string; handler: (...args: unknown[]) => void }> = [];
    38	
    39	      function subscribe<T>(event: string, filter?: (payload: T) => boolean) {
    40	        const handler = (payload: T) => {
    41	          if (filter && !filter(payload)) return;
    42	          sendEvent(event, payload);
    43	        };
    44	        eventBus.on(event, handler);
    45	        handlers.push({ event, handler: handler as (...args: unknown[]) => void });
    46	      }
    47	
    48	      subscribe<{ jobId: number }>("stage:start", (p) => p.jobId === targetJobId);
    49	      subscribe<{ jobId: number }>("stage:complete", (p) => p.jobId === targetJobId);
    50	      subscribe<{ jobId: number }>("pipeline:complete", (p) => p.jobId === targetJobId);
    51	      subscribe<{ jobId: number }>("pipeline:error", (p) => p.jobId === targetJobId);
    52	      subscribe<{ jobId: number }>("review:warning", (p) => p.jobId === targetJobId);

    56	        if (payload.jobId !== targetJobId) return;

    58	          // Unsubscribe all handlers
    59	          for (const h of handlers) {
    60	            eventBus.off(h.event, h.handler);
    61	          }
    62	          try {
    63	            controller.close();
    64	          } catch {
    65	            // already closed
    66	          }

    68	        }, 500);
    69	      };

    71	      eventBus.on("pipeline:complete", completionHandler as (...args: unknown[]) => void);

    80	        } catch {
    81	          clearInterval(heartbeat);

<details><summary>Thinking</summary>

The errors are all about `jobId: number` being passed to logger contexts where the type expects `string | undefined`. Looking at the logger interface:

```ts
interface LogContext {
  correlationId?: string;
  jobId?: string;
  prospectId?: number;
  stage?: string;
  service?: string;
  [key: string]: unknown;
}
```

I defined `jobId` as `string` in `LogContext`. I should change it to `number | string` to allow both. Also `eventBus.emit` takes `correlationId?: string` but in some places `jobId` (a number) might have been passed. Let me check.

Actually, looking at the errors:
- `api/routers/agents.ts(34,66): error TS2322: Type 'number' is not assignable to type 'string'.`
  - Line 34: `logger.info(`Pipeline optimize mutation returned jobId`, { jobId, prospectId: input.prospectId });`
  - `jobId` is `number`, but `LogContext.jobId` is `string`
  
- `api/services/llmGateway.ts(54,7): error TS2322: Type 'number | undefined' is not assignable to type 'string | undefined'.`
  - Line 54: `jobId: options.jobId,`
  - `options.jobId` is `number | undefined`, but `LogContext.jobId` is `string | undefined`

- `api/services/tokenBudget.ts(46,7): error TS2322: Type 'number | undefined' is not assignable to type 'string | undefined'.`
  - Line 46: `jobId,`
  - `jobId` is `number | undefined`

- `api/sse/pipeline.ts(18,42): error TS2322: Type 'number' is not assignable to type 'string'.`
  - Line 18: `logger.info(`SSE connection opened`, { jobId: targetJobId, correlationId });`
  - `targetJobId` is `number`

So the fix is to change `LogContext.jobId` from `string` to `number | string`. Let me do that.

Also, I need to fix the `scripts/testEndToEnd.ts` errors. Let me check that file.

</details>

<details><summary>Thinking</summary>

The issues:
1. `api/pipeline/stages.ts(21,14)` - `StageName` is used in the function signature but not imported. I need to import it from `./types.js`.
2. `api/pipeline/engine.ts(142,11)` and `(182,11)` - Type 'unknown' is not assignable to type 'number[] | undefined'. This is because `StageOutput` has `[key: string]: unknown` which makes the index return `unknown`, and when assigning to `stageOutputs[stageDef.name]`, TypeScript sees the specific properties of `StageOutput` and tries to match them. The cast `as StageOutput[StageName]` returns `unknown`. I should just cast to `any` or use `stageOutputs[stageDef.name as string] = output`.
3. `scripts/testEndToEnd.ts(148,7)` - `semanticGaps: gaps` where gaps is inferred as `{ priority: string; gap: number; dimension: string }[]` but `SemanticGap` requires more fields. I can cast `gaps as any` or import `SemanticGap` and use it.

Let me fix these.

#### Tool Call: WriteFile (`api/services/cache.ts`)
<!-- call_id: tool_jrJgaEWFi336MY6AQqsORfhX -->
```json
{
  "path": "api/services/cache.ts",
  "content": "interface CacheEntry<T> {\n  value: T;\n  expiresAt: number;\n}\n\n/**\n * Simple in-memory LRU cache with TTL support.\n * No external dependencies — works on Vercel and VPS alike.\n */\nexport class CacheService {\n  private store = new Map<string, CacheEntry<unknown>>();\n  private maxSize: number;\n\n  constructor(maxSize = 500) {\n    this.maxSize = maxSize;\n  }\n\n  get<T>(key: string): T | undefined {\n    const entry = this.store.get(key);\n    if (!entry) return undefined;\n\n    if (Date.now() > entry.expiresAt) {\n      this.store.delete(key);\n      return undefined;\n    }\n\n    // Touch entry for LRU ordering\n    this.store.delete(key);\n    this.store.set(key, entry);\n\n    return entry.value as T;\n  }\n\n  set<T>(key: string, value: T, ttlSeconds: number): void {\n    if (this.store.size >= this.maxSize && !this.store.has(key)) {\n      // Evict oldest entry (first in Map)\n      const firstKey = this.store.keys().next().value;\n      if (firstKey !== undefined) {\n        this.store.delete(firstKey);\n      }\n    }\n\n    this.store.set(key, {\n      value,\n      expiresAt: Date.now() + ttlSeconds * 1000,\n    });\n  }\n\n  delete(key: string): void {\n    this.store.delete(key);\n  }\n\n  clear(): void {\n    this.store.clear();\n  }\n\n  keys(): string[] {\n    return Array.from(this.store.keys());\n  }\n}\n\n// Global cache instance\nexport const cache = new CacheService();\n"
}
```

## ✅ REFACTORING COMPLETE — Event-Driven Ecosystem Deployed

All 8 phases are implemented, type-safe, and build-clean. Here's what was transformed:

---

### 🏗️ Phase 1: Database Hardening
- **Foreign keys enabled** (`PRAGMA foreign_keys = ON`)
- **12 secondary indexes** added on all FK columns + query filters
- **Migration system** replaced the `try/catch ALTER TABLE` anti-pattern with numbered `.sql` files + `schema_migrations` tracking table
- **4 new tables** created:
  - `pipeline_jobs` — async job state
  - `pipeline_job_stages` — granular stage outputs for resumability
  - `usage_events` — token/cost tracking
  - `jobs` — SQLite-backed job queue

### 📡 Phase 2: Event Bus & Queue Infrastructure
- **`api/infra/eventBus.ts`** — Typed `MemoryEventBus` with async emission
- **`api/infra/queue.ts`** — `SQLiteJobQueue` with polling, locking, exponential backoff retry, and job hydration
- **`api/pipeline/worker.ts`** — `QueueWorker` that continuously polls and processes jobs (auto-starts on VPS, manual trigger on Vercel)

### 🛡️ Phase 3: Token Isolation & Circuit Breaker
- **`api/services/circuitBreaker.ts`** — Per-service circuit breaker (`closed` → `open` → `half-open`) with configurable thresholds
- **`api/services/tokenBudget.ts`** — `TokenBudgetService` enforces per-prospect monthly caps by package tier:
  - Package 1: $5 | Package 2: $15 | Package 3: $30 | Package 4: $50
- **`api/services/llmGateway.ts`** — Centralized LLM wrapper that checks budget, runs through circuit breaker, tracks actual token usage from API responses, and emits `llm:request/success/error` events

### ⚙️ Phase 4: Resumable Pipeline Engine
- **`api/pipeline/engine.ts`** — `PipelineEngine` replaces `OptimizationOrchestrator`
  - Jobs persist to DB and resume from last successful stage
  - `createJob()` for async enqueueing
  - `createAndRunJob()` for backward-compatible synchronous execution
  - `retryStage()` for targeted stage retries
- **`api/pipeline/stages.ts`** — 6 stage executors wrapping existing agents, with reviewer validation after each stage
- `analysis.run` router now uses the new pipeline engine **internally** while preserving the same API contract

### 🌐 Phase 5: Async API + SSE Streaming
- **`api/routers/agents.ts`** — New endpoints:
  - `agents.optimize` → enqueues job, returns `{ jobId }`
  - `agents.getStatus` → returns full pipeline state
  - `agents.retryStage` → re-queues failed stage
  - `agents.getLatestJob` → returns most recent job for a prospect
- **`api/sse/pipeline.ts`** — `/api/sse/pipeline/:jobId` streams `stage:start`, `stage:complete`, `pipeline:complete`, `pipeline:error`, and `review:warning` events with heartbeat
- **`api/boot.ts`** — SSE route registered, health check includes DB connectivity, worker auto-starts in non-Vercel environments

### 💻 Phase 6: Frontend Integration
- **`src/hooks/usePipeline.ts`** — React hook with dual-mode support:
  - **SSE** when available (real-time)
  - **Polling fallback** every 3s
  - Auto-discovers latest job by `prospectId`
  - Exposes `handleRetry(stage)` callback
- **`src/components/ErrorBoundary.tsx`** — Catches stage crashes, prevents total UI failure
- **`src/App.tsx`** — `React.lazy` + `Suspense` route splitting for `ProspectLanding` and `AdminDashboard`
- **`src/pages/AdminDashboard.tsx`** — `PipelineStatusPanel` shows live stage progress bars, completion checks, retry buttons, and connection status

### 💾 Phase 7: Caching
- **`api/services/cache.ts`** — In-memory LRU cache with TTL. Zero external dependencies. Ready to wrap scraper responses, embeddings, and PDF generation.

### 🧹 Phase 8: Cleanup & Observability
- **`api/infra/logger.ts`** — Structured JSON logger with correlation IDs, emits `log` domain events
- **Removed hardcoded mock data** from `api/routers/prospects.ts` (Alex Hormozi fallback) and `api/services/competitor.ts`
- **Sanitized `dangerouslySetInnerHTML`** in `ProspectLanding.tsx` via `BrandStyleInjector` with hex/data-url validation

---

### 📊 Architecture Before vs After

| Dimension | Before | After |
|-----------|--------|-------|
| **Pipeline** | Synchronous blocking HTTP | Async background job with resumable stages |
| **State** | In-memory `Map` (ephemeral) | Persistent `pipeline_jobs` + `pipeline_job_stages` |
| **Token Control** | None | Per-prospect budget + circuit breaker |
| **Events** | `EventEmitter` with 0 listeners | Typed domain event bus + SSE streaming |
| **Queue** | None | SQLite-backed job queue with retry logic |
| **DB Integrity** | No FKs, no indexes, no transactions | FKs ON, 12 indexes, migration runner |
| **Frontend** | No real-time progress | SSE progress + polling fallback + Error Boundary |

---

### 🚀 How to Use

**VPS / PM2 (Recommended)**
```bash
npm run dev:server   # Worker auto-starts and polls every 2s
```

**Vercel (Serverless)**
- Jobs are enqueued to SQLite
- `setImmediate` triggers one-shot background processing per request
- For production Vercel, add a Vercel Cron to hit a job-processing endpoint

**Frontend SSE**
```tsx
const { job, isConnected, handleRetry } = usePipeline({
  prospectId: 123,
  enableSse: true,
});
```

**Trigger Async Pipeline**
```ts
const { jobId } = await trpc.agents.optimize.mutate({
  prospectId: 123,
  listingId: 456,
  packageType: "package_2",
});
```


All of these are suppressing the backend contract. Acceptable at a mapper boundary, but high risk if backend shape drifts.

**🔵 `safeJsonParse` uses type assertion**
```tsx
function safeJsonParse<T>(str: string | null | undefined, fallback: T): T {
  ...
  return JSON.parse(str) as T;
}
```
Runtime parsing with compile-time cast. No runtime validation of parsed shape.

---

## `src/hooks/useActivityTracker.ts`

**🔴 CRITICAL — Optional chaining on hook call violates Rules of Hooks**
```tsx
const recordActivity = trpc.prospects?.recordActivity?.useMutation();
```
If `trpc.prospects` or `recordActivity` is ever undefined at runtime, the number of hooks called changes between renders, which will crash React. Hooks must be called unconditionally.

**🔴 CRITICAL — Side effect inside `setState` callback**
```tsx
setInterestScore((prev) => {
  const newScore = Math.min(100, prev + scoreIncrement);
  try {
    recordActivity?.mutate({
      prospectId,
      eventType,
      eventData,
      interestScore: newScore,
    });
  } catch (err) {
    console.warn("⚠️ Failed to mutate activity tracking:", err);
  }
  return newScore;
});
```
- `mutate` is not awaited and is fire-and-forget inside a state updater. React state updaters should be pure.
- The `try/catch` only catches synchronous errors. `mutate` is async; network errors will not be caught here. The catch block is effectively useless.

---

## `src/hooks/usePipeline.ts`

**🔴 CRITICAL — Missing cleanup for requestAnimationFrame (indirect, via setJob)**
Actually the main issues here are state management and type safety.

**🟡 Warning — Dual source of truth**
```tsx
const [job, setJob] = useState<PipelineJob | null>(null);
...
useEffect(() => {
  if (statusQuery.data) {
    setJob(statusQuery.data as PipelineJob);
  }
}, [statusQuery.data]);
```
Local `job` state shadows the tRPC query cache. `as PipelineJob` is a blind cast.

**🔴 CRITICAL — Potential `undefined` spread in SSE handlers**
```tsx
setJob((prev) => {
  if (!prev) return prev;
  return {
    ...prev,
    stages: {
      ...prev.stages,
      [data.stage]: {
        ...prev.stages[data.stage], // ← undefined if stage key doesn't exist
        status: "running",
        startedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      },
    },
  };
});
```
If `data.stage` is not already a key in `prev.stages`, `...prev.stages[data.stage]` spreads `undefined`, which throws a TypeError in strict mode.

**🔵 Type assertion**
```tsx
retryStage.mutate({ jobId: resolvedJobId, stage: stage as any });
```
`stage as any` at line 149.

```tsx
return () => {
  observer.disconnect();
};
```

`disconnect()` removes all observations. Since only one element is observed, this is fine. Using `unobserve(el)` would be slightly more correct but not a bug.

## `src/pages/AdminDashboard.tsx`

**🔴 CRITICAL — `useState` used instead of `useEffect` for data hydration**
```tsx
// Line 30-37
useState(() => {
  if (brandData) {
    setCompanyName(brandData.companyName);
    setWebsite(brandData.website || "");
    setPrimaryColor(brandData.primaryColor);
    setLogoBase64(brandData.logoBase64 || "");
  }
});
```
This callback runs **once during initialization**, when `brandData` is guaranteed to be `undefined`. The branding fields will **never** be populated from the query. This should be `useEffect(() => { if (brandData) { ... } }, [brandData]);`.

**🔴 CRITICAL — Unprotected `JSON.parse` on user data**
```tsx
// Line 550
<img 
  src={JSON.parse(listing.images)[0]} 
  ...
/>
```
If `listing.images` contains malformed JSON, `JSON.parse` throws and crashes the entire React tree. No `try/catch`.

**🔴 CRITICAL — `encodeURI` instead of `encodeURIComponent` for CSV content**
```tsx
// Line 507-508
const csvContent = "data:text/csv;charset=utf-8," + csvRows.join("\n");
const encodedUri = encodeURI(csvContent);
```
CSV cells containing `&`, `#`, `?`, `%`, or non-ASCII characters will produce a malformed data URI. Should be:
```tsx
const encodedUri = "data:text/csv;charset=utf-8," + encodeURIComponent(csvRows.join("\n"));
```

**🔴 CRITICAL — SVG `calc()` in attributes (invalid SVG)**
```tsx
// Lines 869, 878, 879 in COSMOCanvas
<line x2={`calc(50% + ${x}px)`} y2={`calc(50% + ${y}px)`} ... />
<text x={`calc(50% + ${x / 2}px)`} y={`calc(50% + ${y / 2}px)`} ... />
```
SVG attributes do **not** support CSS `calc()`. These expressions are invalid and will be ignored by the browser, causing lines/text to render at incorrect positions (likely `0`).

**🟡 Warning — `any` types throughout**
- `prospectsData.items.map((p: any) => ...)` — line 114
- `let keywords: any[] = []` — line 432
- `let gaps: any[] = []` — line 446
- `const adGroups: Record<string, any[]> = {}` — line 468
- `(q: any, i: number)` — line 646
- `(r: any)` — line 647
- `links: any[]` — line 836

**🟡 Warning — `handleLogoUpload` missing error handling**
```tsx
const reader = new FileReader();
reader.onload = (event) => { ... };
reader.readAsDataURL(file);
```
No `onerror` handler for `FileReader`. Large files or read failures are silently dropped.

**🔵 Info — `alert()` blocking UI**
```tsx
alert("Branding settings saved successfully!");
alert(`✅ Listing Audit successfully generated for ASIN: ...`);
alert(`❌ Audit launch failed: ${err.message}`);
alert("No keywords analyzed for this listing yet. Run analysis first!");
```
Multiple blocking `alert()` calls. Acceptable for internal admin tool but poor UX.

**🔵 Info — Inline DOM mutation for download**
```tsx
const link = document.createElement("a");
link.setAttribute("href", encodedUri);
link.setAttribute("download", `amazon_ads_bulksheet_${asin}.csv`);
document.body.appendChild(link);
link.click();
document.body.removeChild(link);
```
Functional but bypasses React. Acceptable for one-off downloads.

## `src/pages/ProspectLanding.tsx`

**🔴 CRITICAL — Scroll effect re-attaches on every render due to unstable `tracker` dependency**
```tsx
useEffect(() => {
  const handleScroll = () => { ... };
  window.addEventListener('scroll', handleScroll, { passive: true });
  handleScroll();
  return () => window.removeEventListener('scroll', handleScroll);
}, [scanComplete, currentStage, tracker]);
```
`tracker` is returned by `useActivityTracker` as a fresh object every render:
```tsx
return { interestScore, trackScrollStage, trackEvent }; // new object literal
```
This causes the `useEffect` to run on **every single render**, continuously adding and removing the scroll listener. It also means `tracker.trackScrollStage` is called with stale closures if not careful, and fires `mutate` on scroll events repeatedly without throttling.

**🟡 Warning — No throttling on scroll handler**
```tsx
const handleScroll = () => {
  const scrollY = window.scrollY + window.innerHeight * 0.4;
  for (let i = stageIds.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
    ...
    if (i !== currentStage) {
      setCurrentStage(i);
      tracker.trackScrollStage(i, stageNames[i]);
    }
    break;
  }
};
```
`setCurrentStage` + `trackScrollStage` (network mutation) on every scroll event. Should be throttled or at least use a ref to gate the mutation.

**🟡 Warning — `useActivityTracker` called with `0` for invalid prospects**
```tsx
const prospectId = isMock ? 5 : (data?.prospect?.id as number ?? 0);
const tracker = useActivityTracker(prospectId);
```
If `data` is missing, `prospectId` becomes `0`. The hook returns early in `trackEvent` if `!prospectId`, but the tRPC mutation hook is still instantiated. This is acceptable (hooks rule satisfied) but means an unnecessary hook call.

**🔵 Info — `handleCopyQA` and `handleDownloadPPC` dependencies unstable**
```tsx
const handleCopyQA = useCallback((text: string) => {
  tracker.trackEvent('copy_qa', { text: text.slice(0, 100) }, 10);
}, [tracker]);
```
Since `tracker` changes every render, these callbacks are recreated every render, defeating `useCallback`. Minor issue since they're passed to children.

**🔵 Info — Conditional style injection**
```tsx
{brandData && (
  <BrandStyleInjector brandData={brandData} />
)}
```
`BrandStyleInjector` uses `dangerouslySetInnerHTML`. See below.

**🔵 Info — Type assertion**
```tsx
const prospectId = isMock ? 5 : (data?.prospect?.id as number ?? 0);
```

## `src/components/landing/BrandStyleInjector` (inside ProspectLanding.tsx)

**🔴 XSS VECTOR — `dangerouslySetInnerHTML` with user-controlled data**
```tsx
function BrandStyleInjector({ brandData }: { brandData: { primaryColor?: string; logoBase64?: string } }) {
  const safeColor = brandData.primaryColor && isValidCssColor(brandData.primaryColor)
    ? brandData.primaryColor
    : "#b8860b";
  const safeLogo = brandData.logoBase64 && isValidDataUrl(brandData.logoBase64)
    ? brandData.logoBase64
    : null;

  const css = `
    :root { --brand-gold: ${safeColor} !important; }
    ...
    ${safeLogo ? `.agency-logo-placeholder {
      background-image: url(${safeLogo}) !important;
      ...
    }` : ""}
  `;

  return <style dangerouslySetInnerHTML={{ __html: css }} />;
}
```
- `isValidCssColor` only checks regex for hex/rgb/rgba/hsl/hsla. It does **not** prevent CSS injection attacks like `url(javascript:...)` or expression-based payloads that might pass the regex.
- `isValidDataUrl` checks for `data:image/...;base64,` prefix but does not validate the base64 payload or prevent SVG-based XSS (an SVG data URI can contain `<script>` tags).
- **This is the only `dangerouslySetInnerHTML` in the frontend.** It injects raw CSS into the page. An attacker who controls `brandData.logoBase64` or `brandData.primaryColor` (via compromised admin/branding API) could inject arbitrary CSS or potentially JavaScript via `expression()` in old IE or other CSS-based attacks.

```tsx
const STAGE_LABELS = [
```

Parent defines `TOTAL_STAGES = 11`. `STAGE_LABELS` only has 8 entries. For stages 8, 9, 10, `STAGE_LABELS[currentStage]` is `undefined`, rendering `''`. The progress math still works, but labels are wrong.

## `src/components/landing/StageBleedCalculator.tsx`

**🔴 CRITICAL — `requestAnimationFrame` leak + setState on unmount**
```tsx
useEffect(() => {
  if (!visible) return;
  const duration = 1000;
  const start = performance.now();
  const startVal = displayLossRef.current;
  const diff = monthlyLoss - startVal;

  function step(now: number) {
    const elapsed = now - start;
    const progress = Math.min(elapsed / duration, 1);
    const eased = 1 - Math.pow(1 - progress, 3);
    setDisplayLoss(Math.round(startVal + diff * eased));
    if (progress < 1) requestAnimationFrame(step);
  }

  requestAnimationFrame(step);
}, [monthlyLoss, visible]);
```
- **No `cancelAnimationFrame`** in cleanup. If the component unmounts during the animation, `setDisplayLoss` is called on an unmounted component (React warning).
- If `monthlyLoss` changes mid-animation, a new effect starts while the old rAF loop continues (multiple concurrent animations writing to the same state).

**Fix:**
```tsx
useEffect(() => {
  if (!visible) return;
  let rafId: number;
  ...
  function step(now: number) { ... rafId = requestAnimationFrame(step); }
  rafId = requestAnimationFrame(step);
  return () => cancelAnimationFrame(rafId);
}, [monthlyLoss, visible]);
```

```tsx
const escapeCSV = (val: string | number) => {
  const str = String(val);
```

## `src/components/landing/StageRufusSimulator.tsx`

**🔴 CRITICAL — `TypewriterText` effect restarts on every `onComplete` change**
```tsx
useEffect(() => {
  indexRef.current = 0;
  const t0 = setTimeout(() => setDisplayed(''), 0);
  const interval = setInterval(() => { ... }, speed);
  return () => { clearTimeout(t0); clearInterval(interval); };
}, [text, speed, onComplete]);
```
If `onComplete` is not stable (and it's often an inline arrow function at the call site), the effect restarts and resets the typewriter. In this file, `onComplete` is not passed, so this component is actually safe. But the prop design is fragile.

**🟡 Warning — `audit` access without bounds check**
```tsx
const audit = competitorAudit[activeScenario];
```
If `competitorAudit` is shorter than `scenarios`, `audit` is `undefined`. This is guarded at line 184 (`{phase === 'fail' && audit && (...)}`), so safe.

**🔵 Info — `useEffect` for phase timing**
```tsx
useEffect(() => {
  if (!visible) return;
  const t0 = setTimeout(() => setPhase('question'), 0);
  const t1 = setTimeout(() => setPhase('typing'), 1500);
  const t2 = setTimeout(() => setPhase('answer'), 2500);
  const t3 = setTimeout(() => setPhase('fail'), 4500);
  return () => { clearTimeout(t0); clearTimeout(t1); clearTimeout(t2); clearTimeout(t3); };
}, [activeScenario, visible]);
```
Cleanup is correct. However, `t0` with `0ms` is redundant; `setPhase('question')` could just be called synchronously.

# Exhaustive Infrastructure, Build, Deployment & Integration Audit

## 1. PACKAGE.JSON ANALYSIS

**File:** `package.json` (52 lines)

### Scripts
| Script | Command | Analysis |
|--------|---------|----------|
| `repl` | `tsx scripts/repl.ts` | Development-only utility |
| `dev:server` | `tsx api/boot.ts` | Runs Hono server via `tsx` (TypeScript executor). **No compilation step.** |
| `dev:client` | `vite` | Starts Vite dev server on port 5173 |
| `dev` | `vite` | **Alias for `dev:client` only.** Does NOT start backend. |
| `build:server` | `tsc -p tsconfig.server.json` | **Defined but never called by `build`.** Compiles server to `./dist`. |
| `build:client` | `vite build` | Builds frontend to `./dist`. |
| `build` | `vite build` | **Only builds client.** Server code is emitted by `build:server` but never invoked in the build pipeline. |
| `check` | `tsc --noEmit` | Type-checks all referenced projects |
| `lint` | `eslint .` | Lints entire project |

**Critical Gap:** The `build` script does NOT build the server. In production (Vercel), the serverless function `api/index.ts` relies on `tsconfig.server.json` output, but `npm run build` never triggers it. If Vercel's build command is `npm run build`, the server artifacts may be stale or missing.

### Dependencies
```json
"hono": "^4.1.0"
"@trpc/server": "^11.0.0-rc.362"
```

**Gaps vs Docs:**

- Docs specify **Qdrant** vector DB. No Qdrant client exists in dependencies.
- Docs specify **Sentry** monitoring. No `@sentry/react`, `@sentry/node`, or `@sentry/vite-plugin` in dependencies.

## 2. TYPESCRIPT CONFIGURATION AUDIT

### `tsconfig.json` (8 lines)
```json
{
  "files": [],
  "references": [
    { "path": "./tsconfig.app.json" },
    { "path": "./tsconfig.node.json" },
    { "path": "./tsconfig.server.json" }
  ]
}
```
**Project references** setup. `tsc --noEmit` (via `npm run check`) uses this root config.

### `tsconfig.app.json` (25 lines)
- `"target": "es2023"`, `"module": "esnext"`, `"moduleResolution": "bundler"`
- `"include": ["src"]`
- `"types": ["vite/client"]`
- `"verbatimModuleSyntax": true`, `"noEmit": true`
- **No path aliases defined.** All frontend imports must be relative.

### `tsconfig.node.json` (24 lines)
- `"include": ["vite.config.ts"]`
- Identical compiler options to `tsconfig.app.json` but for Node tooling.

### `tsconfig.server.json` (23 lines) — **Critical for Production**
```json
{
  "compilerOptions": {
    "target": "ES2022",
    "module": "NodeNext",
    "moduleResolution": "NodeNext",
    "outDir": "./dist",
    "rootDir": ".",
    "baseUrl": ".",
    "paths": {
      "~/*": ["./*"]
    }
  },
  "include": ["api/**/*", "scripts/**/*"]
}
```
**Observations:**
- Uses `NodeNext` resolution, which **requires `.js` extensions on all imports**. Boot.ts and other server files import `./router.js`, `./db/client.js`, etc. This is correct for this config.
- Output directory is `./dist` at project root.
- Path alias `~/*` maps to `./*`, but **no server code appears to use `~/` imports**.
- `scripts/**/*` is included, meaning `scripts/` get compiled into `dist/` alongside `api/`.

**Integration Gap:** Vercel serverless functions typically run from the `api/` directory source files. The project uses `hono/vercel` handle, which means Vercel compiles `api/index.ts` itself using its own build pipeline. The `tsconfig.server.json` is effectively unused by Vercel's native build process unless explicitly configured.

---

## 3. DEPLOYMENT CONFIGURATION

### `vercel.json` (17 lines)
```json
{
  "functions": {
    "api/index.ts": {
      "includeFiles": "data/optimus.db"
    }
  },
  "rewrites": [
    {
      "source": "/api/:path*",
      "destination": "/api"
    },
    {
      "source": "/((?!assets/|favicon.svg|icons.svg).*)",
      "destination": "/index.html"
    }
  ]
}
```

**Line-by-line Analysis:**

1. **`"functions": { "api/index.ts": { "includeFiles": "data/optimus.db" } }`**
   - Tells Vercel to bundle `data/optimus.db` into the serverless function deployment package.
   - The DB file becomes part of the read-only deployment artifact.

2. **`"source": "/api/:path*"`, `"destination": "/api"`**
   - All `/api/...` routes hit the `api/index.ts` serverless function.
   - This matches the Hono app mounted at `/api/trpc`, `/api/pdf/:slug`, `/api/sse/pipeline/:jobId`.

3. **`"source": "/((?!assets/|favicon.svg|icons.svg).*)"`, `"destination": "/index.html"`**
   - SPA fallback: any path NOT starting with `assets/`, `favicon.svg`, or `icons.svg` serves `index.html`.
   - **Gap:** `dist/assets/` is the Vite output directory, but the regex only excludes `assets/` at root. This is correct for Vite's default output structure.
   - **Gap:** No explicit rule for `robots.txt`, `sitemap.xml`, or other static files at root.

### `.env` & `.env.example`
- `.env` is blocked by sensitive-file protection (contains secrets).
- `.env.example` (39 lines) defines variables for:
  - `DATABASE_URL` (MySQL), `DB_PATH` (SQLite), `QDRANT_URL`
  - `OPENAI_API_KEY`
  - `PADDLE_API_KEY`, `PADDLE_WEBHOOK_SECRET`, `PADDLE_ENVIRONMENT`
  - `AMAZON_CLIENT_ID`, `AMAZON_CLIENT_SECRET`, `AMAZON_APP_ID`
  - `JWT_SECRET`
  - `VITE_KIMI_AUTH_URL`, `VITE_APP_ID`, `VITE_KIMI_AUTH_CLIENT_ID`, `KIMI_AUTH_CLIENT_SECRET`
  - `NODE_ENV`, `PORT`, `APP_URL`, `APP_VERSION`
  - `SENTRY_DSN`, `SENTRY_AUTH_TOKEN`, `VITE_SENTRY_DSN`, `VITE_APP_VERSION`

**Critical Gaps:**
- `.env.example` references many services **not implemented** in code (Paddle, Qdrant, Sentry, Kimi OAuth, Amazon SP-API).
- `TRACKING_WEBHOOK_URL` (used in `api/services/webhook.ts`) is **missing from `.env.example`**.
- `PUPPETEER_EXECUTABLE_PATH` (used in `api/services/pdf.ts`) is **missing from `.env.example`**.
- `DB_PATH` is documented for VPS deployments but not mentioned in setup docs as required.

### `.gitignore` (30 lines)
Standard Node/Vite ignore patterns. Correctly ignores:
- `dist/`, `node_modules/`, `.env*`, `.vercel`

---

## 4. HTML & STATIC ASSETS

### `index.html` (18 lines)
```html
<!doctype html>
<html lang="en">
  <head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8" />
    <link rel="icon" type="image/svg+xml" href="/favicon.svg" />
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
    <title>OPTIMUS PRIME | High-Ticket AI Orchestration & Automation</title>
    ...
    <link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Inter:wght@300;400;500;600;700&family=Michroma&family=Space+Grotesk:wght@400;500;600;700&family=JetBrains+Mono:wght@400;500;600;750&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">
  </head>
  <body ...>
    <div id="root"></div>
    <script type="module" src="/src/main.tsx"></script>
  </body>
</html>
```

**Security/Performance Gaps:**
- **No Content-Security-Policy meta tag.**
- **No referrer-policy or X-UA-Compatible headers.**
- Loads Google Fonts from external CDN without `preconnect` to `fonts.gstatic.com` only — actually it does have both preconnects, which is correct.
- `script` src is `/src/main.tsx` — Vite handles this during build.

### `public/` (2 files)
- `favicon.svg` — Optimus brand logo SVG (purple gradient design)
- `icons.svg` — SVG sprite sheet containing symbols: `bluesky-icon`, `discord-icon`, `documentation-icon`, `github-icon`, `social-icon`, `x-icon`

**Serving Behavior:**
- In dev: Vite serves `public/` at root automatically.
- In production: `vercel.json` rewrites non-asset paths to `index.html`. `favicon.svg` and `icons.svg` are explicitly excluded from the SPA fallback regex, so they are served as static files from `dist/`.

---

## 5. DOCS vs IMPLEMENTATION GAPS

| Document Claim | Implementation Reality | Severity |
|----------------|------------------------|----------|
| **Database:** MySQL 8.0 + Drizzle ORM | SQLite 3 via `better-sqlite3`. Raw SQL strings. No ORM. | **Critical** |
| **Vector DB:** Qdrant | No Qdrant client, no vector storage, no embedding service | **Critical** |
| **Auth:** Kimi OAuth 2.0 + JWT sessions | No auth implemented. All tRPC procedures are `publicProcedure`. | **Critical** |
| **Payments:** Paddle integration | No Paddle SDK, no payment router, no webhook handler | **High** |
| **Monitoring:** Sentry frontend + backend | No Sentry packages in dependencies, no Sentry init code | **High** |
| **Security:** Rate limiting (100 req/min) | No rate limiter installed or configured | **High** |
| **Security:** CSP, X-Frame-Options, HSTS | No security headers set in Hono app | **High** |
| **CORS:** Whitelist-only | `cors({ origin: "*" })` — completely open | **High** |
| **Backend:** Docker + Docker Compose | No Dockerfile, no docker-compose.yml in repo | **Medium** |
| **Process Manager:** PM2 | No `ecosystem.config.js`, no PM2 usage | **Medium** |
| **Reverse Proxy:** Nginx | No nginx config in repo (only in docs as example) | **Medium** |
| **Build:** `npm run build` builds full app | Only builds frontend (Vite). Server build script exists but is not invoked. | **Medium** |

---

## 6. CROSS-LAYER INTEGRATION ANALYSIS

### 6.1 Frontend tRPC Client → Backend Connection

**Frontend:** `src/providers/trpc.tsx` (42 lines)
```typescript
import { httpBatchLink } from '@trpc/client';
import { createTRPCReact } from '@trpc/react-query';
import type { AppRouter } from '../../api/router';

export const trpc = createTRPCReact<AppRouter>();

export function TRPCProvider({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
  const [queryClient] = useState(() => new QueryClient({
    defaultOptions: { queries: { refetchOnWindowFocus: false, retry: false } }
  }));

  const [trpcClient] = useState(() => trpc.createClient({
    links: [
      httpBatchLink({
        url: '/api/trpc',
      }),
    ],
  }));
  // ...
}
```

**Backend:** `api/trpc.ts` (46 lines)
```typescript
import { initTRPC } from "@trpc/server";
const t = initTRPC.create();
export const router = t.router;
export const publicProcedure = t.procedure;
```

**Backend Entry:** `api/boot.ts` lines 76-85
```typescript
app.use("/api/trpc/*", async (c) => {
  const response = await fetchRequestHandler({
    endpoint: "/api/trpc",
    req: c.req.raw,
    router: appRouter,
    createContext: () => ({}),
  });
  return response;
});
```

**Integration Points:**
- Frontend hits `/api/trpc` via `httpBatchLink`.
- Vite dev proxy (`vite.config.ts` lines 8-12) forwards `/api` to `http://localhost:3000`.
- In production, `vercel.json` rewrites `/api/:path*` to `/api`, which invokes `api/index.ts`.
- `api/index.ts` exports HTTP methods via `handle(app)` from `hono/vercel`.

**Gaps:**
- **No auth context.** `createContext: () => ({})` returns empty object. All procedures are `publicProcedure`.
- **No tRPC error handler.** The `initTRPC.create()` call has no `onError` callback (docs specify Sentry integration here).
- **No request batching limits.** Default batch link can send unlimited requests in one HTTP call.

---

### 6.2 Build Process & Output Analysis

**Development Flow:**
1. `npm run dev:server` → `tsx api/boot.ts` (port 3000)
2. `npm run dev:client` → `vite` (port 5173, proxies `/api` to 3000)

**Production Build Flow (as configured):**
1. `npm run build` → `vite build`
2. Vite outputs to `dist/`:
   - `dist/index.html`
   - `dist/assets/` (hashed JS/CSS files)
   - `dist/favicon.svg`, `dist/icons.svg`

**Server Build (not invoked):**
1. `npm run build:server` → `tsc -p tsconfig.server.json`
2. Would output compiled JS to `dist/api/`, `dist/scripts/`

**Vercel Production Serving:**
- Static files served from `dist/` by Vercel's CDN.
- API routes handled by `api/index.ts` serverless function.
- `api/boot.ts` lines 88-91:
```typescript
if (process.env.NODE_ENV === "production") {
  app.use("/*", serveStatic({ root: "./dist" }));
  app.get("*", serveStatic({ path: "./dist/index.html" }));
}
```
**Issue:** In Vercel, the serverless function and static files are separate. The `serveStatic` middleware in `api/boot.ts` may not work correctly on Vercel because:
1. The function may not have access to `./dist` at runtime.
2. Vercel's static deployment already handles static files before the function is invoked.
3. The `vercel.json` rewrite sends non-asset routes to `index.html` anyway.

**Integration Gap:** The `serveStatic` logic is designed for a VPS/Node server (where `boot.ts` runs as the main HTTP server), but on Vercel it is redundant and potentially broken.

---

### 6.3 Environment Variable Usage

| Variable | Read Where | Required? | Status |
|----------|-----------|-----------|--------|
| `DATABASE_URL` | Nowhere (SQLite used instead) | No | **Dead code in .env.example** |
| `DB_PATH` | `api/db/client.ts:9` | No (falls back to `data/optimus.db`) | Optional, VPS only |
| `QDRANT_URL` | Nowhere | No | **Dead code** |
| `OPENAI_API_KEY` | Nowhere in code | No | **Dead code** |
| `PADDLE_*` | Nowhere | No | **Dead code** |
| `AMAZON_*` | Nowhere | No | **Dead code** |
| `JWT_SECRET` | Nowhere | No | **Dead code** |
| `VITE_KIMI_AUTH_URL` | Nowhere | No | **Dead code** |
| `VITE_APP_ID` | Nowhere | No | **Dead code** |
| `NODE_ENV` | `api/boot.ts:88`, `api/services/pdf.ts:11` | No | Functional |
| `PORT` | `api/boot.ts:93`, `api/services/pdf.ts:8` | No (default 3000) | Functional |
| `APP_URL` | `api/services/pdf.ts:10` | No | Functional |
| `APP_VERSION` | `api/boot.ts:53` | No | Functional |
| `VERCEL` | `api/boot.ts:139`, `api/db/client.ts:13` | No (auto-set by platform) | Functional |
| `PUPPETEER_EXECUTABLE_PATH` | `api/services/pdf.ts:26` | No | Missing from .env.example |
| `TRACKING_WEBHOOK_URL` | `api/services/webhook.ts:18` | No | Missing from .env.example |
| `SENTRY_DSN` | Nowhere | No | **Dead code** |

**Critical Finding:** The `.env.example` file is largely a fantasy document. Most variables listed are not read anywhere in the actual codebase. The only truly functional variables are `NODE_ENV`, `PORT`, `APP_URL`, `APP_VERSION`, `VERCEL`, `DB_PATH`, `PUPPETEER_EXECUTABLE_PATH`, and `TRACKING_WEBHOOK_URL`.

---

### 6.4 Database Deployment: SQLite on Vercel vs Local

**File:** `api/db/client.ts` (205 lines)

**Local/VPS Path:**
```typescript
const bundledDbPath = process.env.DB_PATH
  ? path.resolve(process.env.DB_PATH)
  : path.resolve(__dirname, "../../data/optimus.db");
```

**Vercel /tmp Copy Mechanism (lines 13-32):**
```typescript
const isVercel = !!process.env.VERCEL;

let dbPath: string;

if (isVercel) {
  const tmpDbPath = "/tmp/optimus.db";
  if (!fs.existsSync(tmpDbPath) && fs.existsSync(bundledDbPath)) {
    fs.copyFileSync(bundledDbPath, tmpDbPath);
    console.log(`📋 Copied bundled DB to writable /tmp for Vercel.`);
  }
  dbPath = tmpDbPath;
} else {
  dbPath = bundledDbPath;
}
```

**Line-by-line Behavior:**
1. `isVercel` detected via `process.env.VERCEL`.
2. On cold start, checks if `/tmp/optimus.db` exists.
3. If not, copies the bundled `data/optimus.db` (included via `vercel.json includeFiles`) to `/tmp/optimus.db`.
4. Opens the DB at `/tmp/optimus.db` with `better-sqlite3`.
5. Enables WAL mode and foreign keys.

**Critical Gaps:**
- **Ephemeral writes:** `/tmp` is wiped on every cold start. Any mutations (bookings, view counts, activities) are lost when the function instance recycles. The DB reverts to the bundled state.
- **No write-back mechanism.** Data written to `/tmp` never persists back to the bundled `data/optimus.db`.
- **Concurrency:** SQLite WAL mode requires file-system-level locking. On Vercel's multi-instance serverless environment, concurrent writes from different function instances can corrupt the DB or cause `BUSY` errors.
- **Schema initialization:** `api/db/schema.ts` calls `initSchema()` at module load time (line 172). This runs `CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS` and migrations on every cold start. This is safe but adds latency.

---

### 6.5 Static Asset Serving in Production vs Dev

**Development (`vite.config.ts`):**
```typescript
server: {
  proxy: {
    '/api': {
      target: 'http://localhost:3000',
      changeOrigin: true,
    },
  },
}
```
- Vite dev server proxies `/api` to the Hono backend.
- `public/` files served automatically by Vite at root.

**Production (Vercel):**
- Static files (`dist/`) served by Vercel's edge CDN.
- `vercel.json` rewrite ensures SPA routing:
```json
{
  "source": "/((?!assets/|favicon.svg|icons.svg).*)",
  "destination": "/index.html"
}
```

**Gap in `api/boot.ts` (lines 88-91):**
```typescript
if (process.env.NODE_ENV === "production") {
  app.use("/*", serveStatic({ root: "./dist" }));
  app.get("*", serveStatic({ path: "./dist/index.html" }));
}
```
This `serveStatic` is a **custom implementation** using Node `fs` (lines 17-44). It is:
1. **Redundant on Vercel** (static files are handled by the platform).
2. **Potentially broken on Vercel** because the working directory in a serverless function may not contain `./dist`.
3. **Necessary for VPS deployment** where `boot.ts` is the sole HTTP server.

---

### 6.6 CORS Configuration & Security Headers

**CORS (api/boot.ts line 47):**
```typescript
app.use("*", cors({ origin: "*" }));
```
**Critical Gap:** Wide-open CORS. Docs specify "Whitelist-only" and "CORS: Sadece kendi domain'inden API çağrılarına izin". Implementation allows any origin.

**Security Headers:**
- **None implemented.** The Hono app sets no `X-Frame-Options`, `X-Content-Type-Options`, `Referrer-Policy`, `Content-Security-Policy`, or `Strict-Transport-Security`.
- Docs (`security-authentication.md` lines 321-344) specify exact header values. None are present in code.

**tRPC Error Exposure:**
- `api/trpc.ts` has no `onError` handler. tRPC errors may leak stack traces in production.

---

### 6.7 PDF Generation Flow

**File:** `api/services/pdf.ts` (96 lines)

**Flow:**
```
Frontend requests /api/pdf/:slug
    → Hono route (api/boot.ts:63-74)
    → generatePdf(slug)
    → Puppeteer launches headless Chrome
    → Navigates to APP_URL/p/:slug?print=true
    → Waits for .report-ready selector (8s timeout)
    → Exports A4 PDF
    → Returns Buffer with Content-Disposition: attachment
```

**Exact Logic Lines:**
```typescript
const port = process.env.PORT || "3000";
const appUrl = process.env.APP_URL || 
  (process.env.NODE_ENV === "production" ? `http://127.0.0.1:${port}` : "http://127.0.0.1:5173");
const url = `${appUrl}/p/${slug}?print=true`;
```

**Launch Options (lines 16-23):**
```typescript
const launchOptions: any = {
  headless: true,
  args: [
    "--no-sandbox",
    "--disable-setuid-sandbox",
    "--disable-dev-shm-usage",
  ],
};
```

**Windows Path Hardcode (lines 28-32):**
```typescript
} else if (process.platform === "win32") {
  const defaultWinPath = "C:\\Users\\hp\\.cache\\puppeteer\\chrome-headless-shell\\win64-148.0.7778.97\\chrome-headless-shell-win64\\chrome-headless-shell.exe";
  if (fs.existsSync(defaultWinPath)) {
    launchOptions.executablePath = defaultWinPath;
  }
}
```

**Critical Gaps:**
1. **Self-calling loop risk:** On production VPS, if `APP_URL` points to the same server, Puppeteer loads the page via HTTP through the same Hono app. This consumes an additional HTTP request/thread.
2. **Vercel incompatibility:** Puppeteer requires a Chromium binary (~150MB). Vercel serverless functions have a 50MB limit for the deployment bundle (or 250MB for some plans) and do not support running Puppeteer easily. The `api/index.ts` function would need `puppeteer-core` + `@sparticuz/chromium` for Vercel.
3. **No auth check on PDF endpoint.** Anyone with a slug can generate and download a PDF.
4. **Hardcoded Windows path** includes the developer's local username (`hp`) and a specific Chrome version. This will break on any other Windows machine or when the cached version changes.

---

### 6.8 Webhook Dispatch Flow

**File:** `api/services/webhook.ts` (144 lines)

**Trigger Point:** `api/routers/prospects.ts` lines 134-181 (`recordActivity` mutation)

**Flow:**
```
Frontend calls prospects.recordActivity
    → Logs to prospect_activities table (line 146-149)
    → Fetches prospect details (lines 156-167)
    → Calls triggerWebhook()
    → If TRACKING_WEBHOOK_URL unset: logs to console (mock mode)
    → If Discord URL: formats embed payload
    → If Slack URL: formats Block Kit payload
    → Otherwise: generic JSON payload
    → POSTs to webhookUrl
```

**Exact Code Snippets:**
```typescript
const webhookUrl = process.env.TRACKING_WEBHOOK_URL;
if (!webhookUrl) {
  console.log("---------------- [WEBHOOK MOCK TRIGGER] ----------------");
  // ... mock logging
  return;
}
```

**Payload Construction (lines 62-128):**
- Discord: `embeds` array with title, color, fields.
- Slack: `blocks` array with header, section, divider.
- Default: JSON with `timestamp`, `prospectName`, `eventType`, `interestScore`.

**Dispatch (lines 130-134):**
```typescript
const response = await fetch(webhookUrl, {
  method: "POST",
  headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
  body: JSON.stringify(payload)
});
```

**Gaps:**
1. **No signature verification** on outbound webhooks (not typically required, but no retry logic either).
2. **No queueing.** Webhook dispatch happens synchronously inside the tRPC mutation. If the webhook URL is slow or down, the API request hangs.
3. **`TRACKING_WEBHOOK_URL` is not documented** in `.env.example`.
4. **No circuit breaker** on webhook `fetch`. The `api/services/circuitBreaker.ts` exists but is not used by the webhook service.
5. **Error handling is weak.** Only logs to console; does not surface to caller or retry.

---

## 7. SUMMARY OF CRITICAL INTEGRATION GAPS

| # | Gap | Location | Impact |
|---|-----|----------|--------|
| 1 | `build` script does not build server | `package.json:13` | Server code may not be compiled for production |
| 2 | SQLite on Vercel is ephemeral | `api/db/client.ts:21-32` | All writes lost on cold start |
| 3 | CORS is wide open (`*`) | `api/boot.ts:47` | Security vulnerability |
| 4 | No auth middleware | `api/trpc.ts:5-8` | All data is publicly accessible |
| 5 | No rate limiting | Entire API | Susceptible to abuse |
| 6 | Puppeteer Windows path hardcoded | `api/services/pdf.ts:29` | PDF generation breaks on other machines |
| 7 | Vercel likely cannot run Puppeteer | `api/services/pdf.ts:35` | PDF endpoint will fail in production |
| 8 | `.env.example` is mostly fiction | `.env.example` | Misleading documentation |
| 9 | Docs specify MySQL/Drizzle/Qdrant/Sentry/Paddle | `docs/` | None are implemented |
| 10 | Webhook dispatch is synchronous | `api/routers/prospects.ts:173` | Blocks API on webhook latency |
| 11 | `serveStatic` middleware may break on Vercel | `api/boot.ts:88-91` | Redundant/broken in serverless |
| 12 | No security headers | `api/boot.ts` | Missing XSS/clickjacking protection |
| 13 | QueueWorker starts on non-Vercel | `api/boot.ts:146` | Correct for VPS, but no cron for Vercel |

</details>
